
α.1.1 WEske kutchissik ayum God Kesuk kah Ohke.
E.1.1 In the beginning God created the heaven and the earth.

α.1.2 Kah Ohke mô matta kuhkena[u]unneunkquttinn8 kah mo[n]teaguinninno, kah pohkenum woskeche m8n[ô]i, kah Nashauanit popomshau woskeche nippekon[t]u.
E.1.2 And the earth was without form, and void; and darkness was upon the face of the deep. And the Spirit of God moved upon the face of the waters.

α.1.3 Onk n8wau God wequaiaj, káh mô wequái.
E.1.3 And God said, Let there be light: and there was light.

α.1.4 Kah wunnaumun God wequai ne ne wunnegen: Kah wutchadchaúbe-ponumun God n[ô]eu wequai kah noeu pohk[è]num.
E.1.4 And God saw the light, that it was good: and God divided the light from the darkness.

α.1.5 Kah wutussowétamun God wequai Kesukod, kah pohkenum wutussoweetamun Nukon: kah mô wunnonk88k kah mo mohtompog negonne kesuk.
E.1.5 And God called the light Day, and the darkness he called Night. And the evening and the morning were the first day.

α.1.6 Kah n8wau God sepakehtam8udj nôeu nippekontu, kah chadchapem8udj nashauweit nippe wutch nippekóntu.
E.1.6 And God said, Let there be a firmament in the midst of the waters, and let it divide the waters from the waters.

α.1.7 Kah ayimup God sepakehtamóonk, kah wtuchadchabeponumunnap nashàueu nippe agwu, uttiyeu agwu sepakehtamóonk, kah nashaueu nippekontu uttiyeu ongkouwe sepakehtamóonk, kah mônkô n$nih.
E.1.7 And God made the firmament, and divided the waters which were under the firmament from the waters which were above the firmament: and it was so.

α.1.8 Kah wuttissoweétamun God sèpakehtamóonk Kesukquash, kah mô wunnonk88k, kah mô mohtompog nahohtôeu kesukok.
E.1.8 And God called the firmament Heaven. And the evening and the morning were the second day.

α.1.9 Kah n8wau God moém8idj nippe ut agwu kesukquash kah pasukqunnu, kah pahkemoidj nanabpeu, kah mônkô n$nih.
E.1.9 And God said, Let the waters under the heaven be gathered together unto one place, and let the dry land appear: and it was so.

α.1.10 Kah wuttissoweétam[u]n God nanabpi ohke, kah mô[e]ém8 nippe wuttissowetamun Kehtoh, & wunnaumun God ne en wunnegen.
E.1.10 And God called the dry land Earth; and the gathering together of the waters called he Seas: and God saw that it was good.

α.1.11 Kah n8wau God dtanuékej ohke moskeht, moskeht skannémunú8k skannémun[a]sh, & meechummue magtugquash meechummú8k meechummuonk nish$noh pasuk neane wuttinnussuonk, ubbùhkumminù8k et woskeche ohke, kah mônkò n$nih.
E.1.11 And God said, Let the earth bring forth grass, the herb yielding seed, and the fruit tree yielding fruit after his kind, whose seed is in itself, upon the earth: and it was so.

α.1.12 Kah ohke dtannegenup mosket, kah mosket[u]kannemennù8k skannemunash, nish$noh pasuk neane wuttinnussuonk, kah mahtug, meechummù8k, ubbuhkumminn88k wuhhogkut nish$noh pasuk neane wuttinnussuonk, kah wunnaumun God ne en wunnegen.
E.1.12 And the earth brought forth grass, and herb yielding seed after his kind, and the tree yielding fruit, whose seed was in itself, after his kind: and God saw that it was good.

α.1.13 Kah mo wunnonk88k, kah mo mohtompog shwekesukod.
E.1.13 And the evening and the morning were the third day.

α.1.14 Kah n8wau God, Wequanantéganùohettich ut wussepakehtam8onganit Kesukquash, & pohshehettich ut nashauwe kesukod, kah ut nashauwe nukkonut, kah kukkinneasuonganúhhettich, kah utt8cheye[ù]hettich, kah kesukodtù8wuhhettich, kah kodtumm8[o]wuhhettich.
E.1.14 And God said, Let there be lights in the firmament of the heaven to divide the day from the night; and let them be for signs, and for seasons, and for days, and years:

α.1.15 Kah n$nag wequanantéganuóhettich ut sépakehtam8wonganit wequasumóhettich ohke, onk mô n$nih.
E.1.15 And let them be for lights in the firmament of the heaven to give light upon the earth: and it was so.

α.1.16 Kah ayum God neesunash missiyeuash wequanantéganash, wequananteg mohtag nananum8m8 kesukod, wequananteg peasik nanaum8m8 nukon, kah anogqsog.
E.1.16 And God made two great lights; the greater light to rule the day, and the lesser light to rule the night: he made the stars also.

α.1.17 Kah uppónu[h] God wussepake[h]tam8onganit kesukquash, woh wequohsumwog ohke.
E.1.17 And God set them in the firmament of the heaven to give light upon the earth,

α.1.18 Onk woh wunnananumunneau kesukod kah núkon, kah pohshém8 nashaueu wequai, kah nashaueu pohkénum, kah wunnaumun God ne en wunnegen.
E.1.18 And to rule over the day and over the night, and to divide the light from the darkness: and God saw that it was good.

α.1.19 Kah mô wunnonk88k kah mo mohtompog yaou quinukok.
E.1.19 And the evening and the morning were the fourth day.

α.1.20 Kah n8wau God, m8nahettich nippekóntu pomómutcheg pomantamwae, kah puppinshaúussog pumunahettich ongkouwe ohket woskeche wussépahkehtam8onganit kesukquash.
E.1.20 And God said, Let the waters bring forth abundantly the moving creature that hath life, and fowl that may fly above the earth in the open firmament of heaven.

α.1.21 Kah kezheau God matikkenunutcheh P8tâbpoh, kah nish$noh pomantamòe óâas noh pompâmayit uttiyeug m8nacheg nippekontu, nish$noh pasuk neane wuttinnussuonk, kah nish$noh 8nuppohwhunin puppinshaash, nish$noh pasuk neane wuttinnussuonk, kah wunnaumun God ne en wunnegen.
E.1.21 And God created great whales, and every living creature that moveth, which the waters brought forth abundantly, after their kind, and every winged fowl after his kind: and God saw that it was good.

α.1.22 Kah 8nanumoh nuhhog God n8wau, Mshéneetuónittegk, kah muttaan8k, kah numwapegk nippe ut kehtohhannit, kah puppinshasog muttâanhettich ohket.
E.1.22 And God blessed them, saying, Be fruitful, and multiply, and fill the waters in the seas, and let fowl multiply in the earth.

α.1.23 Kah mo wanonk88k k[à]h mo mohtompog napanna audtahwhikquinukok.
E.1.23 And the evening and the morning were the fifth day.

α.1.24 Kah n8wau God, Pas8waheonch ohke oâas pomantamwaeu, nish$noh pasuk neane wuttinnussin, neetasuog, p[am]ayéch[e]g kah puppimashimwog ohkekontu, nish$noh pasuk neane wuttinnussin kah monko n$nih.
E.1.24 And God said, Let the earth bring forth the living creature after his kind, cattle, and creeping thing, and beast of the earth after his kind: and it was so.

α.1.25 Kah áoúau God puppinn[à]shimwoh ohkekontu neane wuttinnussuongan8, kah neetasu neane wuttin[u]ussuongan8, kah nish$noh paumayit woskeche ohkekontu neane wuttinnussuongan8, kah wunnaumun God ne en wunnegen.
E.1.25 And God made the beast of the earth after his kind, and cattle after their kind, and every thing that creepeth upon the earth after his kind: and God saw that it was good.

α.1.26 Kah n8wau God, ayéuontuh wosketomp neanséog & kutogqunneunkqussuonkanunnónut, kah nanawunonch namóhsog kehtohhannet kah puppinshaussog kesukqut, kah puppinashimwussog, kah wame ohke, kah nish$noh óáas pomompagit woskeche ohket.
E.1.26 And God said, Let us make man in our image, after our likeness: and let them have dominion over the fish of the sea, and over the fowl of the air, and over the cattle, and over all the earth, and over every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth.

α.1.27 Kah kézheau God woskeetompuh ut nehenwonche wuttin[n]ussuonganit, wuttinnussuonganit God wuttinne kezheuh nahoh, wosketomp kah mittamwossis ukkezheuh nahog.
E.1.27 So God created man in his own image, in the image of God created he him; male and female created he them.

α.1.28 Onk 8nanumuh nahog God, k[a]h wutt[i]nuh nahog God, Mshéneetuonitteg, monagk, kah muttaan8gk ohke, kah m8steo8gk, kah nanaaun8k namohsog kehtohhannit kah puppinshaussog mamahchekesukqut, kah wam[e] p[u]ppinashimwussog paumayitcheg et woskeche ohket.
E.1.28 And God blessed them, and God said unto them, Be fruitful, and multiply, and replenish the earth, and subdue it: and have dominion over the fish of the sea, and over the fowl of the air, and over every living thing that moveth upon the earth.

α.1.29 Kah n8wau God, Kusse kittinnum[m]aunumw8 nish$noh mosket skannemunnu8k skannemunash uttiyeu woskeche wame ohket, kah nish$noh matug dtannegkuk meechum úbbuhkumin88k ubbuhkuminash, woh kummeechumw8.
E.1.29 And God said, Behold, I have given you every herb bearing seed, which is upon the face of all the earth, and every tree, in the which is the fruit of a tree yielding seed; to you it shall be for meat.

α.1.30 Onk wame puppinnashimwog ohkekontu, kah wame puppinsha[a]s mamahchekesukqut, kah nish$noh uppumompagen pomantog ohket, woh meechwog nish$noh oshquashqui moskeht, kah mônkô n$nih.
E.1.30 And to every beast of the earth, and to every fowl of the air, and to every thing that creepeth upon the earth, wherein there is life, I have given every green herb for meat: and it was so.

α.1.31 Kah wunnaumun God nish$noh teaug mahche kezteunk, kah kusseh mo ahche wunneg[e]n, kah mo wanonk88k & mo mohtompog nequtta audtashikquinukok.
E.1.31 And God saw every thing that he had made, and, behold, it was very good. And the evening and the morning were the sixth day.

α.2.1 YEU ne kesteounah kesukquash kah ohke, kah wame ne adtahsehettit.
E.2.1 Thus the heavens and the earth were finished, and all the host of them.

α.2.2 Kah nesausuk audtashikquinukok pakodtiteau God wutan[a]kausuonk ne ayik, kah anwôsin nesausuk audtashikquinuk[o]k wutch wame wutanakausuwònganit ne kest[é]unk.
E.2.2 And on the seventh day God ended his work which he had made; and he rested on the seventh day from all his work which he had made.

α.2.3 Kah God on[à]netam nesausuk audtashikquinuk[o]k kah 8t8wóntamun: newutch neit anwosin wutch wame watunakausuwonganit, ne God kesteunkupa kah ayikup.
E.2.3 And God blessed the seventh day, and sanctified it: because that in it he had rested from all his work which God created and made.

α.2.4 Yeush wutontseong[a]sh kesukquash káh ohke, nag kesteomuk: ne kesukok Jehovah Manit kesteunk ohke kah kesukquash.
E.2.4 These are the generations of the heavens and of the earth when they were created, in the day that the LORD God made the earth and the heavens,

α.2.5 Kah nish$noh ohketeámuk ut ohteakonit negonne asquam ahkénug; kah nish$noh mosket ut ohteakonit ásq neekinnin[8] [n]ewutche Jehovah Mani asq sokanonukkontam8g ohke, kah matta mo wosketompáino woh wánteunk ohke.
E.2.5 And every plant of the field before it was in the earth, and every herb of the field before it grew: for the LORD God had not caused it to rain upon the earth, and there was not a man to till the ground.

α.2.6 Qut ouwan waápu wutch ohkekontu kah wutadtipp[a]dto wame woskeche ohkeit.
E.2.6 But there went up a mist from the earth, and watered the whole face of the ground.

α.2.7 Kah Jehovah Manit kenaiheau wosketompuh wutch nunnobúhteaóuut, kah upp8tâmou ut wutchânut pomantam[ó]e nasháuonk, kah wosketomp mo pomantamẃae keteahogkôunnu.
E.2.7 And the LORD God formed man of the dust of the ground, and breathed into his nostrils the breath of life; and man became a living soul.

α.2.8 Kah Jehovah Manit ohkehteau tanohketeaónk ut Eden wutchepwâou: kah ne upponun wosketompuh neh kahkenáiheau[m]poh.
E.2.8 And the LORD God planted a garden eastward in Eden; and there he put the man whom he had formed.

α.2.9 Kah Jehovah Manit wunnéketeauun wutch ohkekontu nish$noh mahtug ne wanompámukquok, kah wunnegen meechinat: kah mahtug pomantamôe ut n[ô]eu adtanohk[e]teámuk, kah mahtug nashpe woh wahteómuk wanegik kah machuk.
E.2.9 And out of the ground made the LORD God to grow every tree that is pleasant to the sight, and good for food; the tree of life also in the midst of the garden, and the tree of knowledge of good and evil.

α.2.10 Kah seip wutchishau Eden wadtattippattunk tanohketeaonk, kah na wutch pohpohchohshau yauóntupai.
E.2.10 And a river went out of Eden to water the garden; and from thence it was parted, and became into four heads.

α.2.11 Neg[o]nogtag hettamun {Pison}, ne quanupishunk wame ohke[i]t Havilah, na ohtag gold.
E.2.11 The name of the first is Pison: that is it which compasseth the whole land of Havilah, where there is gold;

α.2.12 Kah ne ohkit wunnegen, ne ohteau Bdellium kah Onyx qussuk.
E.2.12 And the gold of that land is good: there is bdellium and the onyx stone.

α.2.13 Onk nahohtôe seip ussowétamun {Gihon} ne quanupishunk wame ohke Kush.
E.2.13 And the name of the second river is Gihon: the same is it that compasseth the whole land of Ethiopia.

α.2.14 Nashwinn[u]8k seip hettamun {Hiddekel}, ne aushunk wutchepw[â]ou Assyria, kah ya[u]unnú8k seip Euphrates.
E.2.14 And the name of the third river is Hiddekel: that is it which goeth toward the east of Assyria. And the fourth river is Euphrates.

α.2.15 Onk Jehovah Manit neemunau Adam, kah upponuh tanohketeonganit Eden, 8nteaúunat, kah wunnânauwéhteauunat.
E.2.15 And the LORD God took the man, and put him into the garden of Eden to dress it and to keep it.

α.2.16 Kah Jehovah Manit unnan8nau wosketompuh, n8wau, Nish$noh mahtug yeu tanogketeaonganit, woh meech8an kummeechin.
E.2.16 And the LORD God commanded the man, saying, Of every tree of the garden thou mayest freely eat:

α.2.17 Qut ne mahtug nashpe woh wahteómuk wanégik kah machuk, matta woh kummeech8un, newutche ne kesukok meech8an nupp8e pish kenup.
E.2.17 But of the tree of the knowledge of good and evil, thou shalt not eat of it: for in the day that thou eatest thereof thou shalt surely die.

α.2.18 Onk Jehovah Manit n8wau, Matta wunnegenninno wosketomp wunn[o]ns[i]in, nutayimau aninnohs[ú]aènuh nagum ut anaquabit.
E.2.18 And the LORD God said, It is not good that the man should be alone; I will make him an help meet for him.

α.2.19 Onk wutche ohkekontu Jehovah Manit kenáiheau nish$noh pasuk puppinashimwoh ut ohteakonit, kah [n]ish$noh puppinsháus mamahchekesukqut, kah nag upp[a]udtaóunuh Adam, kodnaum utt[ô]h ahunont, kah Adam uttoh anont nish$noh ôáas uppomautamun, ne wuttissow[é]sin.
E.2.19 And out of the ground the LORD God formed every beast of the field, and every fowl of the air; and brought them unto Adam to see what he would call them: and whatsoever Adam called every living creature, that was the name thereof.

α.2.20 Onk Adam 8weseuonganuhkâou wame netasu, kah puppinsha[u]soh mamahchekesukqut, kah nish$noh puppinashim ut ohteakontu: qut n[ô] matta na [m]éheon anninohs[ú]aénin, woh anumungqutche Adam.
E.2.20 And Adam gave names to all cattle, and to the fowl of the air, and to every beast of the field; but for Adam there was not found an help meet for him.

α.2.21 Onk Jehovah Manit Adamwoh a[n]innumauau kussukkouéonk kah koueu, k[a]h wunneemunúmauuh pasuk wuhpét[e]og, kah wonk yeânunnum we[y]au[s] wonk nompe.
E.2.21 And the LORD God caused a deep sleep to fall upon Adam, and he slept: and he took one of his ribs, and closed up the flesh instead thereof;

α.2.22 Onk ne muhpeteog Jehovah Manit neemunuk wutch wosketompaut, 8tsheun mittumwossissoh, kah uppas8oh wosketompaut.
E.2.22 And the rib, which the LORD God had taken from man, made he a woman, and brought her unto the man.

α.2.23 Onk Adam n8wau, Yeuoh yeuyeu wusk[o]n wutch n8skon, kah wayaus wutch n8weyaus, pish henno[u] Ishah, newutche wuttinau wosketompaut,
E.2.23 And Adam said, This is now bone of my bones, and flesh of my flesh: she shall be called Woman, because she was taken out of Man.

α.2.24 ne wajeh pish wosketomp nukonont 8shoh kah okasoh, kah pish weetomáu ummittumwussoh, kah nag pish pasukquinnú8 weyaus8.
E.2.24 Therefore shall a man leave his father and his mother, and shall cleave unto his wife: and they shall be one flesh.

α.2.25 Onk neeswe posk[is]suog wosketomp kah ummittumwossoh, kah matta akodchuog.
E.2.25 And they were both naked, the man and his wife, and were not ashamed.

α.3.1 WOnk ask8k m8cheke wunnompewussu onk neg wame puppinash[im]wog ohkekonit, neh Jehovah Manit kesheumpo[h], kah unnau mittamwossissoh, Nux, wusunneas God, matta woh kummeech8h nish$noh pasuk mahtug tanohketeaonganit?
E.3.1 Now the serpent was more subtil than any beast of the field which the LORD God had made. And he said unto the woman, Yea, hath God said, Ye shall not eat of every tree of the garden?

α.3.2 Onk mittumwossis unnau ask8koh, woh nummeechumun magtugque ummeechummuongash tanohketeaonganit.
E.3.2 And the woman said unto the serpent, We may eat of the fruit of the trees of the garden:

α.3.3 Qut ne mahtug ummeechummuonk noeu tanohketeaonganit, God unn8wop, matta woh kummeech8uneau, asuh woh mat kummissunnum8unneau ishkont kenupm8.
E.3.3 But of the fruit of the tree which is in the midst of the garden, God hath said, Ye shall not eat of it, neither shall ye touch it, lest ye die.

α.3.4 Onk ask8k unnau muttumwossissoh, Matta woh nupp8e kenupp8.
E.3.4 And the serpent said unto the woman, Ye shall not surely die:

α.3.5 Newutch God 8wahteoun, ne kesukok meechog, neit woh kuskesuk88ash wohweemoash: kah woh kenaau onatuh Manitt8og, wahteo[ú]un wanegik kah machuk.
E.3.5 For God doth know that in the day ye eat thereof, then your eyes shall be opened, and ye shall be as gods, knowing good and evil.

α.3.6 Neit mittumwossis nag* ne in wunnegen mahtug meechinnat, kah wunnegen nah en m[ô]neaumunneat, kah mahtug ukkodtantamunat ne waantamwáhikquit: neemunum ummeechummuonk, kah ummeechin: kah wonk wuttinnumaun wasukeh weeche, onk ummeechinin.
E.3.6 And when the woman saw that the tree was good for food, and that it was pleasant to the eyes, and a tree to be desired to make one wise, she took of the fruit thereof, and did eat, and gave also unto her husband with her; and he did eat.

α.3.7 Onk nag wuskesuk88ash neeswe woshweem8ash, kah wahteauog upposkiss8ongan8: kah momokukquómauwaog wuhhogkáuh figse wunnepogquosh, kah nish wutadtahwh[u]nu[n]ko[ú]onaoash wutch kuhhogkaoh.
E.3.7 And the eyes of them both were opened, and they knew that they were naked; and they sewed fig leaves together, and made themselves aprons.

α.3.8 Onk n8tamwog 8wadtauatongqussúonk Jehovah Manit pamwushadt tahohketeonganit t[oh]kokquok: neit Adam kah ummittumwussoh puttogquéog wutch anaquabit Jehovah Manit, ut kenugké mahtugk8kontu tanohketeaonganit.
E.3.8 And they heard the voice of the LORD God walking in the garden in the cool of the day: and Adam and his wife hid themselves from the presence of the LORD God amongst the trees of the garden.

α.3.9 Onk Jehovah Manit weekomau Adamoh, kah wuttinuh, toh kutapin.
E.3.9 And the LORD God called unto Adam, and said unto him, Where art thou?

α.3.10 Onk n8wa[u] n8tamo[n] k8wadtauatonkqussuonk ut tanohketeaonganit, neit n8wabesip, newutche nupposkis, kah nupputtogquem.
E.3.10 And he said, I heard thy voice in the garden, and I was afraid, because I was naked; and I hid myself.

α.3.11 Onk wuttinuh howan kummishamungqu[s] kupposkissuonk? sun kummeech m[e]htug[qu]e quohtinunump matta kummeech8unat?
E.3.11 And he said, Who told thee that thou wast naked? Hast thou eaten of the tree, whereof I commanded thee that thou shouldest not eat?

α.3.12 Onk wosketomp n8wau, Mittumwossis ne anumaiyean n8weetomunneat nuttin[namuk] m[e]htug, kah nummeechinap.
E.3.12 And the man said, The woman whom thou gavest to be with me, she gave me of the tree, and I did eat.

α.3.13 Onk Jehovah Manit unnau mittumwossissoh teaguas yeu asean? [K]ah mittumwossis n8wau, ask8k nutass8kekomuk, [kah] nummeechinap.
E.3.13 And the LORD God said unto the woman, What is this that thou hast done? And the woman said, The serpent beguiled me, and I did eat.

α.3.14 Onk Jehovah Manit unnau ask8koh, Newutche yeu kummahche usse[n], kutunkquánumug m8cheke onk wame neg neetasuog, kah m8cheke onk nish$noh puppinashim ohteakonit: kenogkis kuppomusho[n]tou, kah puppisi pish kummeech [ti]s[ó]hkepomantam.
E.3.14 And the LORD God said unto the serpent, Because thou hast done this, thou art cursed above all cattle, and above every beast of the field; upon thy belly shalt thou go, and dust shalt thou eat all the days of thy life:

α.3.15 Onk nupponam sekeneaittuonk nashaue ken, kah mittumwossis, kah nashauwe k8skannémunit, kah 8skannémunit: nagum pish sukqui[h]tham kuppuhkuk, kah pish kussukquttahhamau wogquan.
E.3.15 And I will put enmity between thee and the woman, and between thy seed and her seed; it shall bruise thy head, and thou shalt bruise his heel.

α.3.16 Kah mittumwossissoh unnau, m8chekéhteoe numm8chekéhteóh kutonkquommomm8onk, kah k8wompequauonk: onkquommomwe pish keneecha[m]; kah pish kukkodtanum kasuk, kah pish kenanauwunuk.
E.3.16 Unto the woman he said, I will greatly multiply thy sorrow and thy conception; in sorrow thou shalt bring forth children; and thy desire shall be to thy husband, and he shall rule over thee.

α.3.17 Kah Adamwoh unnau, newutche kukk[é]iketam 8wadtauatonkqussuonk kummittumwussis, kah kummeech mahtug uttiyeu quohti[n]unomp, an[o]n, Matta woh meech8un: ohquoantamun ohke wutche ken, onkquommomwe pish kummeechin tisohkepomantaman.
E.3.17 And unto Adam he said, Because thou hast hearkened unto the voice of thy wife, and hast eaten of the tree, of which I commanded thee, saying, Thou shalt not eat of it: cursed is the ground for thy sake; in sorrow shalt thou eat of it all the days of thy life;

α.3.18 Kah asinekôsog, kah kogkôanogkohquohh8w[â]og pish ta[nn]etuog kuhhogkaut: kah pish kummeech mosket ohteakonit.
E.3.18 Thorns also and thistles shall it bring forth to thee; and thou shalt eat the herb of the field;

α.3.19 Kussittanumwe woh kummeech petukqunneg, nô paje quashkean ohkekontu: newutche nawutch k8te[ni]tte[à]nah, newutche nuppuppissiyeu, kah pish kukqushkem en puppissiyeuut.
E.3.19 In the sweat of thy face shalt thou eat bread, till thou return unto the ground; for out of it wast thou taken: for dust thou art, and unto dust shalt thou return.

α.3.20 Onk Adam ussowénau ummittamwussoh Eve, newutche wame okasúoh pomantogig.
E.3.20 And Adam called his wife's name Eve; because she was the mother of all living.

α.3.21 Onk Jehovah Manit wutayimauoh hahk8nei hogk8unash Adam kah ummittumwus, kah wuth[ó]gquoanoh nahog.
E.3.21 Unto Adam also and to his wife did the LORD God make coats of skins, and clothed them.

α.3.22 Onk Jehovah Manit n8wau, Kusseh[.] wosketomp kuttinnungqun, wahteunk wanegik kah machik, kah yeuyeu ishkont summagunuk wunnutcheg, kah neemunuk pomantamoe mahtug, kah woh ummeechin, onk woh micheme pomantam.
E.3.22 And the LORD God said, Behold, the man is become as one of us, to know good and evil: and now, lest he put forth his hand, and take also of the tree of life, and eat, and live for ever:

α.3.23 Newutche Jehovah Manit, Wussohwohk[ô]nuh wutch tanohketeaonganit Eden, onk woh wonteau ohke, ne waj neemun[o]mukup.
E.3.23 Therefore the LORD God sent him forth from the garden of Eden, to till the ground from whence he was taken.

α.3.24 Nemehkuh soh8hkauau wosketompuh, onk upponau Cherubimsog nogqueu wutchepw[à]ou wutch tanohketeaonganit Eden, kah nashqunáeu togkodteg, ne nish$noh aum8, nanea[i]tetunk ummay pomantamóe mahtug.
E.3.24 So he drove out the man; and he placed at the east of the garden of Eden Cherubims, and a flaming sword which turned every way, to keep the way of the tree of life.

α.4.1 ONK Adam waheau Evoh ummittumwussoh, kah w[om]pequôou, kah neek[heau] Kainoh, kah n8wau, Nutattumun woskeetomp wutch Jehovahut.
E.4.1 And Adam knew Eve his wife; and she conceived, and bare Cain, and said, I have gotten a man from the LORD.

α.4.2 Kah wonk neekeau weematoh Abel, kah Abel assamau sheepsoh, kah Kain 8nehteaun ohke.
E.4.2 And she again bare his brother Abel. And Abel was a keeper of sheep, but Cain was a tiller of the ground.

α.4.3 Onk nôad n$n[i]h8p Kain paudto[ou] ummeechummuonk ohke ummagunat en Jehovahut.
E.4.3 And in process of time it came to pass, that Cain brought of the fruit of the ground an offering unto the LORD.

α.4.4 Kah Abel noh wonk pas8au ummohtommegitte8moh wunneetasáut, kah weeis [ne na] ohtag, kah Jehovah tapeneámaau Abel[o]h kah ne ummág8onk.
E.4.4 And Abel, he also brought of the firstlings of his flock and of the fat thereof. And the LORD had respect unto Abel and to his offering:

α.4.5 Qut matta tapeneauóou Kainoh, kah ne ummag8onk, kah Kain m8cheke musquantam, kah músquan[e]unkqussu.
E.4.5 But unto Cain and to his offering he had not respect. And Cain was very wroth, and his countenance fell.

α.4.6 Kah Jehovah unnau Kainoh, Tohwutch musquantaman? kah tohwutch musquaneunkqusséan?
E.4.6 And the LORD said unto Cain, Why art thou wroth? and why is thy countenance fallen?

α.4.7 Wunnesean, woh mo kuttapeneontóh? kah matta wunnesean, matcheseonk seepsin squoantamut: kah pish k8t8ánumuk, onk noh pish kenanawun.
E.4.7 If thou doest well, shalt thou not be accepted? and if thou doest not well, sin lieth at the door. And unto thee shall be his desire, and thou shalt rule over him.

α.4.8 Kah Kain keket8hkauau Abeloh weematoh, onk n$nih, [à]phettit ohteakonit, Kain neepauwéhtauau weematuh Abel, kah wunnushoh.
E.4.8 And Cain talked with Abel his brother: and it came to pass, when they were in the field, that Cain rose up against Abel his brother, and slew him.

α.4.9 Kah Jehovah unnau Kainoh, Uttiyeuoh Abel keemat? kah n8wau matta n8waheóh neen neemat woh n8wadchan?
E.4.9 And the LORD said unto Cain, Where is Abel thy brother? And he said, I know not: Am I my brother's keeper?

α.4.10 Kah n8wau, Toh kutussim? 8wadtauatonkqussuonk keemat 8sqhéonk nummauunnitteunk wutch ohkekontu.
E.4.10 And he said, What hast thou done? the voice of thy brother's blood crieth unto me from the ground.

α.4.11 Onk yeuyeu ken kutôhqua[n]umit wutch ohkekontu noh w[ô]hshinuk wutt8n attumunuk 8sqheonk keemat wutch kenutcheganit
E.4.11 And now art thou cursed from the earth, which hath opened her mouth to receive thy brother's blood from thy hand;

α.4.12 Wunnehteauan ohke yeu wutche onk yean, matta pish kittinn[u]munkou ummissetuonk, pish k8semewaénu, kah kukkogkeompaénu ut ohkeit.
E.4.12 When thou tillest the ground, it shall not henceforth yield unto thee her strength; a fugitive and a vagabond shalt thou be in the earth.

α.4.13 Onk Kain unnau Jehovahnoh, Nussasamatahwhutteaonk missi ánue onk ne woh wodskinum.
E.4.13 And Cain said unto the LORD, My punishment is greater than I can bear.

α.4.14 Kusseh, kussohh8kah yeu kesukok wutch woskeche ohkit, kah wutch kuskesukqut pish nutatt[a]shit, kah pish n8semewaénu kah nukkogkeompaénu ohkeit: onk pish n$nih nish$noh howan námhukqun pish nunnushik.
E.4.14 Behold, thou hast driven me out this day from the face of the earth; and from thy face shall I be hid; and I shall be a fugitive and a vagabond in the earth; and it shall come to pass, that every one that findeth me shall slay me.

α.4.15 Kah Jehovah wuttinuh, Newutche, howan nashont Kainoh, pish an8tauau nesausuk tahshit nompeu: kah Jehovah ponamauau kuhkinneasuonk Kainoh, ishkont naméheahettit, woh wunnushóuh.
E.4.15 And the LORD said unto him, Therefore whosoever slayeth Cain, vengeance shall be taken on him sevenfold. And the LORD set a mark upon Cain, lest any finding him should kill him.

α.4.16 Onk Kain sohham wutch anaquabit Jehovah, kah wutohtu ohkeit Nod wutchepwâou wutch Eden.
E.4.16 And Cain went out from the presence of the LORD, and dwelt in the land of Nod, on the east of Eden.

α.4.17 Onk Kain waheau ummittumwussoh, kah wompoquóou kah neechau Enoch kah ayim otan, kah ussowetam otan ne [á]sow[á]sunit wunnaumonuh Enoch.
E.4.17 And Cain knew his wife; and she conceived, and bare Enoch: and he builded a city, and called the name of the city, after the name of his son, Enoch.

α.4.18 Kah Enoch wunnaumonaeu Iradoh, kah Irad wunnaumónaeu Mahujael, kah Mahujael wunnaumonaeu Methusael, kah Methusael wunnaumonaeu Lamech.
E.4.18 And unto Enoch was born Irad: and Irad begat Mehujael: and Mehujael begat Methusael: and Methusael begat Lamech.

α.4.19 Onk Lamech nes8kau, pasuk ussowesu Adah, onkatuk ussowesu Zillah.
E.4.19 And Lamech took unto him two wives: the name of the one was Adah, and the name of the other Zillah.

α.4.20 Onk Adah nekheau Jabal, noh wut8shin neg wodóhkutcheg weetuómut, kah wunneetas[ú]m8wog.
E.4.20 And Adah bare Jabal: he was the father of such as dwell in tents, and of such as have cattle.

α.4.21 Onk weemat ussowenau Jubal: noh mo wut8shin neg nohtôepequ[a]cheg Harp kah Organ.
E.4.21 And his brother's name was Jubal: he was the father of all such as handle the harp and organ.

α.4.22 Kah Zillah neechau Tubal$kain kuhk8tomuhteaénin noh ayig wompú[h]shog, kah m8[ô]shog: kah ummussesoh Tubal-kain Naamah.
E.4.22 And Zillah, she also bare Tubalcain, an instructer of every artificer in brass and iron: and the sister of Tubalcain was Naamah.

α.4.23 Kah Lamech unnau ummittumwussoh Adah & Zillah, N8tam8k nuttinn8waonk, kenaau mittumwussoh Lamech, kukkéitam8k nukkeket8hkáonk, newutche nunnush wosketomp kodwoskehit, kah wuskenin toh kodnehit.
E.4.23 And Lamech said unto his wives, Adah and Zillah, Hear my voice; ye wives of Lamech, hearken unto my speech: for I have slain a man to my wounding, and a young man to my hurt.

α.4.24 Kain an8tauwut nesausuk tahshe[u] wunnamuhkut Lamech nesausuk tahshinchag tahsheu kah nesausuk.
E.4.24 If Cain shall be avenged sevenfold, truly Lamech seventy and sevenfold.

α.4.25 Kah Adam waheau wonk ummittumwussoh, kah neechau wunnaumonuh, kah wuttissowénuh Sheth, newutche God nuttinnumunk onkatogke wuskannem nompe Abelóut, Kain nohshompoh.
E.4.25 And Adam knew his wife again; and she bare a son, and called his name Seth: For God, said she, hath appointed me another seed instead of Abel, whom Cain slew.

α.4.26 Onk Sheth wunnaumonaeu, kah wuttissowenoh Enos, kah ne wutche kutche wosketompaog wehquetumwog 8wesuonk Jehovah.
E.4.26 And to Seth, to him also there was born a son; and he called his name Enos: then began men to call upon the name of the LORD.

α.5.1 YEu wussukwhongane uppometuongash Adam, ne kesukok God keṣheunt missinninnúh wuttinheuh wutogqunneunkqussinneat Godut.
E.5.1 This is the book of the generations of Adam. In the day that God created man, in the likeness of God made he him;

α.5.2 Wosketomp, kah mittumwossissoh ukkezheuh: kah 8nanumuh kah wuttissowénuh Adam, ne kesukok kezhit.
E.5.2 Male and female created he them; and blessed them, and called their name Adam, in the day when they were created.

α.5.3 Onk Adam nequt pasuk8we kah nishwinchag kodtumwohkog, wunnaumonáeu nehenwonche wutogqunneunkqussuongano, kah neánusit; kah wuttissowenuh Sheth.
E.5.3 And Adam lived an hundred and thirty years, and begat a son in his own likeness, and after his image; and called his name Seth:

α.5.4 Kah ukkesuk8ash Adam, mahche neekit Sheth, shwosuk tahshit pasuk8we kodtum8, kah neit wunnaumonaeu, kah wuttoneu.
E.5.4 And the days of Adam after he had begotten Seth were eight hundred years: and he begat sons and daughters:

α.5.5 Kah wame kesukodtash uppomantamóonk Adam, pasak8gun tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwáe, kah nabo shwinchag, kah ne wuttit nuppin.
E.5.5 And all the days that Adam lived were nine hundred and thirty years: and he died.

α.5.6 Kah Sheth pomantog nequt pasuk8we kodtumwae, kah napanna tahshit kodtummo, neit wunnaumonaeu Enosh.
E.5.6 And Seth lived an hundred and five years, and begat Enos:

α.5.7 Onk Sheth pomantam mahche neekit Enosh, shwosuk tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwáe, kah nesausuk tahshit kodtumwae, kah wunnaumonaeu, kah wuttôneu.
E.5.7 And Seth lived after he begat Enos eight hundred and seven years, and begat sons and daughters:

α.5.8 Onk wame kesukodtash uppomantamóonk Sheth, p[à]sak8gun tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwae, kah nabo neese kodtumwae neit nupp8.
E.5.8 And all the days of Seth were nine hundred and twelve years: and he died.

α.5.9 Onk Enosh pomantog pas[u]k8gun tahs[h]inchage ko[k]tumwae, neit wunnaumónaeu Kainan.
E.5.9 And Enos lived ninety years, and begat Cainan:

α.5.10 Onk Enosh pomantam mahche neekit Kaina[n] shwosuk tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwae, kah nabo napanna tahshit kodtumwae kah wunnaumonaeu kah wuttôneu.
E.5.10 And Enos lived after he begat Cainan eight hundred and fifteen years, and begat sons and daughters:

α.5.11 Onk wame kesukodtash uppomantamóonk Enosh pasuk8gun tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwae, kah napanna tahshit kodtumwae, neit nupp8.
E.5.11 And all the days of Enos were nine hundred and five years: and he died.

α.5.12 Onk Kainan pomantog nesausuk tahshinchage kodtumwae, neit wunnaumonaeu Mahalaleel.
E.5.12 And Cainan lived seventy years and begat Mahalaleel:

α.5.13 Onk Kainan pomantam mahche neekit Mahalaleel, shwosuk tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwae, kah yauonchage kodtumwae, kah wunnaumónaeu kah wuttôneu.
E.5.13 And Cainan lived after he begat Mahalaleel eight hundred and forty years, and begat sons and daughters:

α.5.14 Onk wame kesukodtash uppomantam[ò]onk Kainan pasak8gun tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwae, kah piukque kodtumwae, neit [u]upp8.
E.5.14 And all the days of Cainan were nine hundred and ten years: and he died.

α.5.15 Onk Mahalaleel pomantog nequtta tahshinchage kodtumwae kah napanna tahshit kodtumwae, kah wunnaumonaeu Jared.
E.5.15 And Mahalaleel lived sixty and five years, and begat Jared:

α.5.16 Onk Mahelaleel pomantam mahche neekit Jared, shwosuk tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwae, kah nishwinchage kodtumwae, kah wunnaumónaeu kah wuttôneu.
E.5.16 And Mahalaleel lived after he begat Jared eight hundred and thirty years, and begat sons and daughters:

α.5.17 Onk wame kesukodtash uppomantamóonk Mahalaleel shwosuk tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwae, kah pasak8gun tahshinchage kah napanna tahshit kodtumwae, neit nupp8.
E.5.17 And all the days of Mahalaleel were eight hundred ninety and five years: and he died.

α.5.18 Jared pomantog nequt pasuk8we kodtumwae, kah nequtta tahshinchage kah neese kodtumwae, neit wunnaumónaeu Enoch.
E.5.18 And Jared lived an hundred sixty and two years, and he begat Enoch:

α.5.19 Onk Jared pomantam mahche neekit Enoch shwosuk tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwae, kah wunnaumónaeu kah wuttôneu.
E.5.19 And Jared lived after he begat Enoch eight hundred years, and begat sons and daughters:

α.5.20 Onk wame kesukodtash uppomantamóonk Jared pasuk8gun tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwae nequtta tahshinchage kah neese kodtumwae, neit nupp8.
E.5.20 And all the days of Jared were nine hundred sixty and two years: and he died.

α.5.21 Onk Enoch pomantog nequtta tahshinchage kah napanna tahshit kodtumwae, neit wunnaumónaeu Methuselah.
E.5.21 And Enoch lived sixty and five years, and begat Methuselah:

α.5.22 Onk Enoch weeche pomushau God, mahche neekit Methuselah, nishwudt pasuk8we kodtumwae, kah wunnaumónaeu, kah wuttôneu.
E.5.22 And Enoch walked with God after he begat Methuselah three hundred years, and begat sons and daughters:

α.5.23 Kah wame kes[u]kodtash uppomantamóonk Enoch nishwudt pasuk8we kodtumwae, nequtta tahshinchage, kah napanna tahshit kodtumwae.
E.5.23 And all the days of Enoch were three hundred sixty and five years:

α.5.24 Kah Enoch weeche pomushaumau God: kah matta na wutápéin newutche God wunnemunoh.
E.5.24 And Enoch walked with God: and he was not; for God took him.

α.5.25 Kah Methuselah pomantog nequt pasuk8we kodtumwae, k[a]h shwosuk tahshinchage, kah nesausuk tahshit kodtumwae neit wunnaumonaeu Lamech.
E.5.25 And Methuselah lived an hundred eighty and seven years, and begat Lamech.

α.5.26 Ka[k] Methuselah pomantam mahche neekit Lamech nesausuk tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwae, shwosuk tahshinchag, kah neese kodtumwae, kah wunnaumónaeu, kah wuttôneu.
E.5.26 And Methuselah lived after he begat Lamech seven hundred eighty and two years, and begat sons and daughters:

α.5.27 Kah wame kesukodtash uppomantamóonk Methuselah pasak8gun tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwae, kah nequtta tahshinchag kah pasak8gun tahshit kodtumwae, neit nupp8.
E.5.27 And all the days of Methuselah were nine hundred sixty and nine years: and he died.

α.5.28 Onk Lamech pamantog nequt pasuk8we kodtumwae: shwosuk tahshinchag, kah neeswe kodtumwae, neit wunnaumónieu.
E.5.28 And Lamech lived an hundred eighty and two years, and begat a son:

α.5.29 Onk wuttissowenuh Noah, an8wadt, Yeuoh pish kittinne kuttaphukqun ne[á]unag kutanakausuonganun, kah wussáuanúm8ongan8 kenutcheganónog, newutche ne ohke Jehovah ohquánittóg-kup.
E.5.29 And he called his name Noah, saying, This same shall comfort us concerning our work and toil of our hands, because of the ground which the LORD hath cursed.

α.5.30 Onk Lamech pomantam mahche neekit Noah, napanna tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwae, pasak8gun tahshinchag, kah napanna tahshit kodtumwae, kah wunnaumónaeu, kah wuttôneu.
E.5.30 And Lamech lived after he begat Noah five hundred ninety and five years, and begat sons and daughters:

α.5.31 Kah wame kesukodtash uppomantamóonk Lamech, nesausuk tahshit pasuk8we, nesausuk tahshinchag, kah nesausuk tahshit kodtumwae, neit nupp8.
E.5.31 And all the days of Lamech were seven hundred seventy and seven years: and he died.

α.5.32 Kah Noah napanna tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwohkog, neit Noah wunnaumonaeu Shem, Ham, kah Japhet.
E.5.32 And Noah was five hundred years old: and Noah begat Shem, Ham, and Japheth.

α.6.1 ONK n$nih wosketompaog n8che monahettit ut woskeche ohkit, kah wutt[ô]nuog.
E.6.1 And it came to pass, when men began to multiply on the face of the earth, and daughters were born unto them,

α.6.2 Wunnaumonuh God nauáog wuttônuh wosketompaog wanétuog, kah 8weetáómóuh neh wame pepenahetticheh.
E.6.2 That the sons of God saw the daughters of men that they were fair; and they took them wives of all which they chose.

α.6.3 Onk Jehovah n8wau, Nunnashauanitt8m matta pish nagwutteáeu achú8hkôóog missinninnuh, newutche noh webe wonk weyausú8: qut ôhch ukkesukkodtumash pish nequt pasuk8we kah neesneechag kodtumwae.
E.6.3 And the LORD said, My spirit shall not always strive with man, for that he also is flesh: yet his days shall be an hundred and twenty years.

α.6.4 Na mô mágoskeetompóou ut ohkeit, onk yeuyeu: onk ompetak wunnaumon[u]h God weetoamáhettit wosketompaog wuttôn8oh onk neekeahettit neg masugkénuppanneg, n8adt ussowesupanneg, waeenómitcheg.
E.6.4 There were giants in the earth in those days; and also after that, when the sons of God came in unto the daughters of men, and they bare children to them, the same became mighty men which were of old, men of renown.

α.6.5 Onk Jehovah wunnaumun ummatcheseonk wosketomp missi ut ohkit, kah nish$noh missantam8e wuttenantamóonk, ut wuttahut, webe matchet ásekésukokish.
E.6.5 And God saw that the wickedness of man was great in the earth, and that every imagination of the thoughts of his heart was only evil continually.

α.6.6 Onk Jehovah aiuskoi[á]ntam ukkezheônuh wosketompuh ut ohket, kah neuantámup ut wuttahuh.
E.6.6 And it repented the LORD that he had made man on the earth, and it grieved him at his heart.

α.6.7 Kah Jehovah n8wop pish nuppagu[a]nóog missinninnúog, neg kezheagkuppanneg, wutch woskeche ohket: missinnin kah puppinashim, kah pohpomompakecheg, kah puppinshasog mamáchekesukqut, newutche nutaiuskoiantam nukkezheauaoh.
E.6.7 And the LORD said, I will destroy man whom I have created from the face of the earth; both man, and beast, and the creeping thing, and the fowls of the air; for it repenteth me that I have made them.

α.6.8 Qut Noah naméheau kitteamonteánittúonk anaquabit Jehovah.
E.6.8 But Noah found grace in the eyes of the LORD.

α.6.9 Yeush uppometuongash Noah: Noah sampweusseaen, kah pannuppu wunneetou ut uppometuonganit, Noah weeche pomushaumau God.
E.6.9 These are the generations of Noah: Noah was a just man and perfect in his generations, and Noah walked with God.

α.6.10 Kah Noah shwinnaumonáeu Shem, Ham, kah Japhet.
E.6.10 And Noah begat three sons, Shem, Ham, and Japheth.

α.6.11 Kah ohke anit ut anaquabit God: kah ohke numwohteau woskehuwaonk.
E.6.11 The earth also was corrupt before God, and the earth was filled with violence.

α.6.12 Kah God moneau ohke, kah kusseh anit newutche wame weyaus anisteou ummay ut ohkit.
E.6.12 And God looked upon the earth, and, behold, it was corrupt; for all flesh had corrupted his way upon the earth.

α.6.13 Kah God unnau Noahoh, 8wóhkukquóssu[ni]n wame weyaus peyaum8 anaquabeh, newutche ohke numwohteau woskenittuonk nashpe nagoh: kah kusseh, pish nuppaguanoog wutch ohkekontu.
E.6.13 And God said unto Noah, The end of all flesh is come before me; for the earth is filled with violence through them; and, behold, I will destroy them with the earth.

α.6.14 Ayimau kuhhog Ark, wutch Gopher mahtugquash woh kutayim âhâguiyeuash ut Arkut: kah pish kuppittukontamun wutch anomut, kah woskeche pittu.
E.6.14 Make thee an ark of gopher wood; rooms shalt thou make in the ark, and shalt pitch it within and without with pitch.

α.6.15 Onk yeu pish kuttinteauun: nissáhteag Ark pish nishwudt pasuk8we ishquonogkodt, kah neanóhkekiskag napannatashinchag ishquonogkodt, kah ne an8hquesp8ogkog shwinchag ishquonogkodt.
E.6.15 And this is the fashion which thou shalt make it of: The length of the ark shall be three hundred cubits, the breadth of it fifty cubits, and the height of it thirty cubits.

α.6.16 Pish kutayim kenogkonég in Arkut, kah ut nequt ishquonogkodt en woh[-] kummasuwayeu pish kukkesteoun: kah wusquoant ut Arkut pish uhquáe kupponamun, negonohtag ohg8nog, nahoht[ô]ohtah, kah nashwunná8g pish kutayim.
E.6.16 A window shalt thou make to the ark, and in a cubit shalt thou finish it above; and the door of the ark shalt thou set in the side thereof; with lower, second, and third stories shalt thou make it.

α.6.17 Kah kusseh neen, kusseh neen nuppaudtoh tomogkon ut ohket pagwatauunat wame weyaus, neg pomantamwe n[à]hnahshoncheg wutch agwe kesukqut: kah nish$noh teaug ne ohtag ohket pish nupp8.
E.6.17 And, behold, I, even I, do bring a flood of waters upon the earth, to destroy all flesh, wherein is the breath of life, from under heaven; and every thing that is in the earth shall die.

α.6.18 Qut ken kummenuhkehteoush n8n8waonk: kah pish kuppetutteaum ut Arkut, ken, kah kenaumonog, kah kummittumwos, kah kenaumonog ummittumwussúoh weeche ken.
E.6.18 But with thee will I establish my covenant; and thou shalt come into the ark, thou, and thy sons, and thy wife, and thy sons' wives with thee.

α.6.19 Kah nish$noh ôaas uppomantamu[n] wame weyaus, nish$noh neesuog woh kuppas8oog ut Arkut, onk woh kenanaiheoog uppomantamunnaoont weeche ken: pish nompaiyeu8, ka[b] squaiyeú8.
E.6.19 And of every living thing of all flesh, two of every sort shalt thou bring into the ark, to keep them alive with thee; they shall be male and female.

α.6.20 Puppinshasog neanussehettit, neetasuog neanussehettit, nish$noh pomompakit ut ohkekontu, neanusséhettit, nish$noh neesuog pish kuppeyauquok, kenanaihéóog, onk woh pomantamwog.
E.6.20 Of fowls after their kind, and of cattle after their kind, of every creeping thing of the earth after his kind, two of every sort shall come unto thee, to keep them alive.

α.6.21 Kah neemunush ken wame ne woh meechimuk, kah pish kummukkinn[ú]mun, kah pish meetsuonganú8 wutche ken kah noghog.
E.6.21 And take thou unto thee of all food that is eaten, and thou shalt gather it to thee; and it shall be for food for thee, and for them.

α.6.22 Kah ne wutussen Noah ne wame God anun8nomp, ne wutussen.
E.6.22 Thus did Noah; according to all that God commanded him, so did he.

α.7.1 ONK Jehovah unnau Noahoh peyaush ken, kah wame n[e]adtahshineog, en Arkut, newutche kenaush sampwesseaen ut anaquabeh, yeu pometuonkanit.
E.7.1 And the LORD said unto Noah, Come thou and all thy house into the ark; for thee have I seen righteous before me in this generation.

α.7.2 Nish$noh uppahkesin puppinashim pish keneemun nehnesausuk tahsheu, nompashim kah squashim: kah nish$noh matta uppakesein puppinashim, nehnees88og, nompashim kah squashim.
E.7.2 Of every clean beast thou shalt take to thee by sevens, the male and his female: and of beasts that are not clean by two, the male and his female.

α.7.3 Netatup puppinshasog mamachekesukqut, nesausuk [h]ettasú8og, nomp[u]hshas kah squashas, onk woh pomantam8m8 8skannemunnu et woskeche ohohket.
E.7.3 Of fowls also of the air by sevens, the male and the female; to keep seed alive upon the face of all the earth.

α.7.4 Newutche mahche nesausuk tahshikquinukok, sokanonteam ut ohkeit yauonchagkodtash kesukodtash kah yauonchagodtash nukonash: kah nish$noh oaas kezteagkup, nuppaguanoog wutch woskeche ohkeit.
E.7.4 For yet seven days, and I will cause it to rain upon the earth forty days and forty nights; and every living substance that I have made will I destroy from off the face of the earth.

α.7.5 Kah Noah wutussen wame ne anunn8nont God.
E.7.5 And Noah did according unto all that the LORD commanded him.

α.7.6 Kah Noah nequtta tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwohkom, tomogkog yeuut ohkit.
E.7.6 And Noah was six hundred years old when the flood of waters was upon the earth.

α.7.7 Kah Noah petutteau, kah wunnaumonuh, kah ummittumwussoh, kah wunnaumonuh ummittumwuss[u]oh weeche, en Arkut, newutche nuppe tomogkon.
E.7.7 And Noah went in, and his sons, and his wife, and his sons' wives with him, into the ark, because of the waters of the flood.

α.7.8 Uppahkesin puppinashim, kah matta uppahkesein puppinashim, puppinshaog, kah nish$noh oaas pomompagit woskeche ohkeit.
E.7.8 Of clean beasts, and of beasts that are not clean, and of fowls, and of every thing that creepeth upon the earth,

α.7.9 Neh neese petutteaog Noahut en arkut, nompaas kah squaas, neanunn8nop Noahoh God.
E.7.9 There went in two and two unto Noah into the ark, the male and the female, as God had commanded Noah.

α.7.10 Onk n$nih mahche nesausuk audtahshikquinukok neit nippe tomogkon ut woskeche [o]hket.
E.7.10 And it came to pass after seven days, that the waters of the flood were upon the earth.

α.7.11 Nequtta tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwáe, pomantog Noah, nahoht[ô]eu nep[á]uz, nabo nesausuk audtahshikquinohhog kes8sh, ne kesukok, tohkékomuash qu[o]gkononogkodtash pohquodchuwánash, kah tomogkonne squoantama[s]h kesukqut póhquaém8uk.
E.7.11 In the six hundredth year of Noah's life, in the second month, the seventeenth day of the month, the same day were all the fountains of the great deep broken up, and the windows of heaven were opened.

α.7.12 Kah sokanonup ohkeit, yauonchagkodtash kesukodtash kah yauonchagkodtash nukonash.
E.7.12 And the rain was upon the earth forty days and forty nights.

α.7.13 Ne kesukok Noah, Shem, kah Ham, kah Japhet, wunnaumonuh Noah, kah ummittumwossoh Noah, kah nishuoh ummittumwussoh wunnaumonuh weeche petutteaog en Arkut.
E.7.13 In the selfsame day entered Noah, and Shem, and Ham, and Japheth, the sons of Noah, and Noah's wife, and the three wives of his sons with them, into the ark;

α.7.14 Nag kah nish$noh wuttinnussin puppinashim, wame neetasuog wuttinussinneau, kah nish$noh pomomp[a]kecheg ut woskeche ohket neanussit, kah nish$nho puppinshas neanussit, kah nish$noh psuksesog wuttónequnnóneau.
E.7.14 They, and every beast after his kind, and all the cattle after their kind, and every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth after his kind, and every fowl after his kind, every bird of every sort.

α.7.15 Kah petukanóog Noahoh en Arkut, nehnees[u]og, kah ne[hn]ee[su]og, wame weyaus neg keteae nehnohsh[an]cheg.
E.7.15 And they went in unto Noah into the ark, two and two of all flesh, wherein is the breath of life.

α.7.16 Kah neg petutteacheg, petutteau nompaus, kah squaus, wame weyaus, nean[un]8nomp God: kah Jehovah ukkuppuhwhoh.
E.7.16 And they that went in, went in male and female of all flesh, as God had commanded him: and the LORD shut him in.

α.7.17 Onk tomogkon yau[o]nchatikqunnu ut woskeche ohket, nippe nano missi, onk tahs[h]eem8 Ark, kah waapem8 wutch ohkeit.
E.7.17 And the flood was forty days upon the earth; and the waters increased, and bare up the ark, and it was lift up above the earth.

α.7.18 Kah nippe moskehtek88, kah nano missi ut woskeche ohket: kah Ark pomushaum8 woskeche nippekontu.
E.7.18 And the waters prevailed, and were increased greatly upon the earth; and the ark went upon the face of the waters.

α.7.19 Kah nippe nano m8nôi mocheke ut woskeche ohket: kah wame kogsuhkôagish ut agwu wame kesukqut nehtippaash.
E.7.19 And the waters prevailed exceedingly upon the earth; and all the high hills, that were under the whole heaven, were covered.

α.7.20 Nabo napanna tashishquonogkot en w[o]hkúmeiye[u] naweequotteau nippe, kah wadchuash natippaash.
E.7.20 Fifteen cubits upward did the waters prevail; and the mountains were covered.

α.7.21 Kah wame weyaus nupp8m8, neg mamonche[c]heg ut woskeche ohkeit: puppinshaog, kah neetasuog, kah puppinashimwog, kah nish$noh pomompakecheg pomompakeog ut woskeche ohket, kah nish$noh wosketomp
E.7.21 And all flesh died that moved upon the earth, both of fowl, and of cattle, and of beast, and of every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth, and every man:

α.7.22 Nish$noh oaas wutch nohnohshon wutch[á]nit wutch pomantamoonk, wame nobohteaoúut, nupp8og.
E.7.22 All in whose nostrils was the breath of life, of all that was in the dry land, died.

α.7.23 Kah nish$noh pasuk oaas pamontog paguanoog, ut woskeche ohket, missinninnuog, kah neetasuog, kah pomompakecheg, kah puppinshasog mamahchekesukqut, kah paguanoog wutch ohkekontu: kah webe Noah na wutchippomantam, kah neg weechayeumoncheg ut Ark.
E.7.23 And every living substance was destroyed which was upon the face of the ground, both man, and cattle, and the creeping things, and the fowl of the heaven; and they were destroyed from the earth: and Noah only remained alive, and they that were with him in the ark.

α.7.24 Neit nuppe nohkúhkom ohke nequt pasuk8e quinne, kah napanna tahshinchag.
E.7.24 And the waters prevailed upon the earth an hundred and fifty days.

α.8.1 ONK God mehquanuma[u] Noahoh, kah nish$noh oass uppomantamun, kah wame neetasuog ne weechayéumukúhpuh ut Ark: kah God pamwusheaheau wabanoh ohket, kah qut[òm]8 nippe.
E.8.1 And God remembered Noah, and every living thing, and all the cattle that was with him in the ark: and God made a wind to pass over the earth, and the waters asswaged;

α.8.2 Kah tohkekomuash mônaiyéuut, kah kenogg[e]neganash kesukqui8k kuppuhh[à]suash, kah sokanon wutch kesukquiug mat sokemun8.
E.8.2 The fountains also of the deep and the windows of heaven were stopped, and the rain from heaven was restrained;

α.8.3 Kah nippe qushkem8 wutch ohkekontu nagwutteau: kah mahchem8ug nequt pasuk88 kah napanna tahshinchagkodtash kesukodtash, neit s[o]hkaém8ug nippe.
E.8.3 And the waters returned from off the earth continually: and after the end of the hundred and fifty days the waters were abated.

α.8.4 Kah Ark musséshin nesausuk audtahsúit nepáuz, nabo nesausuk aúdtahshikquiñahog nepâuz, wadchuash ut Ararat.
E.8.4 And the ark rested in the seventh month, on the seventeenth day of the month, upon the mountains of Ararat.

α.8.5 Kah nippeash nagwutteaeu qushkem8ash noh p[a]jeh piogqussúit nepâuz, piogqussuit nepáuz, neg[o]nne kesukok, neit wanáshquodti[am]ugish n[o]gquodtash.
E.8.5 And the waters decreased continually until the tenth month: in the tenth month, on the first day of the month, were the tops of the mountains seen.

α.8.6 Onk n$nih mahche yaunnéhcheadtequinokok Noah wohshinnum kenogkaneg ut Arkut, ne kezteunkup.
E.8.6 And it came to pass at the end of forty days, that Noah opened the window of the ark which he had made:

α.8.7 Kah an8nau kehchikonkontu, noh papomshad nó pajeh nippe nanohtag wutch ohkekontu.
E.8.7 And he sent forth a raven, which went forth to and fro, until the waters were dried up from off the earth.

α.8.8 Wonk an8nau wuskuhwhunnánoh wutch wuhhogkat, wunnaumunat nanábohteái en woskeche ohkekontu.
E.8.8 Also he sent forth a dove from him, to see if the waters were abated from off the face of the ground;

α.8.9 Qut wuskuhwhunnan mat namehteóou t[o]h woh ohtag wusseet, kah wonk ukqushketunkquoh ut Arkut: newutche nuppe ohteau woskeche wame ohkeit: neit summagunum wunnutcheg kah wunneemunoh, onk uppóṣheuh Arkut.
E.8.9 But the dove found no rest for the sole of her foot, and she returned unto him into the ark, for the waters were on the face of the whole earth: then he put forth his hand, and took her, and pulled her in unto him into the ark.

α.8.10 Kah pahto wonk nesausuk tahshikquinokod, neit wonk an8nau wuskuhwhunnánoh wutch Arkut.
E.8.10 And he stayed yet other seven days; and again he sent forth the dove out of the ark;

α.8.11 Kah wuskuhwhunnau uppéyaaunoh wanonk88k, kah kusseh kenadtam wunnépogque Olive, ne pashkodtog: nemehkuh Noah 8wahteoun sehteaémo nippe wutch ohkekontu.
E.8.11 And the dove came in to him in the evening; and, lo, in her mouth was an olive leaf pluckt off: so Noah knew that the waters were abated from off the earth.

α.8.12 Onk pahto wonk nesausuk tahshikquinukod, kah an8nau wuskuhwhunnanoh kah matta wonk ukqus[h]keaunuk8oh.
E.8.12 And he stayed yet other seven days; and sent forth the dove; which returned not again unto him any more.

α.8.13 Onk n$nih nequtta tahshit pasuk8we, kah na negonne kodtum88k negonne nepâuz, negonne kesukok, nippe nunnohtèau wutch ohkekontu: kah Noah nohhunnúnnum onkwhôsik Ark, kah natawómpu, kah kusseh, wosketohke nunnóhteau.
E.8.13 And it came to pass in the six hundredth and first year, in the first month, the first day of the month, the waters were dried up from off the earth: and Noah removed the covering of the ark, and looked, and, behold, the face of the ground was dry.

α.8.14 Onk nahohtôeu nep[â]uz, neesnechag nabo nesausuk audtahshikquináhhog nepáuz, neit nunnabohteái.
E.8.14 And in the second month, on the seven and twentieth day of the month, was the earth dried.

α.8.15 Kah God ken8nau Noahoh, n8wau.
E.8.15 And God spake unto Noah, saying,

α.8.16 Sohhash wutch Arkut, ken, kah kummittumwos, kenaumonog kah kenaumonog ummittumwussúoh weeche ken.
E.8.16 Go forth of the ark, thou, and thy wife, and thy sons, and thy sons' wives with thee.

α.8.17 Sohh8wush nish$noh oaas uppomantamun weechappémukquéaneg, wame weyaus, puppinshaog, puppinashimwussog, nish$noh pohpomompakécheg pomompakeog ohkekontu, onk woh neech[ú]og m8cheke ut ohkekontu.
E.8.17 Bring forth with thee every living thing that is with thee, of all flesh, both of fowl, and of cattle, and of every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth; that they may breed abundantly in the earth, and be fruitful, and multiply upon the earth.

α.8.18 Onk Noah sohham, kah wunnaumonuh, ummittumwossoh, kah wunnaumonuh ummittumwossúoh weeche nagum.
E.8.18 And Noah went forth, and his sons, and his wife, and his sons' wives with him:

α.8.19 Nish$noh puppinashim, nish$noh pohpomompakit nish$noh puppinshaas, nishnoh oaas uppomompagin ut ohkekontu ne anussehettit, sohhamwog wutch Arkut.
E.8.19 Every beast, every creeping thing, and every fowl, and whatsoever creepeth upon the earth, after their kinds, went forth out of the ark.

α.8.20 Kah Noah kesteauau Altaroh ut Jehovah, kah neemunau nish$noh pahke puppinashim, kah nish$noh pahke puppinshaas, kah wusséphamau chikohtáe sephausuongash ut Altar.
E.8.20 And Noah builded an altar unto the LORD; and took of every clean beast, and of every clean fowl, and offered burnt offerings on the altar.

α.8.21 Kah Jehovah 8weetemontamun, kah Jehovah n8wau ut wuttahut, matta wonk pish nummatchtoôuun ohke newutche wosketompaog, newutche wuttenantam8onk wosketomp wuttahut matchet wutch wuskenuunn[e]at kah matta nuttagkomoh nish$noh oaas uppomantamun, ne mahche usse[a]n.
E.8.21 And the LORD smelled a sweet savour; and the LORD said in his heart, I will not again curse the ground any more for man's sake; for the imagination of man's heart is evil from his youth; neither will I again smite any more every thing living, as I have done.

α.8.22 Nishohekohkék8k, ohkekonat, kah kepenumunát, tohkoi, kah ku[ssi]tteah, nepun kah popòn, kesukod kah nuhkon matta pish ahquohtan8.
E.8.22 While the earth remaineth, seedtime and harvest, and cold and heat, and summer and winter, and day and night shall not cease.

α.9.1 ONK God wun[n]ánumau N[ò]ahoh, kah wunnaumonoh, kah wuttinuh nahog, Mishummeechumegk, kah muttaan8gk, kah numwapegk ohke.
E.9.1 And God blessed Noah and his sons, and said unto them, Be fruitful, and multiply, and replenish the earth.

α.9.2 Kah k8wabesu[ò]nukk8óog, kah kukquishikouoog, nish$noh puppinashim ohket, kah nish$noh puppinshaas mamahchekesukqut, kah wame neg mamonchecheg ut ohkekontu, kah wame namohsog kehtahhannet, kittinumaununk ut kenutchegan8wout wame
E.9.2 And the fear of you and the dread of you shall be upon every beast of the earth, and upon every fowl of the air, upon all that moveth upon the earth, and upon all the fishes of the sea; into your hand are they delivered.

α.9.3 Nish$noh uppomompágin noh pomantog, noh pish k8meechumunneau, onatuh ahchippog, wame kittinnumauunash.
E.9.3 Every moving thing that liveth shall be meat for you; even as the green herb have I given you all things.

α.9.4 Qut weyaus keteaum8ug wusequeheunkanú8g, matta woh kummeech8uneau
E.9.4 But flesh with the life thereof, which is the blood thereof, shall ye not eat.

α.9.5 Kah wunnamuhkut 8squeheunk kuppomantam8ongan8 pish n8chitteamon: pish n8chitteamon ut nish$noh puppinashim, kah nish$noh wosketomp: kah nish$noh howan weematoh pish n8chumon ukketeaonk wosketomp.
E.9.5 And surely your blood of your lives will I require; at the hand of every beast will I require it, and at the hand of man; at the hand of every man's brother will I require the life of man.

α.9.6 Howan se[o]hhog 8sqheonk wosketomp 8skqheonk pish seohhamun nashpe wosketomp: newutche wutogq[u]nneungqunuonganit God kezheau wosketompuh.
E.9.6 Whoso sheddeth man's blood, by man shall his blood be shed: for in the image of God made he man.

α.9.7 Kah kenaau mishummeechumegk, kah muttaan8gk kah neechântam8k m8cheke keit, kah na$ut mutaân8gk.
E.9.7 And you, be ye fruitful, and multiply; bring forth abundantly in the earth, and multiply therein.

α.9.8 Kah God ken8nau Noahoh, kah wunn[á]umonuh weeche, n8wau.
E.9.8 And God spake unto Noah, and to his sons with him, saying,

α.9.9 Kah neen, kusseh, neen kummenuhkehteauonumw8 n8n8waonk, kah k8skannemunneog nahohtôeu ken.
E.9.9 And I, behold, I establish my covenant with you, and with your seed after you;

α.9.10 Kah nish$noh uppomantamun oaas weechauyeumukquean, puppinshas, neetasuog, kah nish$noh puppinashim yeu ohket wéechauyeumukquean: wutche yeug waguppanneg wutche Arkut, onk neit wame puppinashimwog ohkeit.
E.9.10 And with every living creature that is with you, of the fowl, of the cattle, and of every beast of the earth with you; from all that go out of the ark, to every beast of the earth.

α.9.11 Kah kummenuhketeaúonúmw8 n8n8waonk, kah matta pish wonk wame weyaus paguanoon nashpe nippe togmogkon kah matta wonk tomogkonnuun8, onk matcheteauunat ohke.
E.9.11 And I will establish my covenant with you, neither shall all flesh be cut off any more by the waters of a flood; neither shall there any more be a flood to destroy the earth.

α.9.12 Kah God n8wau, yeu ukkukkinueasuonk k8n8waongan ne ayim nashauwee neen kah kenaau, kah nish$noh oaas uppomantamuh weechauyeumukquean wutche wame pometeongash.
E.9.12 And God said, This is the token of the covenant which I make between me and you and every living creature that is with you, for perpetual generations:

α.9.13 Nuppon nutáhtomp matokqsut, onk noh kukkineasuonganu8 wutche k8n8waonganun nashauwe neen kah ohke.
E.9.13 I do set my bow in the cloud, and it shall be for a token of a covenant between me and the earth.

α.9.14 Onk pish n$nih, matohkséhteaon matokqs yeu ohket, ahtomp pish nógqussu ut matokqsit.
E.9.14 And it shall come to pass, when I bring a cloud over the earth, that the bow shall be seen in the cloud:

α.9.15 Neit pish nummehquoantam k8n8waongan8 nashauwe neen kah kenaau, kah nish$noh oaas uppomantamun, wame weyaus: kah matta pish wonk nippe tomogkoninno, paguatoun wame weyaus.
E.9.15 And I will remember my covenant, which is between me and you and every living creature of all flesh; and the waters shall no more become a flood to destroy all flesh.

α.9.16 Kah ahtomp pish appu matokqsut, onk pish nummônneau onk woh nummehquoantam maché nohtag n8n8waonk, nashauwe [et] God kah nish$noh owaas uppomantaman, wame weyaus ohket.
E.9.16 And the bow shall be in the cloud; and I will look upon it, that I may remember the everlasting covenant between God and every living creature of all flesh that is upon the earth.

α.9.17 Kah God unnau Noahoh yeu kukkinneasuonk wutche 8n8waonk ne manuhkehteaun nanshauwe ut neen, kah wame weyaus ohket:
E.9.17 And God said unto Noah, This is the token of the covenant, which I have established between me and all flesh that is upon the earth.

α.9.18 Kah wunnaumonuh Noah waguppanneg Arkut, Shem, Ham, kah Japhet. Ham wut8shin ut Canaan.
E.9.18 And the sons of Noah, that went forth of the ark, were Shem, and Ham, and Japheth: and Ham is the father of Canaan.

α.9.19 Yeush shwewunnaumonuh Noah: kah nashpe naghog wame ohke [n]onkuhkausu.
E.9.19 These are the three sons of Noah: and of them was the whole earth overspread.

α.9.20 Kah Noah kitche ohkehteaenu8, kah ohkeateau weenominneohteuk.
E.9.20 And Noah began to be an husbandman, and he planted a vineyard:

α.9.21 Onk wuttattam ne wine, kah kogkéussippamo[u], kah poskinau ut weetuomut.
E.9.21 And he drank of the wine, and was drunken; and he was uncovered within his tent.

α.9.22 Kah Ham wut8shun Kainan naum upposkisuonk 8shoh, kah wuttinnon neswe weematoh ut poquadchit.
E.9.22 And Ham, the father of Canaan, saw the nakedness of his father, and told his two brethren without.

α.9.23 Neit Shem kah Japhet neemunum hogk8onk, kah upponamauon aehtaueu wuttugket, onk quinkáeog, kah puttaghumwog upposkisuonk 8shuoh: kah wuskesuk88ush ompamohtaash, kah matta naum8og 8shuoh uppóskissuonk.
E.9.23 And Shem and Japheth took a garment, and laid it upon both their shoulders, and went backward, and covered the nakedness of their father; and their faces were backward, and they saw not their father's nakedness.

α.9.24 Kah Noah t8keu wutch 8wineumut kah wahteau peississinutche wunnaumonuh neánhikq[ut].
E.9.24 And Noah awoke from his wine, and knew what his younger son had done unto him.

α.9.25 Na[h] n8wau Kanaan ohquanumunach 8tinninneumuneuh wutti[n]númo[h] weematoh.
E.9.25 And he said, Cursed be Canaan; a servant of servants shall he be unto his brethren.

α.9.26 Onk n8wau, 8nanumunach Jehovah ummanitt8moh Shem, kah Kainan pish 8tinninnumuneoh.
E.9.26 And he said, Blessed be the LORD God of Shem; and Canaan shall be his servant.

α.9.27 Manit pish nupwishunau Japhet, onk pish aye[ú]h wuttayeuonganit Shem, kah Kainan pish 8tinninnumunneoh.
E.9.27 God shall enlarge Japheth, and he shall dwell in the tents of Shem; and Canaan shall be his servant.

α.9.28 Onk Noah pomantam mahche tomogkog nishwudt pasuk8e kodtumwae, kah napanna tahshinchag.
E.9.28 And Noah lived after the flood three hundred and fifty years.

α.9.29 Onk wame ukkesukodtumash Noah pasak8gun tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwae kah napanna tahshinchag kodtumwae, neit nupp8,
E.9.29 And all the days of Noah were nine hundred and fifty years: and he died.

α.10.1 YEU pometuongan8 wunnaumonuh Noah, Shem, Ham kah Japhet, onk wunnaumonauh neetuoh mahche tomogkog
E.10.1 Now these are the generations of the sons of Noah, Shem, Ham, and Japheth: and unto them were sons born after the flood.

α.10.2 Wunnaumonuh J[á]phet, Gomer, kah Magog, kah Madai, kah Javan, kah Tubal, kah Meshek, kah Tiras.
E.10.2 The sons of Japheth; Gomer, and Magog, and Madai, and Javan, and Tubal, and Meshech, and Tiras.

α.10.3 Onk wunnaumonuh Gomer, Ashkenaz, kah Riphath, kah Tog[à]rma.
E.10.3 And the sons of Gomer; Ashkenaz, and Riphath, and Togarmah.

α.10.4 Onk wunnaumonuh Javan, Eisha, kah Tarshish, Kittim, kah Dodanim.
E.10.4 And the sons of Javan; Elishah, and Tarshish, Kittim, and Dodanim.

α.10.5 Nashpe nag chadchabenaog ummu[h]hanôm8wóash Gentiles ut wutohtuw[ó]ut, nishnoh howan neaunag wuttinnont8waonk nish$noh neaunag wutteashshinunneongan8 wutohtuout.
E.10.5 By these were the isles of the Gentiles divided in their lands; every one after his tongue, after their families, in their nations.

α.10.6 Onk wunnaumonuh Ham, Kush, kah Mizraim kah Phut Kanaa[n].
E.10.6 And the sons of Ham; Cush, and Mizraim, and Phut, and Canaan.

α.10.7 Kah wunnaumonuh Kush, Seba kah Havilah, kah Sabtah, kah Raamah, kah Sabtekah: kah wunnaumonuh Raamah, Sheba kah D[e]dan.
E.10.7 And the sons of Cush; Seba, and Havilah, and Sabtah, and Raamah, and Sabtechah: and the sons of Raamah; Sheba, and Dedan.

α.10.8 Onk Kush wunnaumonaeu Nimrod: noh n8che missugkenuk ut ohket.
E.10.8 And Cush begat Nimrod: he began to be a mighty one in the earth.

α.10.9 Missugken audchaen ut anaquabit Jehovah, newutche n8waog netatup Nimrod masugkenuk a[u]dch[a]én anaquabit Jehovah.
E.10.9 He was a mighty hunter before the LORD: wherefore it is said, Even as Nimrod the mighty hunter before the LORD.

α.10.10 Onk newaje kutchissik wuttahs8tamóonk Babel, kah Erech, kah Akkad, kah Kalne ut ohket Shinar.
E.10.10 And the beginning of his kingdom was Babel, and Erech, and Accad, and Calneh, in the land of Shinar.

α.10.11 Ashur sohham ne wutch ohket, kah tannikheteau Niniveh, kah keihtotan Rehoboth kah Kalah.
E.10.11 Out of that land went forth Asshur, and builded Nineveh, and the city Rehoboth, and Calah,

α.10.12 Onk [R]esen nashauwe Niniveh & Kalah yeu missi kei[h]totan.
E.10.12 And Resen between Nineveh and Calah: the same is a great city.

α.10.13 Onk Mizraim wunnaumonaeu Lúdim, kah Anamim, kah Lehabim, & Naphtuhim,
E.10.13 And Mizraim begat Ludim, and Anamim, and Lehabim, and Naphtuhim,

α.10.14 Onk Pathrusim, kah Ka[sl]uhim (newag 8sóhhamun Philistim) kah Kaphtorim.
E.10.14 And Pathrusim, and Casluhim, (out of whom came Philistim,) and Caphtorim.

α.10.15 Onk Kanaan wunnaumonieu Sidon umméhtammetúmoh, kah Heth.
E.10.15 And Canaan begat Sidon his first born, and Heth,

α.10.16 Onk Jebusitog kah Emoritog, kah Girgasitog.
E.10.16 And the Jebusite, and the Amorite, and the Girgasite,

α.10.17 Onk Hivitog, kah Arkitog, & Sinitog.
E.10.17 And the Hivite, and the Arkite, and the Sinite,

α.10.18 Onk Arvaditog, kah Zema[r]itog[,] kah Hamathitog: kah ompetake n[e]adtahshinnehettit Kananitog nanwiyeuog.
E.10.18 And the Arvadite, and the Zemarite, and the Hamathite: and afterward were the families of the Canaanites spread abroad.

α.10.19 Onk ukkuhkonnegon8h Kananitog wutch Sidon peyauan Gerar. Onk yean Gaza aóan Sodom kah Gomorah, Admah & Zeboim missaúmu[sh]au Lashah.
E.10.19 And the border of the Canaanites was from Sidon, as thou comest to Gerar, unto Gaza; as thou goest, unto Sodom, and Gomorrah, and Admah, and Zeboim, even unto Lasha.

α.10.20 Yeuh wunnaumonuh Ham, neadtahshinnehettit, ne unnont8wàhettit wutohtuóut, kah wutohtimoeuwout.
E.10.20 These are the sons of Ham, after their families, after their tongues, in their countries, and in their nations.

α.10.21 Onk na en Shemut 8shuoh wame wunnaumonuh Eber, weematoh Japhet mohtomméginit, wuttit neekinneau.
E.10.21 Unto Shem also, the father of all the children of Eber, the brother of Japheth the elder, even to him were children born.

α.10.22 Wunneechanoh Shem Elam & Ashur kah Arph[a]x[a]d, kah Lud, kah Aram.
E.10.22 The children of Shem; Elam, and Asshur, and Arphaxad, and Lud, and Aram.

α.10.23 Kah wunneechanoh Aram, U[r], kah Hul, kah Gether, kah Mash.
E.10.23 And the children of Aram; Uz, and Hul, and Gether, and Mash.

α.10.24 Onk [A]rphaxad wunnaumonaeu Salah, kah Salah wunnaumonaeu Eber.
E.10.24 And Arphaxad begat Salah; and Salah begat Eber.

α.10.25 Onk neesweekheau Eber, pasuk ussowésu Peleg, newutche noh pomontog ohke cha[c]hauben[à]usu: kah weematoh ussowesu Joktan.
E.10.25 And unto Eber were born two sons: the name of one was Peleg; for in his days was the earth divided; and his brother's name was Joktan.

α.10.26 Onk Joktan wunnaumonaeu Alm[o]dad kah Shele[s]h, kah Hazermaveth, kah Jerah.
E.10.26 And Joktan begat Almodad, and Sheleph, and Hazarmaveth, and Jerah,

α.10.27 Kah Hadoram, kah Uzal, & Diklah.
E.10.27 And Hadoram, and Uzal, and Diklah,

α.10.28 Kah Ob[a]l, kah Abimael, kah Sheba
E.10.28 And Obal, and Abimael, and Sheba,

α.10.29 Kah Ophir[,] kah Havilah, kah Jobab wame yeush wunnaumonoh Joktan.
E.10.29 And Ophir, and Havilah, and Jobab: all these were the sons of Joktan.

α.10.30 Kah neh wado[h]kehettit wutch Mesh[u]a nogqueu Shephar, wadchu wutchepwaou.
E.10.30 And their dwelling was from Mesha, as thou goest unto Sephar a mount of the east.

α.10.31 Yeuh wunnaumonuh Shem, nish$noh wutteatea[h]sheauyéuunneau, ne unnont8wahettit, wutohtu[o]ut, wutohtim[ó]euwóut.
E.10.31 These are the sons of Shem, after their families, after their tongues, in their lands, after their nations.

α.10.32 Yeuh wutteahteáhshaiyeuongan8 wunnaumonu[h] Noah, neaunag uppometuongân8 wutohtuout: kah nashpe yeug chachaubenúmun wutohtimoneash ohket, mahche tomogkog.
E.10.32 These are the families of the sons of Noah, after their generations, in their nations: and by these were the nations divided in the earth after the flood.

α.11.1 KAH wame ohke pasuk unnont8wáonk, kah pasuk hett8wonk.
E.11.1 And the whole earth was of one language, and of one speech.

α.11.2 Kah n$nih wámohettit chepwoáau, namehteaúog mukkoshqut wutohket Shinar, kah ne wutohkinne[u].
E.11.2 And it came to pass, as they journeyed from the east, that they found a plain in the land of Shinar; and they dwelt there.

α.11.3 Kah hettúog, hah, ayeuontuh man8nskog, kah pannuppu chikoswóntu: kah ahtoog man8nskoh wutch qussukquan, kah slime wutch saupae man8n[s]k.
E.11.3 And they said one to another, Go to, let us make brick, and burn them thoroughly. And they had brick for stone, and slime had they for morter.

α.11.4 Kah n8waog, hah ayimontuh keihtotan kah qunnukque kommuk, na woh masukom8mu8k kesuk: kah ayimontuh wesuonk ishkont kussiswaómun yeu ut wame ohkit.
E.11.4 And they said, Go to, let us build us a city and a tower, whose top may reach unto heaven; and let us make us a name, lest we be scattered abroad upon the face of the whole earth.

α.11.5 Kah Jehovah n8keu n8che naum keitotan kah qunnunkqui komuk. uttiyeu wosketomp wunnaumon[û]oh ayimmohettit.
E.11.5 And the LORD came down to see the city and the tower, which the children of men builded.

α.11.6 Kah Jehovah n8wau, kusseh missinninnúog pasuk88og, kah wame pasuk unnontt8waonk: kah yeu n8che ussenaous, kah yeuyeu matta woh wuttamhéoog ne ahcheweséhettit.
E.11.6 And the LORD said, Behold, the people is one, and they have all one language; and this they begin to do: and now nothing will be restrained from them, which they have imagined to do.

α.11.7 Hah n8kétuh pen8wehteúttuh unnont8waonk, onk woh mo wohtauuttéog.
E.11.7 Go to, let us go down, and there confound their language, that they may not understand one another's speech.

α.11.8 Nemehkuh Jehovah chachaubenuh na wutch ut woskeche wame ohket, onk wutahquete [uu]nneau ayimun keitotan.
E.11.8 So the LORD scattered them abroad from thence upon the face of all the earth: and they left off to build the city.

α.11.9 Newaje ussowetamuk Babel, newutche Jehovah na wuttitayimun papén8want8waonk wame ohket: kah na wutche Jehovah wunnanwiéhheun et woskeche wame ohket.
E.11.9 Therefore is the name of it called Babel; because the LORD did there confound the language of all the earth: and from thence did the LORD scatter them abroad upon the face of all the earth.

α.11.10 Yeush wutontseongash Shem, Shem nequt pasuk8we kodtumwohkog wunnaumonaeu Arphaxad neese k[o]dtumwae mahche tomogkog.
E.11.10 These are the generations of Shem: Shem was an hundred years old, and begat Arphaxad two years after the flood:

α.11.11 Kah Shem mahche wunnaumonâeu Arph[a]xad[u]h, napanna tahshit pasuk8we kodtumwohkomup: neit wunnaumonaeu kah wuttoneu.
E.11.11 And Shem lived after he begat Arphaxad five hundred years, and begat sons and daughters.

α.11.12 Kah Arphaxad pamontog shwinchage nabo napanna kodtumwae, neit wunnaumonaeu Salahhoh.
E.11.12 And Arphaxad lived five and thirty years, and begat Salah:

α.11.13 Kah Arphaxad mahche wunnaumonait Salahhoh, yauut pasuk8we kodtumwohkomup, kah nishwe kodtummo, neit wunnaumonau kah wuttôneu.
E.11.13 And Arphaxad lived after he begat Salah four hundred and three years, and begat sons and daughters.

α.11.14 Kah Salah pamontog shwinchage kodtumwae, neit wunnaumonaeu Eberoh.
E.11.14 And Salah lived thirty years, and begat Eber:

α.11.15 Kah Salah mahche wunnaumonait Eberoh, yauut pasuk8we kodtumwohkomup kah nishwe, neit wunnaumonaeu & wuttoneu
E.11.15 And Salah lived after he begat Eber four hundred and three years, and begat sons and daughters.

α.11.16 Kah Eber pam[on]tog shwin[c]hag nabo yau kodtumwae, neit wunnaumonaeu Pelegoh
E.11.16 And Eber lived four and thirty years, and begat Peleg:

α.11.17 Kah Eber mahche wunnaumonait Pelegoh, yauut pasuk8we kodtumwohkomup kah nabo shwinchage, neit wunnaumonaeu kah wuttôneu.
E.11.17 And Eber lived after he begat Peleg four hundred and thirty years, and begat sons and daughters.

α.11.18 Kah Peleg pomontog shwinchage kodtumwae neit wunnaumonaeu R[e]u[ho]h.
E.11.18 And Peleg lived thirty years, and begat Reu:

α.11.19 Kah Peleg mahche wunnaumonait Reuhoh, neese pasuk8we kodtumwohkomup, kah pasak8gun, neit wunnaumonaeu kah wuttôneu.
E.11.19 And Peleg lived after he begat Reu two hundred and nine years, and begat sons and daughters.

α.11.20 Kah Reu pamontog shwinchage kodtumwae kah nees, neit wunnaumonaeu Serugoh.
E.11.20 And Reu lived two and thirty years, and begat Serug:

α.11.21 Kah Reu mahche wunnaumonait Serugoh, neese pasuk8we kodtumwohkomup, kah nesausuk, neit wunnaumonaeu kah wuttôneu.
E.11.21 And Reu lived after he begat Serug two hundred and seven years, and begat sons and daughters.

α.11.22 Kah Serug pamontog shwinchage kodtumwáe, neit wunnaumonaeu Nahoroh.
E.11.22 And Serug lived thirty years, and begat Nahor:

α.11.23 Kah Serug mahche wunnaumonait Nahoroh, neese pasuk8we kodtúmwohkomup, neit wunnaumonaeu kah wuttôneu.
E.11.23 And Serug lived after he begat Nahor two hundred years, and begat sons and daughters.

α.11.24 Kah Nahor pamontog neesneechage kodtumwae nabo pask8gun neit wunnaumonaeu Terahoh.
E.11.24 And Nahor lived nine and twenty years, and begat Terah:

α.11.25 Kah Nahor mahche wunnaumonait Terahoh nequt pasuk8we kodtumwohkomup kah nabo pask8gun, neit wunnaumonaeu & wuttôneu.
E.11.25 And Nahor lived after he begat Terah an hundred and nineteen years, and begat sons and daughters.

α.11.26 Kah Terah pamontog nesausuk tahshinchage kodtumwae, neit wunnaumonaeu Abrahamwoh, Nahoroh, Haranoh.
E.11.26 And Terah lived seventy years, and begat Abram, Nahor, and Haran.

α.11.27 Kah yeush wutontseongash Terah, Terah wunnaumonaeu Abramoh, Nahoroh kah Haranoh, kah Haran wunnaumonaeu Lotuh,
E.11.27 Now these are the generations of Terah: Terah begat Abram, Nahor, and Haran; and Haran begat Lot.

α.11.28 Kah Haran nupup anaquabit 8shoh Terahoh, na ohke ut ne[e]teup, ut Ur ut Kaldes.
E.11.28 And Haran died before his father Terah in the land of his nativity, in Ur of the Chaldees.

α.11.29 Neit Abraham kah Nahor 8mittumwussissinneaoh: Abram [um]mittumwussoh ussowesu Sarai: kah Nahor ummittumwussoh ussowesu Milchah, wuttaunoh Haran, 8shoh milchah, 8shoh Ischah.
E.11.29 And Abram and Nahor took them wives: the name of Abram's wife was Sarai; and the name of Nahor's wife, Milcah, the daughter of Haran, the father of Milcah, and the father of Iscah.

α.11.30 Qut Sarai mehchéeu wanne wunneechaneu.
E.11.30 But Sarai was barren; she had no child.

α.11.31 Kah Terah neemunont Abramoh wunnaumonuh, kah Lot wunnaumonuh Haran, wunnaumonuh onk wunnaumonuh, kah Sarai ápenúache, wunnaumonuh Abram ummittumwussoh: kah weeche sohham8m8uh wutche Ur en Kaldes, onk woh auog ohke Kanaan kah paahettit Haran na wuttaiiñeau
E.11.31 And Terah took Abram his son, and Lot the son of Haran his son's son, and Sarai his daughter in law, his son Abram's wife; and they went forth with them from Ur of the Chaldees, to go into the land of Canaan; and they came unto Haran, and dwelt there.

α.11.32 Kah ukkesukodtumash Terah neese pasuk8we kodtumwáe, kah napanna, neit Terah nupp8 ut Haran.
E.11.32 And the days of Terah were two hundred and five years: and Terah died in Haran.

α.12.1 ONK Jehovah unnop Abramoh, sohhash ken wutch kutohket kah wutch kuttinonkumont, kah wutch k8sh weekit, en ohkeit ne woh kenahtinúnum.
E.12.1 Now the LORD had said unto Abram, Get thee out of thy country, and from thy kindred, and from thy father's house, unto a land that I will shew thee:

α.12.2 Kah kutayimoush missi wutôhtimóin, kah k8nánumush kah kummishteoush k8wésuonk, kah pish k8naneteaònit.
E.12.2 And I will make of thee a great nation, and I will bless thee, and make thy name great; and thou shalt be a blessing:

α.12.3 Kah pish n8nanumóog neg wanánumukquéaneg: kah pish nutohqu[a]num noh ohquanumukquean, kah ut kuhhogka[u] wame wutt8wadtuongash ohket pish wunnanumoog.
E.12.3 And I will bless them that bless thee, and curse him that curseth thee: and in thee shall all families of the earth be blessed.

α.12.4 Neit Abram sohham ne anont Jehovah, kah Lot 8weechauoh kah Abram nesausuk tahshinchage kodtumwohkum kah nabo napanna sohhag en Haran.
E.12.4 So Abram departed, as the LORD had spoken unto him; and Lot went with him: and Abram was seventy and five years old when he departed out of Haran.

α.12.5 Kah Abram neemunau Saraihoh ummittumwussoh, kah Lot weematoh wunnaumonuh, kah wame neadtahshekhettit nish magkunnumohettiche, kah neh keteahogk[o]unoh w[o]dtinó[n]che Har[a]n, kah sohhamwog, onk au[o]g ohke Kanaan, onk peyauog ohkeit Kanaan.
E.12.5 And Abram took Sarai his wife, and Lot his brother's son, and all their substance that they had gathered, and the souls that they had gotten in Haran; and they went forth to go into the land of Canaan; and into the land of Canaan they came.

α.12.6 Kah Abram uppanupwushón ohke, en ohket Sichem, ut pag[ô]ntimmúsasqut Moreh: kah Kanánitog neit ne ohkeit.
E.12.6 And Abram passed through the land unto the place of Sichem, unto the plain of Moreh. And the Canaanite was then in the land.

α.12.7 Neit Jehovah naéitau Abramoh, kah n8wau, k8skannemunn[e]og nuttinnumauónean yeu ohke: kah na wuttit ayimun Altar en Jehovah$ut, uttiyeuwoh naéitauwop.
E.12.7 And the LORD appeared unto Abram, and said, Unto thy seed will I give this land: and there builded he an altar unto the LORD, who appeared unto him.

α.12.8 Kah ne 8ch ontsinnun, en wadchuat wutchepwoóntuwae Bethel, kah ne pnamun week, Bethel wutchéksuau, kah Hai wutchepwóou, kah na$ut ayim Altar en Jehovahnit, kah weehquetum 8wesuonk Jehovah.
E.12.8 And he removed from thence unto a mountain on the east of Bethel, and pitched his tent, having Bethel on the west, and Hai on the east: and there he builded an altar unto the LORD, and called upon the name of the LORD.

α.12.9 Kah Abram nayaiyaiom en Sowanaiyeu
E.12.9 And Abram journeyed, going on still toward the south.

α.12.10 Kah na mahshagquodt ut ohket, kah Abram w8msu en Egipt, naw uttaiin, newutche mahshagquod wussaume ne ut ohkeit
E.12.10 And there was a famine in the land: and Abram went down into Egypt to sojourn there; for the famine was grievous in the land.

α.12.11 Kah n$nih paónt kishke Egipt, unna[u] Saraioh ummittumwussoh, kusseh yeuyeu k8wahush k8neet kummóneónte[á]nit.
E.12.11 And it came to pass, when he was come near to enter into Egypt, that he said unto Sarai his wife, Behold now, I know that thou art a fair woman to look upon:

α.12.12 Newutche pish n$nih Egiptiansog nogquean, n8waog yeuh ummittumwussoh kah woh nunushhukquog, qut kuketeáhukquog
E.12.12 Therefore it shall come to pass, when the Egyptians shall see thee, that they shall say, This is his wife: and they will kill me, but they will save thee alive.

α.12.13 K8wehquetumoush n8wash, neetompas, onk woh n8ni wutche ken: kah nukketeahogkou woh pomantam wutche ken.
E.12.13 Say, I pray thee, thou art my sister: that it may be well with me for thy sake; and my soul shall live because of thee.

α.12.14 Kah n$niyeup Abram paont Egipt, Egiptianog wunnau[ô]uh mittumwussis nikkóme wunneetu.
E.12.14 And it came to pass, that, when Abram was come into Egypt, the Egyptians beheld the woman that she was very fair.
