α.12.15 Kah Wusontimósumoh Pharoh wunnauouh, kah woweenomóuh ut Pharaoh$ut: kah mittumwussis neemunop en Pharaoh wéekit.
E.12.15 The princes also of Pharaoh saw her, and commended her before Pharaoh: and the woman was taken into Pharaoh's house.

α.12.16 Kah wunadchanau Abramoh newutche nagum: kah wuttússhepsumeu, k[â]h wutoxenumeu, kah ukquohquohquánetauogkómeu nomposhimuk, kah wuttinnímu wosketompuh kah mittumwossissoh kah ukquóhquohquonetaúogkomeu usquoshimwo[h] kah Camelsoh.
E.12.16 And he entreated Abram well for her sake: and he had sheep, and oxen, and he asses, and menservants, and maidservants, and she asses, and camels.

α.12.17 Onk Jehovah onkquommómheuh Pharaoh, kah neh weekit, nashpe mishe onkquommom8ongash, newutche Sarai Abram ummittumwussoh.
E.12.17 And the LORD plagued Pharaoh and his house with great plagues because of Sarai Abram's wife.

α.12.18 Neit Pharaoh weekomau Abramoh, & wuttinuh, toh kittinh[e]h? tohwutch mat usséas yeuoh nummittumwus? 
E.12.18 And Pharaoh called Abram and said, What is this that thou hast done unto me? why didst thou not tell me that she was thy wife?

α.12.19 tohwutch n8waan ne[e]tompas ye[u]oh? ne n8che woh nukkod ummittumwussin, newutche yeuyeu kusseh, kummittumwus, nee[m]un kah monchish.
E.12.19 Why saidst thou, She is my sister? so I might have taken her to me to wife: now therefore behold thy wife, take her, and go thy way.

α.12.20 Onk Pharaoh unnau wuttinnúmoh wéoggeheahteóg; kah mon[c]heàheuh nagum, kah ummittumwussoh kah neadtahshekhettit.
E.12.20 And Pharaoh commanded his men concerning him: and they sent him away, and his wife, and all that he had.

α.13.1 NEIT Abram ogquodchuog wutch Egypt, nagum & ummittumwussoh, kah wame ne ahdtahshekit, kah Lot weeche, en Sowanayeu.
E.13.1 And Abram went up out of Egypt, he, and his wife, and all that he had, and Lot with him, into the south.

α.13.2 Onk Abram ahche weenauweeteup puppinashimwoh, Silver kah Gold.
E.13.2 And Abram was very rich in cattle, in silver, and in gold.

α.13.3 Onk neyaiyaiomp wutch Sowanayeu wehque Bethel, ne ohkeit weske wádt8tap nashauwe Bethel, kah nashauwe Hai.
E.13.3 And he went on his journeys from the south even to Bethel, unto the place where his tent had been at the beginning, between Bethel and Hai;

α.13.4 Ne adt áyikup Altar, ne ad negonne ayikup: kah [m]a ut Abram wehquetum 8wesuonk Jehovah.
E.13.4 Unto the place of the altar, which he had make there at the first: and there Abram called on the name of the LORD.

α.13.5 Lot wonk weechaúont Abramoh, papeississitcheg kah matukenukeg neetasuog wunóhteau, kah weekuwóash.
E.13.5 And Lot also, which went with Abram, had flocks, and herds, and tents.

α.13.6 Onk ohke mat tápenum8p wamunon náhoh, noh wuttin weechayeuwuttiñeaóont newutche wuttinneetuongan8 missi, & woh mat weechayeuwuttéog.
E.13.6 And the land was not able to bear them, that they might dwell together: for their substance was great, so that they could not dwell together.

α.13.7 Onk penuánittuonk nashauwe ohtop w[u]tassammuáenumoh wunnetasumoh Abram kah nashauwe wutassammuáenumoh wunneetasumoh Lot, kah Kananitog kah Perisitog neit ne 8tohkinneau.
E.13.7 And there was a strife between the herdmen of Abram's cattle and the herdmen of Lot's cattle: and the Canaanite and the Perizzite dwelled then in the land.

α.13.8 Onk Abram wuttinuh Lotuh, k8weequetumoush ahque penuanittuonk ohtaj nashauwe neen kah ken, kah nashauwe nutassamuaenumog k[á]h kutassammuaénumog, newutche k8weematittimun.
E.13.8 And Abram said unto Lot, Let there be no strife, I pray thee, between me and thee, and between my herdmen and thy herdmen; for we be brethren.

α.13.9 Sun mo wame ohkeno anaquabean? k8weequetumoush chipin kuhhog wutch neen, menadtuhteashean nen nuttinohteasheam, asuh aninnuhteashean nen nummenadteasheam.
E.13.9 Is not the whole land before thee? separate thyself, I pray thee, from me: if thou wilt take the left hand, then I will go to the right; or if thou depart to the right hand, then I will go to the left.

α.13.10 Neit Lot spadtawompu, kah moneam wame mukoshqut Jordan, nippe monat nish$noh$ut, asquam Jehovah paguato8gk Sodom kah Gomorrah: netatuppe wuttit tanohketeaonganit Jehovah, neane ohkit Egypt peyan nogque Zoar.
E.13.10 And Lot lifted up his eyes, and beheld all the plain of Jordan, that it was well watered every where, before the LORD destroyed Sodom and Gomorrah, even as the garden of the LORD, like the land of Egypt, as thou comest unto Zoar.

α.13.11 Neit Lot pepenam wame mukoshqut ut Jordan, kah Lot wutchepwaiyeu, kah chadchabeónittuog.
E.13.11 Then Lot chose him all the plain of Jordan; and Lot journeyed east: and they separated themselves the one from the other.

α.13.12 Kah Abram wutohteup wutohket Kanaan, kah Lot wutohteup keitotanash mukoshquttáut, kah weeteup kishke Sodom.
E.13.12 Abram dwelled in the land of Canaan, and Lot dwelled in the cities of the plain, and pitched his tent toward Sodom.

α.13.13 Qut wosketompaog Sodom matchetowog, kah matchenéhéaog Jehovah m8cheke.
E.13.13 But the men of Sodom were wicked and sinners before the LORD exceedingly.

α.13.14 Neit Jehovah unnau Abramoh mahche Lot chippeit wutch nahog: yeuyeu tohshinish kuskesukquash, kah wutuhquáish wutch uttoh [à]pean, nanumayeu, kah sowanayeu, kah wutchepwayeu, kah wutcheksúayeu.
E.13.14 And the LORD said unto Abram, after that Lot was separated from him, Lift up now thine eyes, and look from the place where thou art northward, and southward, and eastward, and westward:

α.13.15 Newutche wame ne ohke nauman kittinnumauunun, kah kuskannemunog micheme.
E.13.15 For all the land which thou seest, to thee will I give it, and to thy seed for ever.

α.13.16 K8skannemunog nuppon onatuh puppissiyeuut ohkeit, nemehkuh wosketomp woogkeetog puppissiyeuash ohkeit, neit woh woogkemau wonk k8skannemunneoh.
E.13.16 And I will make thy seed as the dust of the earth: so that if a man can number the dust of the earth, then shall thy seed also be numbered.

α.13.17 Omkish paspwushaush ohket nesahteag kah ne anukskag: newutche kittinnumaunnun.
E.13.17 Arise, walk through the land in the length of it and in the breadth of it; for I will give it unto thee.

α.13.18 Neit Abram ontattau wetu, kah paont na wuttaiin pagontimmusasqut Mamre, ut Hebron, kah na$ut ayim Altar wutch Jehovah.
E.13.18 Then Abram removed his tent, and came and dwelt in the plain of Mamre, which is in Hebron, and built there an altar unto the LORD.

α.14.1 ONk n$nihyeup pomantog Amraphel ketass8t Shinar, Ariok ketass8t Elassar, Chedorlaomer ketass8t Elam, kah Tidal ketass8t wutohtimoneash.
E.14.1 And it came to pass in the days of Amraphel king of Shinar, Arioch king of Ellasar, Chedorlaomer king of Elam, and Tidal king of nations;

α.14.2 Yeug ayikeg ayeuwuttuonk, ayeuuhkónittue Bera ketass8t Sodom, kah Birsha ketass8t Gomorrah, Shinab ketass8t Admah, kah Shemeber ketass8t Zeboiim, kah ketass8t Bela, ne Zoareu8.
E.14.2 That these made war with Bera king of Sodom, and with Birsha king of Gomorrah, Shinab king of Admah, and Shemeber king of Zeboiim, and the king of Bela, which is Zoar.

α.14.3 Wame yeug weechúhwuttúog wunnohteaiyeuut Siddim, ne salte kehtoh.
E.14.3 All these were joined together in the vale of Siddim, which is the salt sea.

α.14.4 Nabo neese kodtumwae, wuttinneúmoh Chedorlaomer, kah nabo nishwudt kodtum8g wutahquánumóuh.
E.14.4 Twelve years they served Chedorlaomer, and in the thirteenth year they rebelled.

α.14.5 Onk nabo yauut kodtum8k, Chedorlaomer peyau, kah tahs8timwoh neh weeche kah wuttinnetahwhóuh Rephaimsoh ut Ashteroth$Karnaim, kah Zuzimsoh ut Ham, kah Emimsoh ut Shaveth-Kiri[a]thaim:
E.14.5 And in the fourteenth year came Chedorlaomer, and the kings that were with him, and smote the Rephaims in Ashteroth Karnaim, and the Zuzims in Ham, and the Emins in Shaveh Kiriathaim,

α.14.6 Onk Horitsoh 8wadchum8wòut Seir, pajeh mukoshqut Paran; kishke touohkomuk:
E.14.6 And the Horites in their mount Seir, unto Elparan, which is by the wilderness.

α.14.7 Onk qushkeog kah peyaog ut Enmishpat ne Kadesheu8k, kah wuttinnetahwhouh wame wutohtuwoont Amalekiteog, kah wonk Amaritog wodohkitcheg Hazezon$Tamar.
E.14.7 And they returned, and came to Enmishpat, which is Kadesh, and smote all the country of the Amalekites, and also the Amorites, that dwelt in Hazezontamar.

α.14.8 Onk sohham ketass8t Sodom, kah ketass8t Gomorrae, kah ketass8t Admah kah ketass8t Zeboim, kah ketass8t Bela (ne Zoare[u]8) kah n[à]h 8weech8hwuttinneaoh 8nohkóoúut Siddim.
E.14.8 And there went out the king of Sodom, and the king of Gomorrah, and the king of Admah, and the king of Zeboiim, and the king of Bela (the same is Zoar;) and they joined battle with them in the vale of Siddim;

α.14.9 Ayeuuhkonetue Chedorlaomer ketass8t Elam, kah Tidal ketass8t wutohtimóneat, kah Amraphel ketass8t Shinar, kah Arioch ketass8t Ellasar, yauog Ketass8timwog, ayueuuhkonittue napanna.
E.14.9 With Chedorlaomer the king of Elam, and with Tidal king of nations, and Amraphel king of Shinar, and Arioch king of Ellasar; four kings with five.

α.14.10 Onk 8nóohkói Siddim numwohteau slime pussohtégamit, kah ketass8tamwog Sodom kah Gomorra wussemowog, kah na petshaog, kah nag ashqueneanutcheg ussishauog wadchuut.
E.14.10 And the vale of Siddim was full of slimepits; and the kings of Sodom and Gomorrah fled, and fell there; and they that remained fled to the mountain.

α.14.11 Onk wame neemunnumwog maumachiyeuash ut Sodom, kah Gomorra, kah wame meechum, kah moncheog.
E.14.11 And they took all the goods of Sodom and Gomorrah, and all their victuals, and went their way.

α.14.12 Kah tohqunáog Lotoh, Abram weematoh wunnaumonuh, wodohteup Sodom, kah ummaumatchiash, kah moncheog.
E.14.12 And they took Lot, Abram's brother's son, who dwelt in Sodom, and his goods, and departed.

α.14.13 Onk pasuk peyau pohquohhogkup, kah unnau Abramwoh wuttahebrew, newutche ayeu mukoshquttaut Mamre, Wutamórite, weematoh Eshkol, kah weematoh Aner, kah yeuh 8weetauwadtinuh Abram.
E.14.13 And there came one that had escaped, and told Abram the Hebrew; for he dwelt in the plain of Mamre the Amorite, brother of Eshcol, and brother of Aner: and these were confederate with Abram.

α.14.14 Onk n8tog Abram missinnówi keematti, wáâmunau ukquáquodtatteaumoh wuttinnumoh, at neekinitche nehenwonche weekit, nishwe pasuk88wog, kah neg nahshwosuk tahsuog, kah 8nomatuhkaóuh Dan weehque.
E.14.14 And when Abram heard that his brother was taken captive, he armed his trained servants, born in his own house, three hundred and eighteen, and pursued them unto Dan.

α.14.15 Onk chipwúnau wuhhogkuh ayeuuhkonónat nahog, nagum, kah wuttinnúmoh nukonaeu; onk wuttinnetahwhóuh nahog, kah 8namatuhkaóuh en Hoba, menadchéaniyeu Damaskus.
E.14.15 And he divided himself against them, he and his servants, by night, and smote them, and pursued them unto Hobah, which is on the left hand of Damascus.

α.14.16 Onk quhchuwuttau wame maumachiash, kah wonk pas8wau weematuh Lotuh, kah ummaumachiash, kah mittamwossissog, kah missinninnuh.
E.14.16 And he brought back all the goods, and also brought again his brother Lot, and his goods, and the women also, and the people.

α.14.17 Onk Ketass8t Sodom sohham wunnogskauoh, mahche qushkeit wutch aninnetáhwhaonganit Chedorlaomer kah Ketass8timwog weeche, ut 8n[ô]ohkoout Saveh, Ketass8t wut8nôohkôaiyeumut.
E.14.17 And the king of Sodom went out to meet him after his return from the slaughter of Chedorlaomer, and of the kings that were with him, at the valley of Shaveh, which is the king's dale.

α.14.18 Kah Melchizadeck Ketass8t Salem, sohwu[t]tau petukqunnunk kah wine, kah noh mo wussephausuaénumoh quanunkquappit God.
E.14.18 And Melchizedek king of Salem brought forth bread and wine: and he was the priest of the most high God.

α.14.19 Kah 8nanumuh, kah n8wau, 8nanumunaj Abra[m] nashpe quanunkquapit God, wadchanuk qunni kesuk kah ohke.
E.14.19 And he blessed him, and said, Blessed be Abram of the most high God, possessor of heaven and earth:

α.14.20 Kah 8nànumunaj quanukquapit God, noh ponont kummatwomoh ut kenutcheganit: kah wuttinnúmaoh piukque chippai wame teanteaquashinash.
E.14.20 And blessed be the most high God, which hath delivered thine enemies into thy hand. And he gave him tithes of all.

α.14.21 Kah ketass8t Sodom unnau Abramoh, aninnumah keteahogkon8wóog, kah ken neemun[i]sh maumachiash.
E.14.21 And the king of Sodom said unto Abram, Give me the persons, and take the goods to thyself.

α.14.22 Kah Abram unnau ketass8tamwoh Sodom, nutashinn[u]maomp nunnutcheg Jehovah quanunkquapit God, wadchanuk kesuk kah ohke:
E.14.22 And Abram said to the king of Sodom, I have lift up mine hand unto the LORD, the most high God, the possessor of heaven and earth,

α.14.23 Matta woh keneemunnúmm[ù]unn8h pèmunneat, asuh mattógqunap, kah matta woh neemunnúmo ne teaguas ne ahtoan, ishkont woh kussim n8we[e]n[a]ikeh Abram.
E.14.23 That I will not take from a thread even to a shoelatchet, and that I will not take any thing that is thine, lest thou shouldest say, I have made Abram rich:

α.14.24 Webe yeu meechhettit wuskenuog, kah wutchippiyeum8 neg wosketompaog weechogqueúhpanneg Aner, Eshkol & Mamre, neemunnum[o]hhettich wutchippiyeúm8.
E.14.24 Save only that which the young men have eaten, and the portion of the men which went with me, Aner, Eshcol, and Mamre; let them take their portion.

α.15.1 MAhche yeu n$nag, wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaanuk Abram ut monomansinneat, n8wau, ahque wabesish Abram, ne[n] kutogqunneg, kah ahche mishe kutonkquatunk.
E.15.1 After these things the word of the LORD came unto Abram in a vision, saying, Fear not, Abram: I am thy shield, and thy exceeding great reward.

α.15.2 Kah Abram n8wau, Lord Jehouah, teaguas kittinninnúm[a]h, michemwush[a]au matta wunneecháneunat, & piah[q]utuk ut neekit yeuoh Eleaz[e]r wut$Damaskus.
E.15.2 And Abram said, LORD God, what wilt thou give me, seeing I go childless, and the steward of my house is this Eliezer of Damascus?

α.15.3 Kah Abram n8wau, Kusseh, matta kittinnúmaiyeup wuskannem, kah kusseh noh neekhit ut neekit, noh wamahtunk nutahtauonk.
E.15.3 And Abram said, Behold, to me thou hast given no seed: and, lo, one born in my house is mine heir.

α.15.4 Kah kusseh wuttinn8waonk Jehovah en wuhhogkat n8wau, yeuoh matta pish wam[o]htoou kutahtauonk, qut noh nehenwonche wag kenogkussit, noh pish wamohtoau kutahtóonk.
E.15.4 And, behold, the word of the LORD came unto him, saying, This shall not be thine heir; but he that shall come forth out of thine own bowels shall be thine heir.

α.15.5 Onk uppas8woh poquadchik kah n8wau, yeuyeu natauwompish kesukquieu, kah [o]gkem anogqsog, woh wamogkemat: kah wuttinnuh, onk neyane pish k8skannémunog.
E.15.5 And he brought him forth abroad, and said, Look now toward heaven, and tell the stars, if thou be able to number them: and he said unto him, So shall thy seed be.

α.15.6 Onk wunnamptam en Jehovah$ut, kah wutogquanumoh sampweusseáeneuunneat.
E.15.6 And he believed in the LORD; and he counted it to him for righteousness.

α.15.7 Onk wuttinuh, neen Jehovah sohh8wunukquéop wutch Ur Kaldees, onk woh kittinnumaunun ne ohke, woh kut[a]htaunat.
E.15.7 And he said unto him, I am the LORD that brought thee out of Ur of the Chaldees, to give thee this land to inherit it.

α.15.8 Onk n8wau, Woi Manit Jehovah, ut$toh woh nuttinwahteauun nutahtouunat.
E.15.8 And he said, LORD God, whereby shall I know that I shall inherit it?

α.15.9 Onk wuttinnuh neemunnumwansheh kowashinem, nashwekodtumwohkog, & squoshimwe goat nashwekodtumohkog, kah ram nashwekodtumwohkog, kah turtle wuskuhwhunnan, kah wuskisham wuskuhwhunnan.
E.15.9 And he said unto him, Take me an heifer of three years old, and a she goat of three years old, and a ram of three years old, and a turtledove, and a young pigeon.

α.15.10 Kah yeuh 8wame neemunoh kah wutchadchabenuh ut nôeu, kah wuttattatuppissumoh, qut psuksésoh matta wutchadchabenoh.
E.15.10 And he took unto him all these, and divided them in the midst, and laid each piece one against another: but the birds divided he not.

α.15.11 Kah puppinshasog paahettit weyausut, Abram wutamahóhkaoh.
E.15.11 And when the fowls came down upon the carcases, Abram drove them away.

α.15.12 Kah waont mishekouéonk peyaaunuk Abram, kah kusseh mishepohkeni wabesuonk wunuhkukkongqun.
E.15.12 And when the sun was going down, a deep sleep fell upon Abram; and, lo, an horror of great darkness fell upon him.

α.15.13 Kah unnau Abramoh, wahteaue wahteaush k8skannemunog pish penuwohteaóog ohke matta wuttaihéou, kah pish 8tinninnúmunneauh, kah nag pish wutonkquomo[m]héouh yeuut pasuk8we kodtumwae.
E.15.13 And he said unto Abram, Know of a surety that thy seed shall be a stranger in a land that is not their's, and shall serve them; and they shall afflict them four hundred years;

α.15.14 Kah wonk ne wutohtimóin nag neh wadtinneúmhettiche pish n8summoog kah ompetak pish sohhamwog mishénaeetuonganit.
E.15.14 And also that nation, whom they shall serve, will I judge: and afterward shall they come out with great substance.

α.15.15 Onk pish kutom k8shut wunohteaeu, pish kuttit posukkinit ut k8nenukukquinneat.
E.15.15 And thou shalt go to thy fathers in peace; thou shalt be buried in a good old age.

α.15.16 Qut yauut pometuonganú8g pish wonk qushkeog, newutche ummatcheseongan8 Amoritsog asquam numwohtáno.
E.15.16 But in the fourth generation they shall come hither again: for the iniquity of the Amorites is not yet full.

α.15.17 Kah n$nih w[a]nt onk pohkenai, kah kusseh neahhuttannunnag pagutto[o]8k, kah wequánanteg chagohtag pa[n]nupshaum8 nashauwe chepaiyeuut.
E.15.17 And it came to pass, that, when the sun went down, and it was dark, behold a smoking furnace, and a burning lamp that passed between those pieces.

α.15.18 Ne kesukok Jehovah wuno8wau Abramoh, n8wau, en k8skannemunut nummagun yeu ohke wutch Egypt Sepuut, onk yeanke[h]teihtequt Euphrates.
E.15.18 In the same day the LORD made a covenant with Abram, saying, Unto thy seed have I given this land, from the river of Egypt unto the great river, the river Euphrates:

α.15.19 Ukkenit, Ukkenezit, U[k]kadmonit.
E.15.19 The Kenites, and the Kenizzites, and the Kadmonites,

α.15.20 Wuthittit, Upperisit, kah Rephaimog.
E.15.20 And the Hittites, and the Perizzites, and the Rephaims,

α.15.21 Kah Wutamorit, kah Ukkananit, kah Wkgirgasit, kah wut$Jebusit.
E.15.21 And the Amorites, and the Canaanites, and the Girgashites, and the Jebusites.

α.16.1 QUt Sarai Abram ummittamwussoh matta wunneekitteunk8oh; kah wuttinnúmu mittumwussissoh wutegiptionuh ussowesu Hagar.
E.16.1 Now Sarai Abram's wife bare him no children: and she had an handmaid, an Egyptian, whose name was Hagar.

α.16.2 Kah Sarai unnau Abramoh, kusseh yeu$yeu God numméchehúk k8wehquetumoush weet[u]am nuttinnum, mamiit woh n8nechā nashpe nagum: kah Abram wun8swetauoh ne an8wadt Sarai.
E.16.2 And Sarai said unto Abram, Behold now, the LORD hath restrained me from bearing: I pray thee, go in unto my maid; it may be that I may obtain children by her. And Abram hearkened to the voice of Sarai.

α.16.3 Neit Sarai ummittumwussoh Abram, nemunau Hagaroh wuttinnum wut$egiptianoh, mahche piukque kodtumwae wutohket Abram ohket Kanaan, kah wuttinnumauunoh wessukeh Abram 8mittumwississinneat.
E.16.3 And Sarai Abram's wife took Hagar her maid the Egyptian, after Abram had dwelt ten years in the land of Canaan, and gave her to her husband Abram to be his wife.

α.16.4 Kah petutteauóneau Hagaroh kah wompoquoouh, kah wahteunk 8wompoquauonk ummishonanumáu wussonksquaumoh, nehenwonche wuskesukqut.
E.16.4 And he went in unto Hagar, and she conceived: and when she saw that she had conceived, her mistress was despised in her eyes.

α.16.5 Kah Sarai unnau Abramoh, nuttinhetteáonk kuttinhin, kuttinnumanup nuttinnũ ut kuhpânôganit, kah nag 8wompwequauonk nummishananumit nehenwonche wuskesukqut, Jehovah wussittich nashauwe ken, kah nashauwe nen.
E.16.5 And Sarai said unto Abram, My wrong be upon thee: I have given my maid into thy bosom; and when she saw that she had conceived, I was despised in her eyes: the LORD judge between me and thee.

α.16.6 Kah Abram únnau Saraihoh, kusseh kittinnum kenutcheganit appu, unneh uttô[h] en wunegik ut kuskesukqut: kah Sarai onkapunanont, 8semoetunkquoh wutch anaquabit.
E.16.6 But Abram said unto Sarai, Behold, thy maid is in thine hand; do to her as it pleaseth thee. And when Sarai dealt hardly with her, she fled from her face.

α.16.7 Kah wunnamheuh wutangelsumoh God ut kishke tohekomu ut touohkomukqut, kishke tohkekomuut ut mayut Shur.
E.16.7 And the angel of the LORD found her by a fountain of water in the wilderness, by the fountain in the way to Shur.

α.16.8 Kah n8wau, Hagar wuttinnúmoh Sarai tunoh k8m, kah tunoh kuttoh, kah n8wau, n8chepuhh8wam wuskesukqut nussonksquom Sarai.
E.16.8 And he said, Hagar, Sarai's maid, whence camest thou? and whither wilt thou go? And she said, I flee from the face of my mistress Sarai.

α.16.9 Onk wutangelsumoh J[o]hovah wuttinuh qushkeshe[n] kussonksqomut, kah hopush ut agwu wunnutcheganit.
E.16.9 And the angel of the LORD said unto her, Return to thy mistress, and submit thyself under her hands.

α.16.10 Onk wutangelsumoh Jehovah wuttinuh muttaanhennon nummuttaáneh k8skannemunog m8cheke, matta pish waogkemoóg, newutche monaog.
E.16.10 And the angel of the LORD said unto her, I will multiply thy seed exceedingly, that it shall not be numbered for multitude.

α.16.11 Kah wutangelsumoh God wuttinuh kusseh k8wompequau, pish k8naumoni, kah pish kuttissowen Ishmael, newutche n8tam God kutohquanum[ó]onk.
E.16.11 And the angel of the LORD said unto her, Behold, thou art with child and shalt bear a son, and shalt call his name Ishmael; because the LORD hath heard thy affliction.

α.16.12 Kah pish touohkomukquoshimweninnú8, wunnutcheg ayeuuhkoneau nish$noh wosketomp, & nish$noh wosketomp wunnutcheg ayeuwohkonuk: kah pish ayeu anaquabenit wame weematoh.
E.16.12 And he will be a wild man; his hand will be against every man, and every man's hand against him; and he shall dwell in the presence of all his brethren.

α.16.13 Onk wutti[s]sowenon Manit ne an8wop ken Manit kenaeh, newutche n8wau sun nunnatinneah noh nógqueh?
E.16.13 And she called the name of the LORD that spake unto her, Thou God seest me: for she said, Have I also here looked after him that seeth me?

α.16.14 Newutche wuttohhamuk ussowétamun Beerlahairoi, kusseh nashauwe Kadesh kah Bered ohteau.
E.16.14 Wherefore the well was called Beerlahairoi; behold, it is between Kadesh and Bered.

α.16.15 Onk Hagar neechau wunnaumonuh Abram, kah Abram wuttissowenon wunnaumonuh Hagar neechaje[h], Ishmael.
E.16.15 And Hagar bare Abram a son: and Abram called his son's name, which Hagar bare, Ishmael.

α.16.16 Kah Abram shwòsuk tahshinchag kódtumwohkomup kah nequtta, Hagar neechad Ishameloh wutch Abramoh.
E.16.16 And Abram was fourscore and six years old, when Hagar bare Ishmael to Abram.

α.17.1 KAH abram pask8gun audtashinchage kodtumwohkog ka[h] pask8gun, Jehovah nae[i]hte[á]u Abramoh, kah wuttinuh, nen Manit wame manuhkésee, pompomushaush anaquabeh kah pannuppe wunneetush.
E.17.1 And when Abram was ninety years old and nine, the LORD appeared to Abram, and said unto him, I am the Almighty God; walk before me, and be thou perfect.

α.17.2 Kah nutayim n8n8waonk nashauwe nen kah ken, kah kummuttaanhesh m8cheke m8cheke.
E.17.2 And I will make my covenant between me and thee, and will multiply thee exceedingly.

α.17.3 Kah Abram sukoshk[o]dtassun, kah God ukken8nun, n8wau.
E.17.3 And Abram fell on his face: and God talked with him, saying,

α.17.4 Papaume nen, kusseh n8n8wáonk k8weetomuk, kah ken pish wut8shin monagish wutohtimóneash.
E.17.4 As for me, behold, my covenant is with thee, and thou shalt be a father of many nations.

α.17.5 Kah matta pish wonk kuttehinnit[$]eóh Abram, qut pish kuttissowis Abraham, newutche katayimoush 8t8shin monagish wutohtimóneash. 
E.17.5 Neither shall thy name any more be called Abram, but thy name shall be Abraham; for a father of many nations have I made thee.

α.17.6 Kah kummuttaanhesh m8cheke m8cheke, kah kutayimoush wutohtimoneash, kah ketass8tamwog pish 8mwog kuhhogkat.
E.17.6 And I will make thee exceeding fruitful, and I will make nations of thee, and kings shall come out of thee.

α.17.7 Kah nummenuhketeuh n8n8waonk nashauwe nen kah ken, kah k8skannemunn[e]og nahohtóeu ken, ut uppométuongan8wout, wutch machemohtag wunn8waonk, kah woh neen kummanitt8m, onk k8skannemunneog nahohtôeu ken.
E.17.7 And I will establish my covenant between me and thee and thy seed after thee in their generations for an everlasting covenant, to be a God unto thee, and to thy seed after thee.

α.17.8 Kah kittinnumaush kah k8skannemunneog nahoht[ô]eu ken ohke neadt pen8wehteayeap, wame ohke Kanaan, machemohtag ohtoonk, kah nen n$nag** ummanitt8m8oh.
E.17.8 And I will give unto thee, and to thy seed after thee, the land wherein thou art a stranger, all the land of Canaan, for an everlasting possession; and I will be their God.

α.17.9 Kah wuttinuh God Abrahamoh, kah pish kenanaeihteóh n8n8waonk, ken kah k8skannemunneog nahoht[ó]eu ken uppometuongan8óut.
E.17.9 And God said unto Abraham, Thou shalt keep my covenant therefore, thou, and thy seed after thee in their generations.

α.17.10 Yeu n8n8waonk uttoh pish nanauwéhteauóg ut nashauwe nen kah ken & k8skannemunog na[h]ohtoeu ken, nishnoh pasuk wosketomp pish quoshqusausu.
E.17.10 This is my covenant, which ye shall keep, between me and you and thy seed after thee; Every man child among you shall be circumcised.

α.17.11 Kah pish kukquôshqussumumw8 ut uhquáeu k8weyaus8, kah yeu pish kukkinneasuonk wutche wunn8waonk nashauwe ut nen kah kenaau.
E.17.11 And ye shall circumcise the flesh of your foreskin; and it shall be a token of the covenant betwixt me and you.

α.17.12 Kah noh shwosuk audtahshikqun apit, pish quoshqusausu [k]enugkeu kenaau, nish$noh wosketomp ut kuppometuongan8wóut, noh ut neekit weetuomut, kah noh tapwhut howane penuwot wutche teauguash, uttiyeuoh mat wánaumóneyéan.
E.17.12 And he that is eight days old shall be circumcised among you, every man child in your generations, he that is born in the house, or bought with money of any stranger, which is not of thy seed.

α.17.13 Noh ut neekhit keekit, kah n$noh adtoáop teauguash, noh mos wunnamuhkut quoshqusausu, kah n8n8w[a]onk pish ohteau keyausut, wutche machemohtag wunn8waonk.
E.17.13 He that is born in thy house, and he that is bought with thy money, must needs be circumcised: and my covenant shall be in your flesh for an everlasting covenant.

α.17.14 Kah matta quoshqusauseg wosketomp, 8weyaus ut uhquáeu matta quoshqusaussu8k, n$noh kéteahogkou pish tumwuswau wutch ummissinninnút[u], n$noh p[ó]qunnu[m] n8n8waonk.
E.17.14 And the uncircumcised man child whose flesh of his foreskin is not circumcised, that soul shall be cut off from his people; he hath broken my covenant.

α.17.15 Kah wuttnih God Abrahamoh, papaume Sarai ummittamwussoh, matta pish kittehhenoh Sarai, qut pish ussowesu Sarah.
E.17.15 And God said unto Abraham, As for Sarai thy wife, thou shalt not call her name Sarai, but Sarah shall her name be.

α.17.16 Kah pish n8nanum, kah kittinnumaush wunnaumonuh nashpe nagum kah n8nanum, kah noh pish wutohtimowonganu8, ukketass8tamóm8oh missinninnúog pish 8mwog wutch wuhhogkat.
E.17.16 And I will bless her, and give thee a son also of her: yea, I will bless her, and she shall be a mother of nations; kings of people shall be of her.

α.17.17 Neit Abraham sukoshkodtassun, kah hahanou, kah n8wau ut wuttahut, sun woh n8neecha[n], nequt pasuk8we kodtumwohkomon, kah Sarah pasak8gun tashinchage kodtumwohkog, sun pish neechau?
E.17.17 Then Abraham fell upon his face, and laughed, and said in his heart, Shall a child be born unto him that is an hundred years old? and shall Sarah, that is ninety years old, bear?

α.17.18 Onk Abraham unnau Goduh, Woi onk woh Ishmael pomantam ut anaquabean.
E.17.18 And Abraham said unto God, O that Ishmael might live before thee!

α.17.19 Kah God n8wau, Sarah kummittumwos wunnamuhkut pish k8ch wunnaumoni, kah pish kuttissowen Isaak, kah pish nummenuhkehteau n8n8waonk wutche machemohtag wunn8waonk, kah wuskannemunneoh nahohtóeu.
E.17.19 And God said, Sarah thy wife shall bear thee a son indeed; and thou shalt call his name Isaac: and I will establish my covenant with him for an everlasting covenant, and with his seed after him.

α.17.20 Kah papaume Ishmael ken8taush, kusseh n8nanum, nummishummeechumeh kah nummuttaáneh m8cheke m8cheke, pish nabonees88woh santimoh, onk nummishteoh wutohtim.
E.17.20 And as for Ishmael, I have heard thee: Behold, I have blessed him, and will make him fruitful, and will multiply him exceedingly; twelve princes shall he beget, and I will make him a great nation.

α.17.21 Qut n8n8waonk nummenuhkehteauo[u] Isaak, uttoh woh Sarah neechadche wutche ken ne wonk aquompak kodtum8k.
E.17.21 But my covenant will I establish with Isaac, which Sarah shall bear unto thee at this set time in the next year.

α.17.22 Kah ahque keket8kauont, kah God ashpet wutch Abrahamut.
E.17.22 And he left off talking with him, and God went up from Abraham.

α.17.23 Neit Abram neemunau Ishmaeloh wunnaumonuh, kah wame neekinutche ut weekit, & wame adtoadcheh wutche tea[u]gash nish$noh pasuk wosketomp, kenugke wosketompáog weekit Abraham, onk quoshqussum weyaus ut uhquae, ne kesukok ne àn8wop God.
E.17.23 And Abraham took Ishmael his son, and all that were born in his house, and all that were bought with his money, every male among the men of Abraham's house; and circumcised the flesh of their foreskin in the selfsame day, as God had said unto him.

α.17.24 Kah Abraham pask8gun tahshinchage kodtumwohkom, kah pask8gun, ne quoshqusuk 8weyaus ut uhqua[e].
E.17.24 And Abraham was ninety years old and nine, when he was circumcised in the flesh of his foreskin.

α.17.25 Kah Ishmael wunnaumonh nabo nishwe kodtumwohkumoh ne quoshqussuk 8weyaus ut uhquae.
E.17.25 And Ishmael his son was thirteen years old, when he was circumcised in the flesh of his foreskin.

α.17.26 Ne keṣukok quoshqusausu Abraham kah Ishmael wunnaumonuh.
E.17.26 In the selfsame day was Abraham circumcised, and Ishmael his son.

α.17.27 Kah wame wosketompaog ut weekit, neekinutcheh ut weekit, kah adtoohpoh wutche teauguas penuwohteuh 8weeche quoshqusau[ssun]euh.
E.17.27 And all the men of his house, born in the house, and bought with money of the stranger, were circumcised with him.

α.18.1 ONk Jehovah naeihtaau ut pagontimusasqut Mamre, kah appu wusquoantamut weekit kâsittag.
E.18.1 And the LORD appeared unto him in the plains of Mamre: and he sat in the tent door in the heat of the day;

α.18.2 Kah ashpuhquait natawompu kah kusseh, nishuoh wosketompuh weechekompaumuk, kah nauont quogqúeu wutch squoantamut weekit, kah wunnogskauwoh, kah mauwaeu en ohkekontu.
E.18.2 And he lift up his eyes and looked, and, lo, three men stood by him: and when he saw them, he ran to meet them from the tent door, and bowed himself toward the ground,

α.18.3 Nah n8wau nusontimom, namehteaúnon kitteamonteànittuonk ut anaquabean, ahque paumushaush k8wehquetumoush wutch kittinninnúmut.
E.18.3 And said, My LORD, if now I have found favour in thy sight, pass not away, I pray thee, from thy servant:

α.18.4 Neemskomunach nippeémes k8wehquetumoush, kah kutchessittau8k kusseet8woash kah anwôsinn8k ut kishkunk.
E.18.4 Let a little water, I pray you, be fetched, and wash your feet, and rest yourselves under the tree:

α.18.5 Kah neemskom kodchuhkoi petukqunneg, neemóunúhkun kuttahh8wóog, mahche ne nag woh kummonchem8, newutche yeuwadj payauónat kittinnum, onk nag n8wáog ussish ne án8wáan.
E.18.5 And I will fetch a morsel of bread, and comfort ye your hearts; after that ye shall pass on: for therefore are ye come to your servant. And they said, So do, as thou hast said.

α.18.6 Kah Abraham kenupshau en wetuomut en Sarahut, kah n8wau, teanuk nanashwunush shwe peksú8 nanohkinn[ô]hsik n8khik, tuttouhpunash, petukqunnunganéhtaash ut n8tau a[n]otag.
E.18.6 And Abraham hastened into the tent unto Sarah, and said, Make ready quickly three measures of fine meal, knead it, and make cakes upon the hearth.

α.18.7 Kah Abraham ussishau wunneetasumut, kah nôs8au Kalfoh n8hkésu kah weekun, kah uppaudtaonuh wuskénuh, kah teanuk ukkesoh.
E.18.7 And Abraham ran unto the herd, and fetcht a calf tender and good, and gave it unto a young man; and he hasted to dress it.

α.18.8 Kah nemunum butter kah sogkodtunk, Kalfoh ne kesiswoncheh, kah upponuh anaquabenit nahoh, kah noh kishke neepau ut kishkunk onk meetsuog.
E.18.8 And he took butter, and milk, and the calf which he had dressed, and set it before them; and he stood by them under the tree, and they did eat.

α.18.9 Kah wuttinnóuh, uttoh woh Sarah kummittamwus? kah n8wau kusseh weetuomut.
E.18.9 And they said unto him, Where is Sarah thy wife? And he said, Behold, in the tent.

α.18.10 Onk n8wau, qushkeon nukqushkem en kuhhogkaáau, ne adt8che pomantam8wonganú8k, kah kusseh Sarah kummittumwussis pish wunnaumonaieu, kah Sarah n8tam ut weetuomut, squontamut, ut uppusquanuwóut.
E.18.10 And he said, I will certainly return unto thee according to the time of life; and, lo, Sarah thy wife shall have a son. And Sarah heard it in the tent door, which was behind him.

α.18.11 Kah Abraham kah Sarah mohtantam88og, kah sepepomantamwog, kah Sarah wutahquenaiin neyane mittumwussissog.
E.18.11 Now Abraham and Sarah were old and well stricken in age; and it ceased to be with Sarah after the manner of women.

α.18.12 Newutche Sarah kemeu hahanu, kah n8wau mohtántamon woh n8weekontam8ongan, kah nussontimom wonk mohta[n]tog?
E.18.12 Therefore Sarah laughed within herself, saying, After I am waxed old shall I have pleasure, my lord being old also?

α.18.13 Kah Jehovah unnau Abrahamoh, tohwhutch Sarah hahanit? an8wadt, sun wunnamuhkut woh neecham mohtantamon?
E.18.13 And the LORD said unto Abraham, Wherefore did Sarah laugh, saying, Shall I of a surety bear a child, which am old?

α.18.14 Woh wussiog-gehukqun Jehovah[?] neádt8che kuhk8wámuk pish nukqushkem en kuhhogkat, neádt8che pomantamowonganu8k, kah Sarah pish wunnaumónieu.
E.18.14 Is any thing too hard for the LORD? At the time appointed I will return unto thee, according to the time of life, and Sarah shall have a son.

α.18.15 Neit Sarah quen8wau, n8wau, matta nutahánu, newutche wabesu; onk n8wau matchaog, qut kutahánup.
E.18.15 Then Sarah denied, saying, I laughed not; for she was afraid. And he said, Nay; but thou didst laugh.

α.18.16 Kah wosketompaog neepoog nawutch, onk nuhquaéog Sodom: kah Abraham 8weechauuh, ummonchanuh en mayut.
E.18.16 And the men rose up from thence, and looked toward Sodom: and Abraham went with them to bring them on the way.

α.18.17 Onk Jehovah n8wau, sun woh nutáhtuttáuon Abraham, ne kodnéhheog?
E.18.17 And the LORD said, Shall I hide from Abraham that thing which I do;

α.18.18 Newutche Abraham wunnamuhkut pish 8tohtimóin missi kah menuhkoi, kah wame wutohtimóneash ohkeit pish 8nanumoog ut nagum.
E.18.18 Seeing that Abraham shall surely become a great and mighty nation, and all the nations of the earth shall be blessed in him?

α.18.19 Newutche n8wáeh, noh woh piahtimau wunneechanoh, kah weechininnúmonche nahohtôeu, kah pish nanaihteaog ummay Jehovah, ussen sampwagk, kah wussittumôonk, onk woh Jehovah uppaudtauon Abrahamoh ne anomp.
E.18.19 For I know him, that he will command his children and his household after him, and they shall keep the way of the LORD, to do justice and judgment; that the LORD may bring upon Abraham that which he hath spoken of him.

α.18.20 Kah Jehovah n8wau, newutche missi ummauunitteauáonk Sodom, kah Gomorrah, kah newutche ummatchéseonganooash ahche uhqunneunkquodtash.
E.18.20 And the LORD said, Because the cry of Sodom and Gomorrah is great, and because their sin is very grievous;

α.18.21 Nunn8kem yeuyeu, kah nunnaum toh wuttin usseneau neyan8wómuk, ne paôónukqueh qut matta n$nán8g, onk nukkodwahteoun:
E.18.21 I will go down now, and see whether they have done altogether according to the cry of it, which is come unto me; and if not, I will know.

α.18.22 Kah w[e]sketompaog qushkeog na$wutch, kah auog nogque Sodom$ut, qut Abraham ash neepau anaquabit Jehovah.
E.18.22 And the men turned their faces from thence, and went toward Sodom: but Abraham stood yet before the LORD.

α.18.23 Onk Abraham uppas8sukauoh, kah n8wau, Sun kuppagwun sampwesecheg weeche matchet8wog?
E.18.23 And Abraham drew near, and said, Wilt thou also destroy the righteous with the wicked?

α.18.24 Paguodcheh napannatashinchagodtog sampwesecheg ut keiht8tanit, sun woh kuppagw[u]n, kah matta woh k8wadchanum8h ne ayeuonk, newutche napannatahshinchagodtog sampwesecheg na apitcheg?
E.18.24 Peradventure there be fifty righteous within the city: wilt thou also destroy and not spare the place for the fifty righteous that are therein?

α.18.25 Na8sukash ne ussen, nushon sampweussécheg weeche matcheet8woh: kah sampwesecheg neyan[e]yeuunát matcheet8ut, na8sukash, noh wussituk wame muttaok, sun mat sampwesu?
E.18.25 That be far from thee to do after this manner, to slay the righteous with the wicked: and that the righteous should be as the wicked, that be far from thee: Shall not the Judge of all the earth do right?

α.18.26 Kah Jehovah n8wau n[à]méheog napannatahshinchagodtog sampweusseáenúog ut Sodom, ennom8tani, neit nukketeahôog wame neg noh apitcheg newutche nág.
E.18.26 And the LORD said, If I find in Sodom fifty righteous within the city, then I will spare all the place for their sakes.

α.18.27 Neit Abraham wunnamp8hamaúoh, kah n8wau, kusseh yeuyeu, wo[û]s nutapshom ken8non Jehovah, qut nen webe puppisai kah pukque.
E.18.27 And Abraham answered and said, Behold now, I have taken upon me to speak unto the LORD, which am but dust and ashes:

α.18.28 Paguodche matta wutappéineau napannatahsuog sampwesecheg, neh woh napanna wutteáshinéhchagsinneau, sun kuppáguadtoh wame ke[i]htotan ukquenassinneaóut napanna tahsuog? kah n8wau, naut nameheoh yauonchagkodtog kah napanna tahsuog, matta nuppaguadtaónun.
E.18.28 Peradventure there shall lack five of the fifty righteous: wilt thou destroy all the city for lack of five? And he said, If I find there forty and five, I will not destroy it.

α.18.29 Kah wonk ukken8nuh & n8wau paguodche woh naut kenameh yauonchagkodtog kah n8wau matta woh nutussen newutche yauonchagodtog.
E.18.29 And he spake unto him yet again, and said, Peradventure there shall be forty found there. And he said, I will not do it for forty's sake.

α.18.30 Kah wuttinuh wóiyikisseuh k8wehquetumoush ahque musquantaj God, kah nukket8k[a]m, paguadche naut kenameh shwinchagodtog kah n8wau matta woh nutussen naut nameheog shwinchagodtog.
E.18.30 And he said unto him, Oh let not the LORD be angry, and I will speak: Peradventure there shall thirty be found there. And he said, I will not do it, if I find thirty there.

α.18.31 Kah n8wau, kusseh yeuyeu wôus ne nuttinne ken8non God, paguodche woh nesneechagkodtog kenameh naut, kah n8wau matta woh nuppaguanoog wutche neesneechagodtoh.
E.18.31 And he said, Behold now, I have taken upon me to speak unto the LORD: Peradventure there shall be twenty found there. And he said, I will not destroy it for twenty's sake.

α.18.32 Kah n8wau woiyikisseuh k8wehquetumoush ahque musquantaj God, kah webe majish pasukqut nukkeket8kam, paguodche woh kenameh piukqussuog: kah n8wau, matta woh nuppaguanoog piukqusséhettit.
E.18.32 And he said, Oh let not the LORD be angry, and I will speak yet but this once: Peradventure ten shall be found there. And he said, I will not destroy it for ten's sake.

α.18.33 Neit Jehovah monchu quenau mahche ken8nont Abraham, onk Abraham au wutohket.
E.18.33 And the LORD went his way, as soon as he had left communing with Abraham: and Abraham returned unto his place.

α.19.1 ONk neesuog Angelsog peyauog Sodom, wannongk88k kah Lot áppu 8squoantamut Sodom, n[â]ont, neepau onk woh wunnogskauoh, kah nau[aé]mo wuskesuk en ohkekontu.
E.19.1 And there came two angels to Sodom at even; and Lot sat in the gate of Sodom: and Lot seeing them rose up to meet them; and he bowed himself with his face toward the ground;

α.19.2 Kah n8wau kusseh yeuyeu nussontimomog quinnupp[e]gk k[o]wéquetumauúnnumw8 weekit kuttinninnúmw8, kah nequttaqunohteagk, kah kutchessittau8k kusseet8woash, onk nompoáeu omohkeóg pish kummonchemw8 kuttâongan8w[ó]ut, kah n8waog matta, qut nutapimun poquadchik wompanu
E.19.2 And he said, Behold now, my lords, turn in, I pray you, into your servant's house, and tarry all night, and wash your feet, and ye shall rise up early, and go on your ways. And they said, Nay; but we will abide in the street all night.

α.19.3 Kah m8cheke ummenuhke na[t]umpassúmuh nahog, kah qunnuppeog, petutteaog weekit, onk ummishadtupweheuh, kah apwau weekog petukqunnuk, kah meesuog.
E.19.3 And he pressed upon them greatly; and they turned in unto him, and entered into his house; and he made them a feast, and did bake unleavened bread, and they did eat.

α.19.4 Qut asquam kaéhetteg wosketompaog ne Keiht8tanat, wosketompaog Sodom, weenuhkomog wetu, wuskenuog kah kutchisog, wame missinninnúog waéenu Otan.
E.19.4 But before they lay down, the men of the city, even the men of Sodom, compassed the house round, both old and young, all the people from every quarter:

α.19.5 Kah wehkomóog Lotuh, kah wuttinóuh, uttiyeug wosketompaog pétakunkqueáneg yeu nohk[o]g? sohwhutaiinnean, onk woh n8wahéonnónog.
E.19.5 And they called unto Lot, and said unto him, Where are the men which came in to thee this night? bring them out unto us, that we may know them.

α.19.6 Onk Lot sohham wutch squoantamut, kah yeánittánum nahohtôeu.
E.19.6 And Lot went out at the door unto them, and shut the door after him,

α.19.7 Kah n8wau k8wehquetumaunumw8 neematog ahque ne en matchesegk.
E.19.7 And said, I pray you, brethren, do not so wickedly.

α.19.8 Kusseh yeuyeu nesuog nuttânog, matta waheunkeg wosketompuh, k8wehquetumauuñumw8 nag kuppaudtaunnaóont kenaau, kah unnehhuk nag ut$toh en tapeneamóg ut[-] kuskesukkouóut, webe yeug wosketompaog ahque toh unn[é]heuk, newutche yeu waj peyaog ut agwe onkouohtáut neekit.
E.19.8 Behold now, I have two daughters which have not known man; let me, I pray you, bring them out unto you, and do ye to them as is good in your eyes: only unto these men do nothing; for therefore came they under the shadow of my roof.

α.19.9 Kah n8waog amakompau, wonk n8waog yeuoh pasuk wuttinneapeyon, kah kodwussittum, yeuyeu kumm8chéke kummatchenehennumun onk nagoh, onk ukquentauóuh wosketompuh Lotuh m8cheke, onk pas8tshaog kod pohquanumwog squoant.
E.19.9 And they said, Stand back. And they said again, This one fellow came in to sojourn, and he will needs be a judge: now will we deal worse with thee, than with them. And they pressed sore upon the man, even Lot, and came near to break the door.

α.19.10 Qut wosketompaog s[o]nkhenchaiéog, kah pethennaog Lotuh wetuómut, en wuhhogkaoont, onk yeanittânumwog.
E.19.10 But the men put forth their hand, and pulled Lot into the house to them, and shut to the door.

α.19.11 Kah wuttogkomouh wosketompuh pogkenumoonk, neg apitcheg squoantamut, papeissitcheg kah matikénukeg, onk sauanumwog ummiskomunnaout squoant.
E.19.11 And they smote the men that were at the door of the house with blindness, both small and great: so that they wearied themselves to find the door.

α.19.12 Kah wosketompaog unnaog Lotuh, sun yeu wuttapinneau onkatoganeg, asuh waseenumukqueaneg, kah kenaumonog kah kuttânog, kah nish$noh teag ahtôan yeuut otanit, yeu$wutch sohh8us yeu wutch ayeuonganit.
E.19.12 And the men said unto Lot, Hast thou here any besides? son in law, and thy sons, and thy daughters, and whatsoever thou hast in the city, bring them out of this place:

α.19.13 Newutche nuppaguatauunn[a]n yeu ayeuonk, newutche ummishont8waongan8 nano missi ut anaquabit Jehovah, kah Jehovah nuttann8nukqun nuppaguatauunnanonat.
E.19.13 For we will destroy this place, because the cry of them is waxen great before the face of the LORD; and the LORD hath sent us to destroy it.

α.19.14 Onk Lot sohham, ken8nau wasenumukqutcheh, uttoh weetauomunutcheh wutt[ô]noh, kah n8wau, neepau8k, sohham8k yeu wutche ayeuonganit, newutche Jehovah yeu uppaguatauun otan: qut ut wuskesukqut wasenumukqutcheh neyane ohk8wau mamúskeyimuk.
E.19.14 And Lot went out, and spake unto his sons in law, which married his daughters, and said, Up, get you out of this place; for the LORD will destroy this city. But he seemed as one that mocked unto his sons in law.

α.19.15 Kah nompoáeu Angelsog wahwápimàog Lotuh, n8waog, omkish, nee[m]un kummittumwos kah neeswe kuttânog, yeu apitcheg, ishkont kummahtus, otan ut umm[a]tches[e]onganit.
E.19.15 And when the morning arose, then the angels hastened Lot, saying, Arise, take thy wife, and thy two daughters, which are here; lest thou be consumed in the iniquity of the city.

α.19.16 Kah padjeh n$naiyit, wosketompaog ukkogken[ô]un wunnutcheg, kah wunnutcheg ummittumwussoh, kah wunnutcheganoash neswe wutt[ô]nuh Jehovah k[o]dtumonteanumōt) kah wussohh8un[o]uh & upponouh poquadch8tanit.
E.19.16 And while he lingered, the men laid hold upon his hand, and upon the hand of his wife, and upon the hand of his two daughters; the LORD being merciful unto him: and they brought him forth, and set him without the city.

α.19.17 Onk n$nih pas8wahettit poquadchit n8wau pohquohwutaush kuppomantamóonk, ahqúe ompamuhquash, asuh ahque apsh wame mukoshquttáut, pohquohush en wadchuut, ishkont kutushk[o]mehit.
E.19.17 And it came to pass, when they had brought them forth abroad, that he said, Escape for thy life; look not behind thee, neither stay thou in all the plain; escape to the mountain, lest thou be consumed.

α.19.18 Kah Lot wuttinuh náhoh woi ahquye n$naj nussontimom.
E.19.18 And Lot said unto them, Oh, not so, my LORD:

α.19.19 Kusseh yeuyeu kittinnum miskom kitteamonteaneteaonk ut anaquabean & kummishteaun kummonaneteaonk neasé[a]nshean, wadchanumo[n] nuppomantamoonk matta woh teanuk nuppohquonum8 en wadchuut ishkont wosketuonk nunnahtwunuk kah woh nunnup.
E.19.19 Behold now, thy servant hath found grace in thy sight, and thou hast magnified thy mercy, which thou hast shewed unto me in saving my life; and I cannot escape to the mountain, lest some evil take me, and I die:

α.19.20 Kusseh yeuyeu, yeu otan páhs8 woh nútusishonat, kah pe[a]sin, woh na p[à]udshonti (matta peasininn8?) & pish nukketeahogkou pomantam.
E.19.20 Behold now, this city is near to flee unto, and it is a little one: Oh, let me escape thither, (is it not a little one?) and my soul shall live.

α.19.21 Onk wuttinuh kusseh kutapeneaumaunun yeu$wutche, kah matta woh nukkepuhtea[ù] yeu Otan, ne wéhquetamaean.
E.19.21 And he said unto him, See, I have accepted thee concerning this thing also, that I will not overthrow this city, for the which thou hast spoken.

α.19.22 Kenupsash ná ussishash newutche matta woh toh nutussúh, toh woh na kuppeasin, newajeh hettamuk Otan Zoar.
E.19.22 Haste thee, escape thither; for I cannot do anything till thou be come thither. Therefore the name of the city was called Zoar.

α.19.23 Nepàus paspishop ut ohkeit, Lot petutte[á]dt Zoar,
E.19.23 The sun was risen upon the earth when Lot entered into Zoar.

α.19.24 Neit Jehovah sokanum ut Sodom & ut Gomorra brimstone, kah n8tau wutche Jehovah wutche kesukquiug.
E.19.24 Then the LORD rained upon Sodom and upon Gomorrah brimstone and fire from the LORD out of heaven;

α.19.25 Kah ukkepuhonash yeush Keihtotanash kah wamemukoshqut kah wame neg noh apitcheg Otanatash & ne noh adtanegik ohkekontu.
E.19.25 And he overthrew those cities, and all the plain, and all the inhabitants of the cities, and that which grew upon the ground.

α.19.26 Qut ummit[t]umwussoh ompámuhquaéoh wutch uppusquanit, kah ayeuau pogkomu[h]quonkanu salt.
E.19.26 But his wife looked back from behind him, and she became a pillar of salt.

α.19.27 Kah Abraham t8keu nompo[a]éu en na neepokup ut anaquabit Jehovah.
E.19.27 And Abraham gat up early in the morning to the place where he stood before the LORD:

α.19.28 Kah unnohquaeu nogqueu Sodom kah Gomorra, kah nogqueu wame ne ohkit mukoshqutaut kah umm[o]neneamun, kah kusseh puku[t]aou [o]hket onatuh ahhut sabasumuk áhu[n]nupukutáig.
E.19.28 And he looked toward Sodom and Gomorrah, and toward all the land of the plain, and beheld, and, lo, the smoke of the country went up as the smoke of a furnace.

α.19.29 Onk n$nih God paguatunk otanash mukoshquttaut, God mehquanumau Abraham, kah sohh8waunau Lotuh, wutch noeu kepuhkonittuongunit, ne kepuht[é]adt otanash ne wadohkit Lot.
E.19.29 And it came to pass, when God destroyed the cities of the plain, that God remembered Abraham, and sent Lot out of the midst of the overthrow, when he overthrew the cities in the which Lot dwelt.

α.19.30 Kah Lot sohh[á]m wutch Zoar onk ayeu wàdchuut, kah neswe wutt[à]unoh weeche: newutche wabesu ayin Zoar, kah weetu hassun$nekit nagum kah neswe wuttaunoh.
E.19.30 And Lot went up out of Zoar, and dwelt in the mountain, and his two daughters with him; for he feared to dwell in Zoar: and he dwelt in a cave, he and his two daughters.

α.19.31 Kah mohtomegit unnau weesumussoh K8shun kutchaiyeu8, kah matta woh toh wosketompaun8 yeu ohket kuppetakonukqunnanonut, ne asehettit wame muttaohkéog.
E.19.31 And the firstborn said unto the younger, Our father is old, and there is not a man in the earth to come in unto us after the manner of all the earth:

α.19.32 Hah wuttàttamwéheuntuh K8shin wine, onk woh keneesinan onk woh k8wadchanumauom[ún] 8skanemoneuh K8shin.
E.19.32 Come, let us make our father drink wine, and we will lie with him, that we may preserve seed of our father.

α.19.33 Onk wuttattamweheaog 8shuoh wine ne nohkog, onk mohtomegit petutteau, onk neesin 8shoh, kah matta wahteáu ne seepsuk kah omohkeit.
E.19.33 And they made their father drink wine that night: and the firstborn went in, and lay with her father; and he perceived not when she lay down, nor when she arose.

α.19.34 Onk n$nih nompuhkeit, mohtomegit unnau wesumussoh, kusseh neennup n8sh wanongk8k: wonk wuttattamweheuntuh wine yeu nohkog, kah petutteash, kah neesin onk woh k8wadchanumauómun 8skannemeneuh K8shin
E.19.34 And it came to pass on the morrow, that the firstborn said unto the younger, Behold, I lay yesternight with my father: let us make him drink wine this night also; and go thou in, and lie with him, that we may preserve seed of our father.

α.19.35 Kah wonk 8tattamweheóuh 8sh8oh wine ne nohkog, kah peississit nepau kah wūnesinuh, kah matta wahteau ne seepsuk kah ne omohkeit.
E.19.35 And they made their father drink wine that night also: and the younger arose, and lay with him; and he perceived not when she lay down, nor when she arose.

α.19.36 Nemehkuh neeswe wuttônuh Lot wompequ[a]uog wutche 8sh8oh.
E.19.36 Thus were both the daughters of Lot with child by their father.

α.19.37 Kah mohtomegit wunnaumonieu, kah wuttissowenuh Moab, yeuoh 8sh8oh Moabitog yeu pajeh kesukok.
E.19.37 And the first born bare a son, and called his name Moab: the same is the father of the Moabites unto this day.

α.19.38 Kah wesumussoh wonk wunnaumonieu kah wuttissowenuh Be[n]m[a]mi: yeuoh 8sh8oh wunnechanoh Ammon yeu pajeh kesukok.
E.19.38 And the younger, she also bare a son, and called his name Benammi: the same is the father of the children of Ammon unto this day.

α.20.1 ONK Abraham na 8mun sowanohkomukqut kah wutohtu nashauwe Kadesh kah Shur, kah namshpeyau ut Gerar.
E.20.1 And Abraham journeyed from thence toward the south country, and dwelled between Kadesh and Shur, and sojourned in Gerar.

α.20.2 Kah Abraham n8wau papaume Sarah úmmittumwussoh yeuoh nummissis kah Abimelek ketass8t ut Gerar an8team8 kah wunnemunoh Sarah.
E.20.2 And Abraham said of Sarah his wife, She is my sister: and Abimelech king of Gerar sent, and took Sarah.

α.20.3 Qtu God peyaonau Abimelechuh ut kouénat kah wuttinuh, kusseh ken kenup newutch[e] na mittumwussis neemunadt, newutche noh wussoh.
E.20.3 But God came to Abimelech in a dream by night, and said to him, Behold, thou art but a dead man, for the woman which thou hast taken; for she is a man's wife.

α.20.4 Qut Abimeléch asquam pas8sukauonk & n8wau, Lord, wonk kenéhtoh sampweseae wutohtimoin.
E.20.4 But Abimelech had not come near her: and he said, LORD, wilt thou slay also a righteous nation?

α.20.5 Sunnummatta nuttugk8us yeuoh nummissis & nagum nux nagum nehenwonche n8wop yeuoh nuttonugqus: ut nussampwetea[n]aonganit, & [ma]tta woskehuwomun8ut nunnutcheg y[e]u nutussen.
E.20.5 Said he not unto me, She is my sister? and she, even she herself said, He is my brother: in the integrity of my heart and innocency of my hands have I done this.

α.20.6 Onk God wuttinuh ut kouenat, nux n8wahteoun yeu kutussen k8ssampwet[e]ah[a]onganit, newutche kutchekénu[n]up wutch kummatcheneheneat, newutche matta kitt[in]na numunoh mussin.
E.20.6 And God said unto him in a dream, Yea, I know that thou didst this in the integrity of thy heart; for I also withheld thee from sinning against me: therefore suffered I thee not to touch her.

α.20.7 Kah yeuyeu qushkenumau wosketomp u[m]mittamwussoh, newutche noh Manittowompaenin onk pish kuppeantam wanshhuk, kah pish kuppomant[a]m kah matta qushkenumauoa[d]t, wahteaush pish wunnamuhkut kenup ken kah wame neahtauan.
E.20.7 Now therefore restore the man his wife; for he is a prophet, and he shall pray for thee, and thou shalt live: and if thou restore her not, know thou that thou shalt surely die, thou, and all that are thine.

α.20.8 Newajeh Abimeléch omohku nompoaeu, kah wekomau wame wuttinnumoh, kah yeush kuttw8ongash wuttininnonash wam[u] ut wuttauogk8wóut. onk wosketompaog m8cheke wabesuog.
E.20.8 Therefore Abimelech rose early in the morning, and called all his servants, and told all these things in their ears: and the men were sore afraid.

α.20.9 Neit Abimelech wehkomau Abrahamoh kah wuttinnuh. toh kittinheimûn? kah toh kittinne wuttamhish onk woh kuppaudtah kah nutass8timóonk ummishe matchesenat? kuttinhenneash nish matta woh aséonsh.
E.20.9 Then Abimelech called Abraham, and said unto him, What hast thou done unto us? and what have I offended thee, that thou hast brought on me and on my kingdom a great sin? thou hast done deeds unto me that ought not to be done.

α.20.10 Kah Abimelech unnau Abrahamoh, teaguas kenaum yeu waj ussean?
E.20.10 And Abimelech said unto Abraham, What sawest thou, that thou hast done this thing?

α.20.11 Kah Abraham n8wau, newutche nuttenantamup wunnamuhkut, qushaonk God matta yeu ayeuonganit ohtano, onk woh [n]unnushhukquog newutche nummittumwussoh.
E.20.11 And Abraham said, Because I thought, Surely the fear of God is not in this place; and they will slay me for my wife's sake.

α.20.12 Qut wunnamuhkut noh nummissis, ne wuttónoh n8sh, qut matta wutônuh no-kas, onk n8mittum wussissin.
E.20.12 And yet indeed she is my sister; she is the daughter of my father, but not the daughter of my mother; and she became my wife.

α.20.13 Onk n$nih God ayimungquean nanwúsho[n] wutch weekit n8sh, nuttinóp, yeu k8womoausuonk pish ánhean nish$noh ut uttôh paôog, n8wash papaume neen nunnohtónugqus.
E.20.13 And it came to pass, when God caused me to wander from my father's house, that I said unto her, This is thy kindness which thou shalt shew unto me; at every place whither we shall come, say of me, He is my brother.

α.20.14 Kah Abimelech neemunau shepsoh, kah oxinoh kah wosketompae wuttinnúmoh, kah mittumwussisse wuttinnumoh, kah wuttinnumaunuh Abrahamoh, & ukqushkenumauuh wonk Sarahhoh ummittumwussoh.
E.20.14 And Abimelech took sheep, and oxen, and menservants, and womenservants, and gave them unto Abraham, and restored him Sarah his wife.

α.20.15 Kah Abimelech n8wau kusseh, nutohke ohteau anaquabean, wutohkish uttoh wekeneaman.
E.20.15 And Abimelech said, Behold, my land is before thee: dwell where it pleaseth thee.

α.20.16 Onk Sarah unnau, kusseh nuttinnumau kenohtonugqus nequt muttanonganogkodtash silver: kusseh yeuoh kuttungquequohhou, k8wutche neg weetomukqueaneg, kah wame, yeu unáushkomunàh.
E.20.16 And unto Sarah he said, Behold, I have given thy brother a thousand pieces of silver: behold, he is to thee a covering of the eyes, unto all that are with thee, and with all other: thus she was reproved.

α.20.17 Neit Abraham peantamauau Goduh: onk God neetskeheau Abimelechuh, kah ummittumwussoh, kah mittumwussisse wuttinnúmoh, & neecháog.
E.20.17 So Abraham prayed unto God: and God healed Abimelech, and his wife, and his maidservants; and they bare children.

α.20.18 Newutche God kuppohham wame wuttóontómuk8m8uh ut weekit Abimelech, newutche Sarah ummittumwussoh Abraham
E.20.18 For the LORD had fast closed up all the wombs of the house of Abimelech, because of Sarah Abraham's wife.

α.21.1 ONK Jehovah nátawóhhau Saraihoh ne án8wop, kah Jehovah wuttinhuh Sarahoh ne anomp.
E.21.1 And the LORD visited Sarah as he had said, and the LORD did unto Sarah as he had spoken.

α.21.2 Kah Sarah wompoquau, & neechanishau Abraham wunnaumonuh, ut ukkeechiyeuunneat, ut utt8che neán ukkehtimop God.
E.21.2 For Sarah conceived, and bare Abraham a son in his old age, at the set time of which God had spoken to him.

α.21.3 Onk Abraham wuttussowenuh wunnaumonuh neh neekitteawunche, Sarah neekitteáw[o]nche, Isaak.
E.21.3 And Abraham called the name of his son that was born unto him, whom Sarah bare to him, Isaac.

α.21.4 Onk Abraham quóshquswau wunnaumonuh Isaakoh nishwosuk audtashshikquinápinit, God ne anunn8nop,
E.21.4 And Abraham circumcised his son Isaac being eight days old, as God had commanded him.

α.21.5 Kah Abraham nequt pasuk8e kodtumwohkom neekitteawudt wunnaumonuh Isaakoh.
E.21.5 And Abraham was an hundred years old, when his son Isaac was born unto him.

α.21.6 Onk Sarah n8wau, God nutahánhik, wame n8togig n8weetanum8mukquog.
E.21.6 And Sarah said, God hath made me to laugh, so that all that hear will laugh with me.

α.21.7 Onk n8wau howan woh ánont Abrahamoh, Sarah woh n8s[ó]oh mukiesoh? newutche nunnechanush wunnaumonuh nean kechisuut.
E.21.7 And she said, Who would have said unto Abraham, that Sarah should have given children suck? for I have born him a son in his old age.

α.21.8 Onk mukkies kenuppétu, kah 8cheninnop: & Abraham mishenukissu ne kesukkok Isaak 8chenin[á]t.
E.21.8 And the child grew, and was weaned: and Abraham made a great feast the same day that Isaac was weaned.

α.21.9 Onk Sarah naau wunnaumonuh Hagar Wutegyptianú8 neekiteauompuh Abrahamoh, momontauont.
E.21.9 And Sarah saw the son of Hagar the Egyptian, which she had born unto Abraham, mocking.

α.21.10 Newutche unnau Abrahamoh, pogkes yeuoh missinnóe mittumwussis kah wunnaumonuh, newutche wunnaumonuh yeuoh missinoe mittumwussis, matta pish nómpanunk8 weeche nunnaumonuh, weeche Isaak.
E.21.10 Wherefore she said unto Abraham, Cast out this bondwoman and her son: for the son of this bondwoman shall not be heir with my son, even with Isaac.

α.21.11 Onk yeu 8saume 8tamanatamhukqun ut anaquabit Abraham newutche wunnaumonuh.
E.21.11 And the thing was very grievous in Abraham's sight because of his son.

α.21.12 Onk unnah Go[h] Abrahamoh, ahque 8tamanatamhukqush ut anaquabean newutche wusken, kah newutche kummissinnóe mittumwussis: wame ne an8wadt Sarah n8tamweussish wuttinn8waonk: newutche ut Isaak k8skannémuneog pish henneog.
E.21.12 And God said unto Abraham, Let it not be grievous in thy sight because of the lad, and because of thy bondwoman; in all that Sarah hath said unto thee, hearken unto her voice; for in Isaac shall thy seed be called.

α.21.13 Kah wonk wunnaumonuh missinnomittumwussis pish nutayimau wutohtimoin newutche noh k8skannem.
E.21.13 And also of the son of the bondwoman will I make a nation, because he is thy seed.

α.21.14 Kah Abraham nompoaeu omohku, neemun petukqunnunk, kah wisquad numwohta nuppe, kah wutt[ó]nnumaun Hagaroh, (wunnayéutunon) & wusken, kah moncheaheuh: & monchu, kah nanwushau touohkomukqut Beersheba.
E.21.14 And Abraham rose up early in the morning, and took bread, and a bottle of water, and gave it unto Hagar, putting it on her shoulder, and the child, and sent her away: and she departed, and wandered in the wilderness of Beersheba.

α.21.15 Kah nippe mahtshau wishquadt: onk ponau mukkiesoh agwu poshquodchuut.
E.21.15 And the water was spent in the bottle, and she cast the child under one of the shrubs.

α.21.16 Kah monchu, kah nummatappu uppiuhsukukauou, n[o]asu, woh p[a]udohtamuk, newutche n8wau ahque naumutti wunnupp8onk wusken, kah uppiuhsukukauouh kah wuttauatongqussu kah mau,
E.21.16 And she went, and sat her down over against him a good way off, as it were a bow shot: for she said, Let me not see the death of the child. And she sat over against him, and lift up her voice, and wept.

α.21.17 Kah God n8tam wuttauatonkqussuōk wusken, kah wutangelumoh God wehkomau Hag[à]roh wutche kesukquiug, kah wuttinuh tohspinau Hagar? ahque wabesish, newutche n8tam God wuttauatónkqussuonk wusken uttôh apit.
E.21.17 And God heard the voice of the lad; and the angel of God called to Hagar out of heaven, and said unto her, What aileth thee, Hagar? fear not; for God hath heard the voice of the lad where he is.

α.21.18 Neepaush waapin wusken, kenàmwi[n] kenutcheganit: newutche nutayimau missi wutohtimoin.
E.21.18 Arise, lift up the lad, and hold him in thine hand; for I will make him a great nation.

α.21.19 Kah God w[ô]shwunum wuskesukquash kah naum wutahhamonk, kah monchu, kah numwôhpágunau wishquau nippe, kah wuttattumweheuh wuskenuh.
E.21.19 And God opened her eyes, and she saw a well of water; and she went, and filled the bottle with water, and gave the lad drink.

α.21.20 Kah God weetomau wuskenuh, kah kenuppétu kah weekitam touohkomuk, kah sasompwohtau.
E.21.20 And God was with the lad; and he grew, and dwelt in the wilderness, and became an archer.

α.21.21 Kah ayeu touohkomukqut Haran, kah okasa nemunau mittumwu[s]soh wutch ohkit Egypt.
E.21.21 And he dwelt in the wilderness of Paran: and his mother took him a wife out of the land of Egypt.

α.21.22 Onk n$nih, ne ahquompak Abimelech kah Phikol kehchimugquomp wutayeuteomuh ken8n[à]og Abrahamoh, n8waog, God k8weetomuk nish$noh kutussen.
E.21.22 And it came to pass at that time, that Abimelech and Phichol the chief captain of his host spake unto Abraham, saying, God is with thee in all that thou doest:

α.21.23 Newutche yeuyeu chadchekéemeh yeu nashpeu God, onk matta woh kuppann8wáenéhu, asuh mat nunnàumon, asuh nat nunnaumon wunnaumonuh, netatúpe womoausuonk ne anhen, ne pish kuttinhen & ne ut ohket uttoh anea[u]peyoan.
E.21.23 Now therefore swear unto me here by God that thou wilt not deal falsely with me, nor with my son, nor with my son's son: but according to the kindness that I have done unto thee, thou shalt do unto me, and to the land wherein thou hast sojourned.

α.21.24 Kah Abraham n8wau nutchadchekéyeuam.
E.21.24 And Abraham said, I will swear.

α.21.25 Onk Abraham áushkomau Abimelechuh newutche wuttáhamonk, uttiyeu Abimelech wuttin[u]úmoh chekeeu nemunumohettit.
E.21.25 And Abraham reproved Abimelech because of a well of water, which Abimelech's servants had violently taken away.

α.21.26 Kah Abimelech n8wau, matta n8wá[o]n howan yeu asit, asuh matta kutuss8unah, asuh matta n8tam8unah, qut yeu kesukok.
E.21.26 And Abimelech said, I wot not who hath done this thing; neither didst thou tell me, neither yet heard I of it, but to day.

α.21.27 Kah Abraham neemunau sheepsoh, kah oxenoh, & wuttinnumáuunuh Abimelechuh onk neeswe wunn8wàog.
E.21.27 And Abraham took sheep and oxen, and gave them unto Abimelech; and both of them made a covenant.

α.21.28 Onk Abraham chippúnau nesausuk tahsuoh sqoshimwoh shepwussémesog wutch shepsehtu.
E.21.28 And Abraham set seven ewe lambs of the flock by themselves.

α.21.29 Onk Abimelech unnau Abrahamoh, toh nauwuttam88 yeug nesausuk tahsuog sqoshimwog shipwussémesog neg chaupunàcheg.
E.21.29 And Abimelech said unto Abraham, What mean these seven ewe lambs which thou hast set by themselves?

α.21.30 Onk n8wau, newutche yeug nesausuk tahsuog squoshimwog shepsemesog k8tnôòg nunnutcheganit, neg woh n8wauwaónukquog, yeu nukkuthamunah yeu wuttahamonk.
E.21.30 And he said, For these seven ewe lambs shalt thou take of my hand, that they may be a witness unto me, that I have digged this well.

α.21.31 Newutche wuttehéttamun ne ohke Beersheba: newutche nag neeswe wutchadchekéyeuwónittuog.
E.21.31 Wherefore he called that place Beersheba; because there they sware both of them.

α.21.32 Nemehkuh wunn8waog ut Beersheba neit Abimelech neepau & Phikol kechemugquomp wutayeuwehtéomut, & qushkeog en wutohtuout Philistiansog.
E.21.32 Thus they made a covenant at Beersheba: then Abimelech rose up, and Phichol the chief captain of his host, and they returned into the land of the Philistines.

α.21.33 Onk ohketeau matugquemesash ut Beersheba, kah na$ut wéhquetum 8wesuonk Jehovah micheme pomantamoe Manit.
E.21.33 And Abraham planted a grove in Beersheba, and called there on the name of the LORD, the everlasting God.

α.21.34 Kah Abraham wuttineapeyón wutohtuout Philistins m8chetikqunne.
E.21.34 And Abraham sojourned in the Philistines' land many days.

α.22.1 ONK n$nih, mahche n$nag, God qutcheheau Abrahamoh, onk wuttinuh, Abraham, kah n8wau neen yeu.
E.22.1 And it came to pass after these things, that God did tempt Abraham, and said unto him, Abraham: and he said, Behold, here I am.

α.22.2 Kah n8wau neemun yeuyeu kenaumon kenukquetegheàe Isaak noh womonadt, kah aush ohkit Moriah, kah naut sephaush chikóhsue sephausuonk ut pasuk wadchuut uttiyeu máshamauun.
E.22.2 And he said, Take now thy son, thine only son Isaac, whom thou lovest, and get thee into the land of Moriah; and offer him there for a burnt offering upon one of the mountains which I will tell thee of.

α.22.3 Onk Abraham nompoaeu omohkeu, kah appápuwenehteaú wuttassimoh, onk weechâau neesuo[h] 8skenumoh, kah Isaakoh wunnaumonuh, & papassetaham wuttuhqunash wutche chikohsue sephausuonk, kah neepau kah au ayeuonganit ne anómp God.
E.22.3 And Abraham rose up early in the morning, and saddled his ass, and took two of his young men with him, and Isaac his son, and clave the wood for the burnt offering, and rose up, and went unto the place of which God had told him.

α.22.4 Neit nashikquinukok Abraham spuhquaiau kah naum ayeuonk n8adtut.
E.22.4 Then on the third day Abraham lifted up his eyes, and saw the place afar off.

α.22.5 Kah Abraham unnau 8skenumoh, yeu appek weeche asse, kah neen kah nunkomp y[ó] nuttónan, kah n8wowussumómun, kah wonk hô kuppeyéaunúmun.
E.22.5 And Abraham said unto his young men, Abide ye here with the ass; and I and the lad will go yonder and worship, and come again to you.

α.22.6 Kah Abraham neemunum sephausuwae wuttuhqunash, kah upponamunash Isaakait wunnaumonat, kah neemunum n8teau wunnutcheganit, kah chohquog, kah neeshauog.
E.22.6 And Abraham took the wood of the burnt offering, and laid it upon Isaac his son; and he took the fire in his hand, and a knife; and they went both of them together.

α.22.7 Kah Isaak ken8nau Abrahamoh 8shoh kah n8wau, N8sh, kah n8wau, neen yeu nunnaumon, kah n8wau, kusseh, n8tau, kah wuttuhqunash, qut uttiyeuoh shepsemes, wutch chikohsue sephausuonk;
E.22.7 And Isaac spake unto Abraham his father, and said, My father: and he said, Here am I, my son. And he said, Behold the fire and the wood: but where is the lamb for a burnt offering?

α.22.8 Kah Abraham n8wau[:] nunnaumon, God pish quoshaéiteau wuhhogkuh shepsemésoh wutche chikohtae sephausuonk, kah neeshauog.
E.22.8 And Abraham said, My son, God will provide himself a lamb for a burnt offering: so they went both of them together.

α.22.9 Kah peyaog ayeuonganit ne maṣhamaomp God, kah Abraham na wuttit ayimun Altar, kah wunishitteau wuttuhqunash, kah tahtogkuppunau Isaakoh wunnaumonuh, & upponuh woskeche Altar woskeche wuttuhqunit.
E.22.9 And they came to the place which God had told him of; and Abraham built an altar there, and laid the wood in order, and bound Isaac his son, and laid him on the altar upon the wood.

α.22.10 Kah Abraham summagunum wunnutcheg neemunum chohquog, onk woh nushau wunnaumonuh.
E.22.10 And Abraham stretched forth his hand, and took the knife to slay his son.

α.22.11 Kah wutangelumoh Jehovah 8wekomuh wutch Kesukqut kah n8wau, Abraham Abraham, kah n8wau neen yeu.
E.22.11 And the angel of the LORD called unto him out of heaven, and said, Abraham, Abraham: and he said, Here am I.

α.22.12 Kah n8wau, ahque ponsh kenutcheg nunkompaut, asuh ahque toh$henne, newutche n8wahteoun yeuyeu kukqush God, newutche mutta kukkishpadtamien kenaumon.
E.22.12 And he said, Lay not thine hand upon the lad, neither do thou any thing unto him: for now I know that thou fearest God, seeing thou hast not withheld thy son, thine only son from me.

α.22.13 Kah Abraham spuhquaeu, kah natauwompu, kah kusseh, uppushquanit shepse nomposhim sadtúwunnadchin kuppahtu: kah Abraham naau kah neemunau shepsoh nomposhimwoh, kah wussephâusinuh, wutche ch[i]ohhtae sephausuonk nompu ut wunnaumonuh.
E.22.13 And Abraham lifted up his eyes, and looked, and behold behind him a ram caught in a thicket by his horns: and Abraham went and took the ram, and offered him up for a burnt offering in the stead of his son.

α.22.14 Kah Abraham ne ayeuonk wuttissowetamun, Je[k]ovah$jireh, ne an8womuk ne pajeh yeu kesukok, 8wadchumut Jehovah pish naumun.
E.22.14 And Abraham called the name of that place Jehovahjireh: as it is said to this day, In the mount of the LORD it shall be seen.

α.22.15 Kah wutangelumoh Jehovah weekomau Abrahamoh wutch kesukqut nahoht[ô]eu.
E.22.15 And the angel of the LORD called unto Abraham out of heaven the second time,

α.22.16 Kah n8wau, nashpeu nehenwonche neen nutchadchekeyeuwam, n8wau Jehovah newutche yeu kutussen, kah matta kukkishpadtamieu kenaumon kenukquttegheáe.
E.22.16 And said, By myself have I sworn, saith the LORD, for because thou hast done this thing, and hast not withheld thy son, thine only son:

α.22.17 Wunanitteaon k8nanumoush, Kah m8chekehuwaon numm8chekeh k8skannemeneog, onatuh anogqsog kesukqut, kah onatuh nogayeu keechepam kehtahhennit, kah k8skannemunneog pish ohtóog 8squontam8 ummatwom8oh.
E.22.17 That in blessing I will bless thee, and in multiplying I will multiply thy seed as the stars of the heaven, and as the sand which is upon the sea shore; and thy seed shall possess the gate of his enemies;

α.22.18 Kah ut k8skannemunut wame wutohtimoneash ut ohkit pish wunnanetamunash, newutche kenosweetam nuttiñ8waonk.
E.22.18 And in thy seed shall all the nations of the earth be blessed; because thou hast obeyed my voice.

α.22.19 Neit Abraham qushkeu en 8skenúmut kah neepauog, kah weech[à]ittuog en Beersheba, kah Abraham wutohtu ut Beersheba.
E.22.19 So Abraham returned unto his young men, and they rose up and went together to Beersheba; and Abraham dwelt at Beersheba.

α.22.20 Kah n$nah, mahche n$nag, unnonah Abraham, n8wau, kusseh Milcah nagum wonk neechauau keematoh Nahor.
E.22.20 And it came to pass after these things, that it was told Abraham, saying, Behold, Milcah, she hath also born children unto thy brother Nahor;

α.22.21 Huz mohtommeginitcheh kah Buz weematoh. Kah Kemuel 8shoh Aram,
E.22.21 Huz his firstborn, and Buz his brother, and Kemuel the father of Aram,

α.22.22 kah Chesed, kah Hazo, kah Pildash, kah Jidlaph, kah Bethuel.
E.22.22 And Chesed, and Hazo, and Pildash, and Jidlaph, and Bethuel.

α.22.23 Kah Bethuel wuttoneu Rebeckah: yeuoh shwosuk tahsuoh Milk[œ]h wunnechanshonuh Nahoroh weematah Abraham.
E.22.23 And Bethuel begat Rebekah: these eight Milcah did bear to Nahor, Abraham's brother.

α.22.24 Kah nees8kauonche ussowesu Reumah neechau wonk Teba & Taham & Thahash & Maachah.
E.22.24 And his concubine, whose name was Reumah, she bare also Tebah, and Gaham, and Thahash, and Maachah.

α.23.1 KAH Sarah nequt pasak8we kodtumwohkom, & neesneechag & nesausuk yeush ukkodtum8ash uppomantamôonk Sarah.
E.23.1 And Sarah was an hundred and seven and twenty years old: these were the years of the life of Sarah.

α.23.2 Kah Sarah ut nupp8 ut Kirjatharba, ne Hebron ohkeit Kanaan, kah ummauunnitteaaunshuh.
E.23.2 And Sarah died in Kirjatharba; the same is Hebron in the land of Canaan: and Abraham came to mourn for Sarah, and to weep for her.

α.23.3 Kah Abraham neepau wutch anaquábit wunnup8moh, & ken8nau wunnaumonuh Heth, n8wau.
E.23.3 And Abraham stood up from before his dead, and spake unto the sons of Heth, saying,

α.23.4 Neen nuppenuwohteau, kah nuttinneapeyon weeche kenaau, aninnumaiegk ohtauunat posekinittuae ohke, onk woh nupposekin nunnup8m wutch anaquabeh.
E.23.4 I am a stranger and a sojourner with you: give me a possession of a buryingplace with you, that I may bury my dead out of my sight.

α.23.5 Kah wunnechanoh Heth namp8hamauaog Abrahamoh, wuttinouh.
E.23.5 And the children of Heth answered Abraham, saying unto him,

α.23.6 N8taiinnean nussontimom ken manittoe Sontim k8wutche neenawun, toh weekeneaman n8weenohkeinônit posekin kenup8m: matta hawan neenawun woh k8wohquoantamàuun8mun n8wenohkéinónash wutche ken, qut woh kupposekin kenap8m.
E.23.6 Hear us, my lord: thou art a mighty prince among us: in the choice of our sepulchres bury thy dead; none of us shall withhold from thee his sepulchre, but that thou mayest bury thy dead.

α.23.7 Kah Abraham neepau kah náuaeihtauau missininnuh ne wadohkinutcheh, anaquabhettit wunneechanuh Heth.
E.23.7 And Abraham stood up, and bowed himself to the people of the land, even to the children of Heth.

α.23.8 Kah ukken8nuh nahog, n8wau, unnà[n]tàm[ó]g nuppposekinon nup8m wutch anaquabeh, n8tiegk, kah nanompasittumaiegk Ephron wunnaumonuh Zohar.
E.23.8 And he communed with them, saying, If it be your mind that I should bury my dead out of my sight; hear me, and intreat for me to Ephron the son of Zohar,

α.23.9 Onk woh nuttinumunk wuthassunnegk Màchpelah, ne ohtunk 8quahtikonit, uttoh án8adtik woh n8ch aninumungqun wutch ahtaunat posekinatue ohke.
E.23.9 That he may give me the cave of Machpelah, which he hath, which is in the end of his field; for as much money as it is worth he shall give it me for a possession of a buryingplace amongst you.

α.23.10 Kah Ephron weetomau wunneechanoh Heth: kah Ephron wuthittite namp8hamauau Abrahamoh n8tau[a]hettit wunnech[a]noh Heth, wame neg petuteacheg squoantamut wut8tant, n8wau.
E.23.10 And Ephron dwelt among the children of Heth: and Ephron the Hittite answered Abraham in the audience of the children of Heth, even of all that went in at the gate of his city, saying,

α.23.11 Matta nussontimom, n8tah, kuttinumaúunun ohteuk, kah hassunnegk ne na ohtag kittinnumaúunun, anaquabhettit wunnaumon8h nummissinninnumog kuttinnumauunun, posekin kenup8m.
E.23.11 Nay, my lord, hear me: the field give I thee, and the cave that is therein, I give it thee; in the presence of the sons of my people give I it thee: bury thy dead.

α.23.12 Kah Abraham nauaeu ut anaquabhettit missinninnuog ne wadtohkitcheg.
E.23.12 And Abraham bowed down himself before the people of the land.

α.23.13 Kah ken8nau Ephronuh, n8tamohettit missinninnuog neg na apitcheg, n8wau, qut tapeneaumau k8wehquetumoush n8tah kittinnumaush teauguash wutch ohke, nohtinnumah onk hô na nupposekinnon nupp8m.
E.23.13 And he spake unto Ephron in the audience of the people of the land, saying, But if thou wilt give it, I pray thee, hear me: I will give thee money for the field; take it of me, and I will bury my dead there.

α.23.14 Kah Ephron wunnamp8hamauoh Abrahamoh wuttinuh.
E.23.14 And Ephron answered Abraham, saying unto him,

α.23.15 Nussontimom n8tah, ohke nôadtu yauudt paduk88ash shekelsash Silver, ne ne teaguas ut nashauwe nen kah ken? newutche posekin kenup8m.
E.23.15 My lord, hearken unto me: the land is worth four hundred shekels of silver; what is that betwixt me and thee? bury therefore thy dead.

α.23.16 Kah Abraham 8namptauau Ephronuh, kah Abraham quttahhamauau Ephronuh silver né mashamungqut, n8tamohettit wunnaumonuh Heth, yauut pasuk8oash shekelsash silver wanegegkish ut kenugke kodtauwompasuenuog.
E.23.16 And Abraham hearkened unto Ephron; and Abraham weighed to Ephron the silver, which he had named in the audience of the sons of Heth, four hundred shekels of silver, current money with the merchant.

α.23.17 Kah wutohteuk Ephron ohteuk ut Machpal[a]h anaquohtag Mamre, ohteuk kah h[u]ssunnegk ne na ohtag, & wame matugquash ne ohteakonit, 8taht8onganin.
E.23.17 And the field of Ephron which was in Machpelah, which was before Mamre, the field, and the cave which was therein, and all the trees that were in the field, that were in all the borders round about, were made sure

α.23.18 En Abrahamut wutohthuonk anaquabhettit wunnaumonuh Heth, k8wutche wame petutteacheg 8squoantamut wut8tan.
E.23.18 Unto Abraham for a possession in the presence of the children of Heth, before all that went in at the gate of his city.

α.23.19 Yeu mahche n$nag[?] Abraham posekinau Sarahoh ummittumwussoh ha[ss]unnekit ohteakonit Machpel[e]h anaquohtag Mamre ne Hebron ut ohkit Kanaan.
E.23.19 And after this, Abraham buried Sarah his wife in the cave of the field of Machpelah before Mamre: the same is Hebron in the land of Canaan.

α.23.20 Kah ohteuk kah [h]assunnek ne na ohtag ayimu[n] wunnamuhkut wutohti[n] ut Abrahā wutche ohtauun posekinittuae ohke ut kishke wunnaumomuh Heth.
E.23.20 And the field, and the cave that is therein, were made sure unto Abraham for a possession of a buryingplace by the sons of Heth.

α.24.1 ONK Abraham kutchisu8, kah sepepomantam, kah Jehvoah mahche wunnanumuh Abraham wutch wame teanteaguashinish.
E.24.1 And Abraham was old, and well stricken in age: and the LORD had blessed Abraham in all things.

α.24.2 Kah Abraham unnau masugkenutche wuttinnumoh ut wekit nanawunnumúnit wame ne adtashadch[á]suadt, ponsh k8wehquetumoush kenutcheg agwu neehquaut.
E.24.2 And Abraham said unto his eldest servant of his house, that ruled over all that he had, Put, I pray thee, thy hand under my thigh:

α.24.3 Kah kutchadchekeyeuwahush nashpeu Jehovah Keitannit kesukqut, kah Keihtannit ut muttaohket, onk woh m[a]t keneemunoh ummittamwussoh nunnaumon, wuttâun8[ô]h Kananitog neg weetomukuppanneg.
E.24.3 And I will make thee swear by the LORD, the God of heaven, and the God of the earth, that thou shalt not take a wife unto my son of the daughters of the Canaanites, among whom I dwell:

α.24.4 Qut woh kuttôm nehenwonche nutohket, kah nutti[nón]kumòhtu kah neemun ummittumwussoh nunnaumon Isaak.
E.24.4 But thou shalt go unto my country, and to my kindred, and take a wife unto my son Isaac.

α.24.5 Kah wuttinnúmun wuttinuh, paguodche mittamwossis matta weekontam8h yeu pajeh weechógqunat yeu ohket: neit wonk hô nuppasou kenaumon ohkei[t] ne w[ó]mop.
E.24.5 And the servant said unto him, Peradventure the woman will not be willing to follow me unto this land: must I needs bring thy son again unto the land from whence thou camest?

α.24.6 [Onk] Abraham wuttinuh, ahque pas8 na wonk nunnaumon.
E.24.6 And Abraham said unto him, Beware thou that thou bring not my son thither again.

α.24.7 Jehovah Keihta[nn]it ut kesukqut, noh neemunit wutch weekit n8sh, onk wutch ohkit nuttino[n]kumóut, onk noh kan8shop, kah noh chadchekeimip, n8wau, Yeu kittinnumáunun ohke wutch k8skannemunneut, noh pish an8nau wutangelumoh ut anaquaushaan, kah na pish k8tnon ummittamwussoh nunnaumon.
E.24.7 The LORD God of heaven, which took me from my father's house, and from the land of my kindred, and which spake unto me, and that sware unto me, saying, Unto thy seed will I give this land; he shall send his angel before thee, and thou shalt take a wife unto my son from thence.

α.24.8 Kah mittamwossis matta weekontam8g kutasukongqunat, neit woh kuppahkhit yeu wutch nutchadchekeyeuaonganit, webe ahque pas8 nunnaumon na$ut.
E.24.8 And if the woman will not be willing to follow thee, then thou shalt be clear from this my oath: only bring not my son thither again.
