α.24.9 Kah wutt[i]númun wunnutcheg ponam Abraham wussontimomut agwu weehquaut, kah wutchadchekeimoh papaume nish aunaksh.
E.24.9 And the servant put his hand under the thigh of Abraham his master, and sware to him concerning that matter.

α.24.10 Kah wuttinnúmun neemunau piukqussuoh Kamelsoh, wussontimom Ukkamelsoh, kah monchu (newutche wame ummaumachiash wussontimomuh,[,] wunnutcheganit ohtaash) kah neepau, kah monchu en Mesopotamia wut8tanit Nahor.
E.24.10 And the servant took ten camels of the camels of his master, and departed; for all the goods of his master were in his hand: and he arose, and went to Mesopotamia, unto the city of Nahor.

α.24.11 Kah ukkamelsumoh uppesitúkqussumheuh ut poquadchu 8tanit, kishke wuttahhamonganit, wanonk88k, mittumwussisog ât8chu sohamohettit wutáhapahettit.
E.24.11 And he made his camels to kneel down without the city by a well of water at the time of the evening, even the time that women go out to draw water.

α.24.12 Kah n8wau, Woi Jehovah Ummanitt8moh nussontimom Abraham, k8wehquetumoush aninnumah wunne pomushaonk yeu kesukok, kah womóausuaineh nussontimom Abraham.
E.24.12 And he said O LORD God of my master Abraham, I pray thee, send me good speed this day, and shew kindness unto my master Abraham.

α.24.13 Kusseh, yeu nunneepauun kishke wuttahamong[a]nit, kah wuttâun8oh wosketompaog 8tanit, sohhamóhettit wadhupahettit.
E.24.13 Behold, I stand here by the well of water; and the daughters of the men of the city come out to draw water:

α.24.14 Onk n$nag nunksqua noh woh anog, ponsh kupp8thansh onk woh n8tattam, kah n8wadt, wuttattash, kah wonk n8tattamweh kukkamelsog, n$noh 8wutch ânadcheh kittinnúm Isaak: kah neit woh n8wahteóh k8womausuneheaonk nussontimom.
E.24.14 And let it come to pass, that the damsel to whom I shall say, Let down thy pitcher, I pray thee, that I may drink; and she shall say, Drink, and I will give thy camels drink also: let the same be she that thou hast appointed for thy servant Isaac; and thereby shall I know that thou hast shewed kindness unto my master.

α.24.15 Kah n$nih, asq maht8og, kusseh, Rebeckeh soham noh neeteup ut Bethuel, wunnaumonuh Milchah ummittumwussoh Nahor, weematoh Abraham: upp8thansh ohteau wuttugkeit.
E.24.15 And it came to pass, before he had done speaking, that, behold, Rebekah came out, who was born to Bethuel, son of Milcah, the wife of Nahor, Abraham's brother, with her pitcher upon her shoulder.

α.24.16 Onk nunksquau wunneetu m8cheke móneaúunat penomp matta wosketomp 8waheuh: onk n8keu ut wutta[h]amonganit kah numwôquom upp8thonch8mut, kah kadchu.
E.24.16 And the damsel was very fair to look upon, a virgin, neither had any man known her: and she went down to the well, and filled her pitcher, and came up.

α.24.17 Kah wuttinnúmun quogqueu wunnogskauoh, kah n8wau, Wuttattamwuhhe k8weehquetumoush ohguhsemese nippe ut p8thonch[ú]ut.
E.24.17 And the servant ran to meet her, and said, Let me, I pray thee, drink a little water of thy pitcher.

α.24.18 Kah n8wau wuttattash Nussontimom kah kenuppesen, kah n8kinum upp8thonchu ut wunnutcheganit kah 8tattamehuh.
E.24.18 And she said, Drink, my lord: and she hasted, and let down her pitcher upon her hand, and gave him drink.

α.24.19 Kah mahche wuttattamweheunt, n8wau, kah wonk n8thupau Kukkamelsog, onk mahts[i]pamhettit.
E.24.19 And when she had done giving him drink, she said, I will draw water for thy camels also, until they have done drinking.

α.24.20 Kah ukkénuppeússen, sokunum upp8thansh ut neetasuog 8tattamwaech8wont, kah quogqueu en wutahamonganit wuttóhupau, wutóhupauau wame ukkmelsumoh.
E.24.20 And she hasted, and emptied her pitcher into the trough, and ran again unto the well to draw water, and drew for all his camels.

α.24.21 Kah wosketomp monchantog chequnikompau, uttoh wuttin Jeh[o]vah wunnantamun uppomushaonk asuh matta.
E.24.21 And the man wondering at her held his peace, to wit whether the LORD had made his journey prosperous or not.

α.24.22 Onk n$nih Kamelsog mahche pissumwóhettit, woskeetomp neemunum Golde sogussóhou unatohkéquan paushe shekel, kah neenash kehtiputénapeash wutch wunnutchegash, unatóhkéqunash piukqutash shekelsash gold.
E.24.22 And it came to pass, as the camels had done drinking, that the man took a golden earring of half a shekel weight, and two bracelets for her hands of ten shekels weight of gold;

α.24.23 Kah n8wau howan wuttaunoh ken? missohamah k8wehquetumoush, mohchoi K8sh week toh woh apéog?
E.24.23 And said, Whose daughter art thou? tell me, I pray thee: is there room in thy father's house for us to lodge in?

α.24.24 Kah wuttinuh, neen wuttaunoh Bethuel, wunnaumonuh Milchah nekitteauwómpuh Nahoroh.
E.24.24 And she said unto him, I am the daughter of Bethuel the son of Milcah, which she bare unto Nahor.

α.24.25 Wonk wuttinuh n8wadchanumumun sekupoghungash & weatchiminneash wamut kah toh woh kaemuk.
E.24.25 She said moreover unto him, We have both straw and provender enough, and room to lodge in.

α.24.26 Onk wosketomp nauwaémo uppuhkuk onk wowussumau Jehovah.
E.24.26 And the man bowed down his head, and worshipped the LORD.

α.24.27 Kah n8wau 8nanumunaj Jehovah ummánitt8moh nussontimómoh tohneadt ummonaneteaonk, kah 8nomway[e]uonk pomushàon mayut, Jéhovah nutuss8wúnuk weekit nussontimom waweematutog.
E.24.27 And he said, Blessed be the LORD God of my master Abraham, who hath not left destitute my master of his mercy and his truth: I being in the way, the LORD led me to the house of my master's brethren.

α.24.28 Kah nunksquau monchashau, kah wuttinonash yeushoh neg noh àpitcheg weekit okasoh.
E.24.28 And the damsel ran, and told them of her mother's house these things.

α.24.29 Kah Rebekah wunohtónukqussu, kah ussowenau Laban, kah Laban sohwushau ussishau wosketompaut wutahamonganit.
E.24.29 And Rebekah had a brother, and his name was Laban: and Laban ran out unto the man, unto the well.

α.24.30 Onk n$nih, nag* wussagsóhou, kah kehtúpittenàpeash ut wunnutcheganit ummissisoh, an8wadt, yeu nuttugqun wosketomp, onk peyaónau wosketomp[u]h, kah kusseh, neepau kishke Kamelsut, kishke wutahamonganit.
E.24.30 And it came to pass, when he saw the earring and bracelets upon his sister's hands, and when he heard the words of Rebekah his sister, saying, Thus spake the man unto me; that he came unto the man; and, behold, he stood by the camels at the well.

α.24.31 Kah n8wau, pétutteash ken k8nanumuk Jehovah, tohwutch neepaiyean poquadchit? newutche nummahche quaquashweetam wetu, kah ayeuonk toh aphettit Kamelsog.
E.24.31 And he said, Come in, thou blessed of the LORD; wherefore standest thou without? for I have prepared the house, and room for the camels.

α.24.32 Onk wosketomp petutteau wetuómut, kah ómpineau ukkamelsoh, kah wuttinnumáup sekuppoghungash kah weatchiminneash wutche kamelsog, kah nippe kutchessittauun wussetash, kah wussetoash wosketompaog wechógqutcheh.
E.24.32 And the man came into the house: and he ungirded his camels, and gave straw and provender for the camels, and water to wash his feet, and the men's feet that were with him.

α.24.33 Kah upponamauóoh mechum anaquabenit, n8wau, mátta nummetsúh, onk m[a]hche éyon nuttinshàonk, kah n8wau, keket8kash.
E.24.33 And there was set meat before him to eat: but he said, I will not eat, until I have told mine errand. And he said, Speak on.

α.24.34 Kah n8wau, nen Abraham wuttinnúmoh.
E.24.34 And he said, I am Abraham's servant.

α.24.35 Onk Jehovah misheu wunnanumau nussontimomoh, kah ummishheuh, kah wuttinnúmauh flocksog kah heardsog, silver kah gold, wuttinnúmoh wosketompuh: kah mittumwossissoh, kamelsoh kah assesoh.
E.24.35 And the LORD hath blessed my master greatly; and he is become great: and he hath given him flocks, and herds, and silver, and gold, and menservants, and maidservants, and camels, and asses.

α.24.36 Kah Sarah ummittumwussoh nussontimom 8chekitau[ó]panuh wunnaumonuh nussontimomuh kahchisqo8ut: kah wuttinnumauonash wame wuta[h]toongash.
E.24.36 And Sarah my master's wife bare a son to my master when she was old: and unto him hath he given all that he hath.

α.24.37 Kah nussontimom nutchadchekeyeuwàhuk, n8wau, matta keneemunóh ummittumwussoh nunnaúmon wutaun8oh Kananite[o]g uttiyeu ohke wadohkéomp.
E.24.37 And my master made me swear, saying, Thou shalt not take a wife to my son of the daughters of the Canaanites, in whose land I dwell:

α.24.38 Qut woh kuttôm n8sh weekit, kah nuttinauwomôuhtu, kah neemun ummittumwussoh nunnaumon.
E.24.38 But thou shalt go unto my father's house, and to my kindred, and take a wife unto my son.

α.24.39 Kah nuttinop nussontimom, paguodche mittamwussis matta nutasukunk8.
E.24.39 And I said unto my master, Peradventure the woman will not follow me.

α.24.40 Kah nuttinuk, Jeho[u]ah noh anaquabit nuppomusham, noh pish k8weecháhtinug wutangelsumoh, kah k8[n]teunk kummay, kah pish keneemun ummittumwssuoh nunnaumon wutch nutauwamôtu, kah n8sh wekit. 
E.24.40 And he said unto me, The LORD, before whom I walk, will send his angel with thee, and prosper thy way; and thou shalt take a wife for my son of my kindred, and of my father's house:

α.24.41 Neit pish kuppahkeh kuhhog wutch nutchadchekeyeuwaonk peyôan nutauwamóhtu, kah mat eninnumungk8an, pish kuppahke kuhhog wutche nutchadchekeyeuwaonganit.
E.24.41 Then shalt thou be clear from this my oath, when thou comest to my kindred; and if they give not thee one, thou shalt be clear from my oath.

α.24.42 Kah nuppeyam yeu kesukok wutahamonganit, kah nussip, woi Jehovah um-manitt8moh nussontimom Abraham, wunnehteauan nummay uttôh àyoi.
E.24.42 And I came this day unto the well, and said, O LORD God of my master Abraham, if now thou do prosper my way which I go:

α.24.43 Kusseh nunneepóh kishke wutahamonganit, kah woh n$nih, nunksqua paont wuttúhhupau, kah unog, aninnumah k8wehquetumoush nippemes wutch kupp8th[o]nchúut, woh n8tattam.
E.24.43 Behold, I stand by the well of water; and it shall come to pass, that when the virgin cometh forth to draw water, and I say to her, Give me, I pray thee, a little water of thy pitcher to drink;

α.24.44 Onk unugquéan, wuttattash ken, kah wonk n8thupau kukkamelsog: n$noh 8wutch ne[h] Jehovah an8wóhpah wunnaumonuh nussontimom.
E.24.44 And she say to me, Both drink thou, and I will also draw for thy camels: let the same be the woman whom the LORD hath appointed out for my master's son.

α.24.45 Kah asq maht8aon ut nuttàhut, kusseh, Rebekah sohham kah uppothonchúm wuttogkit ohteau, kah w[ô]msu en wutahamonganit, kah wuttuhhuppau, kah nuttinôp wuttattam[ó]heh k8wehquetumoush.
E.24.45 And before I had done speaking in mine heart, behold, Rebekah came forth with her pitcher on her shoulder; and she went down unto the well, and drew water: and I said unto her, Let me drink, I pray thee.

α.24.46 Kah ukkenuppesen, kah unn8kinumun upp8thonchúm wutch wuhhogkat, kah n8wau, wuttattash, kah wonk n8tattamweh kukkamelsog, kah n8t[a]ttamup kah wonk wuttattamweheau kamelsoh.
E.24.46 And she made haste, and let down her pitcher from her shoulder, and said, Drink, and I will give thy camels drink also: so I drank, and she made the camels drink also.

α.24.47 Kah nunnat8tom[a]u[o]p, kah nussip howan wuttaunoh ken? kah n8wau wuttaunoh Bethuel, wunnaumonuh Nahor, noh Milchah nekitteauompuh: Kah nupponumau sogkuss[o]hou wuskesukqut kah keteuputenàp[e]ash ut wunnutcheganit.
E.24.47 And I asked her, and said, Whose daughter art thou? And she said, the daughter of Bethuel, Nahor's son, whom Milcah bare unto him: and I put the earring upon her face, and the bracelets upon her hands.

α.24.48 Kah nunn[a]aunum nuppuhkuk, kah n8wowussumup Jehovah, kah nuttabuttantamau God ummanitt8moh nussontimom Abraham, noh pas8gk8h en sampwe mayut neemunon nussontimom weematoh wuttaunoh wutch wunnaumonuh.
E.24.48 And I bowed down my head, and worshipped the LORD, and blessed the LORD God of my master Abraham, which had led me in the right way to take my master's brother's daughter unto his son.

α.24.49 Onk yeuyeu, womonetuáeu unnehheòg, kah sampwe[n]eheog, nussontimom, ussegq, asuh matta, ussegq, onk woh nukqushkem menadchéanit assuh nuttinohkôunit.
E.24.49 And now if ye will deal kindly and truly with my master, tell me: and if not, tell me; that I may turn to the right hand, or to the left.

α.24.50 Neit Laban kah Bethuel wunnamp8hamauoh, kah n8waog: yeu 8m88 Jehovah$ut, matta woh kittinninn8mun màchuk asuh wunnegik.
E.24.50 Then Laban and Bethuel answered and said, The thing proceedeth from the LORD: we cannot speak unto thee bad or good.

α.24.51 Kusseh Rebekah ut anaquabean, neemun, kah monchish, kah kussontimom wunnaumonuh ummittumwossisitch, nean8wop Jehovah.
E.24.51 Behold, Rebekah is before thee, take her, and go, and let her be thy master's son's wife, as the LORD hath spoken.

α.24.52 Onk n$nih Abraham wuttinnúmoh n8tog ukkuttw8ongash woussumau Jehovah en ohkeau.
E.24.52 And it came to pass, that, when Abraham's servant heard their words, he worshipped the LORD, bowing himself to the earth.

α.24.53 Onk wuttinnúmun sohwhunum nompakouunash silver, nompakouunash gold kah hogk8wongash, kah wuttinnumaunash Rebekah: kah aninnumauau wunohtonugqussoh, kah okasoh waanegugish.
E.24.53 And the servant brought forth jewels of silver, and jewels of gold, and raiment, and gave them to Rebekah: he gave also to her brother and to her mother precious things.

α.24.54 Kah nag meetsuog, kah wuttattamwog, nagum, kah wosketompuh neh weetomukqutcheh, kah 8wampanohkon, kah omohkéog mohtompog, kah n8wau, monche[à]heh en nussontimomut.
E.24.54 And they did eat and drink, he and the men that were with him, and tarried all night; and they rose up in the morning, and he said, Send me away unto my master.

α.24.55 Kah wunohtónugqussoh kah okasoh n8w[à]og, nunksqua n8wetómukqunan ogguhse quinne yean piukkukquinne, mahche ne nag pish monchu.
E.24.55 And her brother and her mother said, Let the damsel abide with us a few days, at the least ten; after that she shall go.

α.24.56 Kah wuttinuh nahog, ahque wuttamhegq, Jehovah wunnehteunk nummay, moncheahegq onk woh nuttom nussontimomut,
E.24.56 And he said unto them, Hinder me not, seeing the LORD hath prospered my way; send me away that I may go to my master.

α.24.57 Onk n8waog, nowehkomómun nunksquau, onk nat8tomauóun ut wutt8nut.
E.24.57 And they said, We will call the damsel, and enquire at her mouth.

α.24.58 Kah weekomáog Rebekah, kah wuttinouh, yeuoh woh k8wechau wosketomp? kah n8wau, n8weechau:
E.24.58 And they called Rebekah, and said unto her, Wilt thou go with this man? And she said, I will go.

α.24.59 Onk wuttinánumóuh monchek Rebekah ummisses8oh, kah nonomukqutche kah wuttinnúmoh Abraham kah 8wosketompomoh.
E.24.59 And they sent away Rebekah their sister, and her nurse, and Abraham's servant, and his men.

α.24.60 Onk wunnanumáog Rebekah, kah wuttinóuh ken nummissesin, ken muttanonganúush piukque muttanonganog kussuog, kah k8skannemuneog ahtauhettich 8squoantam8ash nag sekeneauóncheg.
E.24.60 And they blessed Rebekah, and said unto her, Thou art our sister, be thou the mother of thousands of millions, and let thy seed possess the gate of those which hate them.

α.24.61 Kah Rebekah neepau, kah wunnunksquomoh, kah nai8mukquog kamelsoh, kah asukauóog wosketompuh: kah wuttinnúmun, neemunau Rebekah kah monchu.
E.24.61 And Rebekah arose, and her damsels, and they rode upon the camels, and followed the man: and the servant took Rebekah, and went his way.

α.24.62 Kah Isaak om mayut wutahamonganit Lahairoi, newutche wutohtu sowan ohkit.
E.24.62 And Isaac came from the way of the well Lahairoi; for he dwelt in the south country.

α.24.63 Onk Isaak sohham en ohteakonit wunnonkquáe natwontame peantamunat, kah aspuhquait, naau, kah kusseh kamelsoh pey[á]og.
E.24.63 And Isaac went out to meditate in the field at the eventide: and he lifted up his eyes, and saw, and, behold, the camels were coming.

α.24.64 Kah Rebekah spuhqu[a]eu, kah nauont Isaakoh, n8keu wutch kamelsut.
E.24.64 And Rebekah lifted up her eyes, and when she saw Isaac, she lighted off the camel.

α.24.65 Newutche unnop wuttinnúmu[nu]h, howan yeuoh wosketomp pamushadt ohteakonit kenogskunkqun? onk wuttinnúmun n8wau nussontimom, newutche neemunoh yán[e]qu[o]h[h8], weyánequawhun.
E.24.65 For she had said unto the servant, What man is this that walketh in the field to meet us? And the servant had said, It is my master: therefore she took a vail, and covered herself.

α.24.66 Kah wuttinnumun wuttinnon Isaakuh wame ne asit.
E.24.66 And the servant told Isaac all things that he had done.

α.24.67 Onk Isaak uppas8oh okasa Sarahoh wekit, kah nemunnau Rebekah kah 8mittumwussissinneuh, kah 8womonuh: onk Isaak wekontamwaheau mahche nupinit okasa.
E.24.67 And Isaac brought her into his mother Sarah's tent, and took Rebekah, and she became his wife; and he loved her: and Isaac was comforted after his mother's death.

α.25.1 NEit wonk Abraham ummittumwussu, kah ussowesu Ketura.
E.25.1 Then again Abraham took a wife, and her name was Keturah.

α.25.2 Kah wunnekitteunkquoh Zimram, kah Jokshan, kah Medan, kah Midian, kah Ishbak, kah Shuah.
E.25.2 And she bare him Zimran, and Jokshan, and Medan, and Midian, and Ishbak, and Shuah.

α.25.3 Kah Jokshan wunnaumonaeu Sheba kah Dedan, kah wunnaumonuh Dedan Ashurun, kah Letushim, kah Leumim.
E.25.3 And Jokshan begat Sheba, and Dedan. And the sons of Dedan were Asshurim, and Letushim, and Leummim.

α.25.4 Kah wunnaumonuh Midiah, Epha, kah Epher, kah Hanoch, kah Abida, kah Eldaah, wame yeuh wunneechanoh Ketura.
E.25.4 And the sons of Midian; Ephah, and Epher, and Hanoch, and Abidah, and Eldaah. All these were the children of Keturah.

α.25.5 Onk Abraham aninnumauau wame wutahtuonk Isaakuh.
E.25.5 And Abraham gave all that he had unto Isaac.

α.25.6 Qut wunnaumonáuh 8wisquinneunk wutch Abraham, Abraham wuttinnumauh aninnumoadtuongash, kah ummoncheàheuh en wutchepwoou, wutch Isaak wunnaumonat (as pomantog) en wutchepwoóhket.
E.25.6 But unto the sons of the concubines, which Abraham had, Abraham gave gifts, and sent them away from Isaac his son, while he yet lived, eastward, unto the east country.

α.25.7 Kah yeush ukkesukodtumash kodtumoàsh Abraham uppomantamóonk ne pamontog, nequt pasuk8we kodtumo, kah nesausuk tahshinchag kodtumo, kah nabo napanna tahshit kodtumwae. 
E.25.7 And these are the days of the years of Abraham's life which he lived, an hundred threescore and fifteen years.

α.25.8 Neit Abraham nashauwonau wunnashauanitt8moh, kah nupp8 ut wunne kutchisúunneat mahtauntam, kah sepepomantam, kah mukinàu en ummissinninnúmehtu.
E.25.8 Then Abraham gave up the ghost, and died in a good old age, an old man, and full of years; and was gathered to his people.

α.25.9 Kah wunnaumonuh Isa[a]k kah Ishmael nag upposekinóuh, ut hassunnekit Machpelah, wutohteakonit Ephron wunnaumonuh Zohar wuttahittit, anaquohtag Mamre.
E.25.9 And his sons Isaac and Ishmael buried him in the cave of Machpelah, in the field of Ephron the son of Zohar the Hittite, which is before Mamre;

α.25.10 Ne ohteuk âdt omop Abraham wunnaumonuh Heth, na Abraham posakinon, kah Sarah ummittumwussoh.
E.25.10 The field which Abraham purchased of the sons of Heth: there was Abraham buried, and Sarah his wife.

α.25.11 Onk n$nih mahche nupuk Abraham, God wunnanumau wunnaumonuh Isaak, kah Isaak wutohtu kishke wutahamonganit Lahairoi.
E.25.11 And it came to pass after the death of Abraham, that God blessed his son Isaac; and Isaac dwelt by the well Lahairoi.

α.25.12 Kah yeush wutontseongash Ishmael wunnaumonuh Abraham, noh Hagar wut-egyptian, ummaidumoh Sarah neechauompuh Abrahamoh.
E.25.12 Now these are the generations of Ishmael, Abraham's son, whom Hagar the Egyptian, Sarah's handmaid, bare unto Abraham:

α.25.13 Kah yeush 8wesuongash wunnaumonuh Ishmael nashpeu 8wesuongan88ash, neyaunag uppometeuonganú8ash, mohtomekheonche Ishmael, Nebajoth, kah K[e]dar, kah Adbeel, kah Mibsam[.]
E.25.13 And these are the names of the sons of Ishmael, by their names, according to their generations: the firstborn of Ishmael, Nebajoth; and Kedar, and Adbeel, and Mibsam,

α.25.14 Kah Mishma, kah Dumah, kah Massa.
E.25.14 And Mishma, and Dumah, and Massa,

α.25.15 H[á]dar kah Tema, Jetur, kah Naphish, kah Kedemah[.]
E.25.15 Hadar, and Tema, Jetur, Naphish, and Kedemah:

α.25.16 Yeuh wunnaumonuh Ishmael kah yeush wuttissow[e]suongan88ash, neyaunag wut8tenáoash kah 8wonkon8sin88ash: nabo neesuog sontimóog, neyaunag wutohtimôn8woash.
E.25.16 These are the sons of Ishmael, and these are their names, by their towns, and by their castles; twelve princes according to their nations.

α.25.17 Kah yeush kodtum8ash uppomantamóonk Ishmael, nequt pasuk8e kodtumo, shwinchag kodtumo, kah nesausuk tashit kodtumwae, kah nashauwoneau wunnashauanitt8moh, kah nupp8, kah mukinau en ummissinninnúmehtu.
E.25.17 And these are the years of the life of Ishmael, an hundred and thirty and seven years: and he gave up the ghost and died; and was gathered unto his people.

α.25.18 Onk wutohtuog wutch Havilah onk yean Shur, ne ohteau anaquohtag Egypt, nogquein Assyria: kah nupp8 anaquabenit weematoh.
E.25.18 And they dwelt from Havilah unto Shur, that is before Egypt, as thou goest toward Assyria: and he died in the presence of all his brethren.

α.25.19 Kah yeush wutontseongash Isaak, wunnaumonuh Abraham, Abraham wunnaumoneau Isa[a]k.
E.25.19 And these are the generations of Isaac, Abraham's son: Abraham begat Isaac:

α.25.20 Kah Isaak yauunchage kodtumwohkom womittumwussissit Rebekah wuttaunoh Bethuel wussyrian, Uppadan-Aram, ummississoh Laban Wussyrian.
E.25.20 And Isaac was forty years old when he took Rebekah to wife, the daughter of Bethuel the Syrian of Padanaram, the sister to Laban the Syrian.

α.25.21 Onk Isaak wehquetumauau Jehovah wutche ummittumwussoh, newutche mehchéyeu, onk Jehovah ukkittumonkutaúoh, kah Rebekah ne ummittumwussoh wompoquauoh.
E.25.21 And Isaac intreated the LORD for his wife, because she was barren: and the LORD was intreated of him, and Rebekah his wife conceived.

α.25.22 Kah mukkiésog wogkóuineánittuog ut wuttinnomhogkat, kah n8wau, wunnamuhkut n$nag, tohwutc yeu spinai? onk monchu onk woh nat8tomauau Jehovah.
E.25.22 And the children struggled together within her; and she said, If it be so, why am I thus? And she went to enquire of the LORD.

α.25.23 Kah Jehovah wuttinuh: neesinash wutohtimóineash ohtáash ut kutôontómukkomut: kah neese chippissuog missinninnúog pish chippeog wutch kenogkus[s]it: kah nequt chippissuog missinninnúog pish wutanuwunuhkésumóuh onkatoge missinninnúh, kah masugkenuk pish 8tinnúmuneu[h] peississit.
E.25.23 And the LORD said unto her, Two nations are in thy womb, and two manner of people shall be separated from thy bowels; and the one people shall be stronger than the other people; and the elder shall serve the younger.

α.25.24 Onk mahche tahshikquinógoh ne woh adt nee[c]hadt, kusseh ogquo[h]s[ú]8og ut wutôontómukkomut. 
E.25.24 And when her days to be delivered were fulfilled, behold, there were twins in her womb.

α.25.25 Kah negonnu sohhog musquesu, wame ut woskeche, onatuh mashquoshiàmuk, kah wuttissowenuh Esau.
E.25.25 And the first came out red, all over like an hairy garment; and they called his name Esau.

α.25.26 Kah mahche n$nag weematoh sohweeoh, kah wunnutcheg kogk[ô]unum Esau wogqu[an] kah 8wesuonk hettamun Jakob, kah Isaak nequtta tohshinchage kodtumwohkom nekitteaùut.
E.25.26 And after that came his brother out, and his hand took hold on Esau's heel; and his name was called Jacob: and Isaac was threescore years old when she bare them.

α.25.27 Onk mukitchogqussuog kenuppétuog, kah Esau [àn]adchau wosketomp ut ohteakonit: onk Jakob unninnanum8, apeu weetuómut.
E.25.27 And the boys grew: and Esau was a cunning hunter, a man of the field; and Jacob was a plain man, dwelling in tents.

α.25.28 Kah Isaak wómoneau Esauoh, newutch meechwoh 8weyausum, qut Rebekah womonau Jakoboh.
E.25.28 And Isaac loved Esau, because he did eat of his venison: but Rebekah loved Jacob.

α.25.29 Kah Jakob neepatau sôbàhég: kah Esau 8m ohteakonit kah sauunum.
E.25.29 And Jacob sod pottage: and Esau came from the field, and he was faint:

α.25.30 Kah Esau unnau Jakoboh, ne moshqu[a]g unnanumeh quompatash ne moshquag k8wehquetumoush newutche nussauunum newadche hennit Edom.
E.25.30 And Esau said to Jacob, Feed me, I pray thee, with that same red pottage; for I am faint: therefore was his name called Edom.

α.25.31 Kah Jakob n8wau, eyeu kesukok enninnumah kummohtomegitteàowonk.
E.25.31 And Jacob said, Sell me this day thy birthright.

α.25.32 Kah Esau n8wau, kusseh neen nahen n$nup, kah toh woh nuttin wunnenéhukqun yeu mohtommégitteaeuwonk?
E.25.32 And Esau said, Behold, I am at the point to die: and what profit shall this birthright do to me?

α.25.33 Kah Jakob n8wau, chadchekeimeh yeu kesukok, kah wutchadchekéimuh, káh aninumauau ummohtommégittauoonk Jakoboh.
E.25.33 And Jacob said, Swear to me this day; and he sware unto him: and he sold his birthright unto Jacob.

α.25.34 Neit Jakob assamau Esauoh petukqunneg, kah sabaheg tuttuppuhquamash, kah meetsu, kah wuttattam, kah neepau, kah monchu kah Esau umishanóntamuh ummohtommegittauoonk.
E.25.34 Then Jacob gave Esau bread and pottage of lentiles; and he did eat and drink, and rose up, and went his way: thus Esau despised his birthright.

α.26.1 ONk mo mahshagquodt ohkit, matta negonne mahshogquodt ut ukkesukodtumut Abraham qut onkatuk, kah Isaak au Abimelekait ketass8timwe Philisti[m]s, ut Gerar.
E.26.1 And there was a famine in the land, beside the first famine that was in the days of Abraham. And Isaac went unto Abimelech king of the Philistines unto Gerar.

α.26.2 Kah Jehovah wunnaéihtauoh, kah n8wau, ahque w8msish en Egypt, wutohkish en ohkit uttiyeu ànon.
E.26.2 And the LORD appeared unto him, and said, Go not down into Egypt; dwell in the land which I shall tell thee of:

α.26.3 Enneápeyaush yeu ohke, kah k8weetomush, kah k8nanumush, newutche kittinnumàunash ken & k8skannémunneog wame yeush ohkeash, kah nutussen chadchekéimaonk ne chadchekéimogkup Abraham k8sh.
E.26.3 Sojourn in this land, and I will be with thee, and will bless thee; for unto thee, and unto thy seed, I will give all these countries, and I will perform the oath which I sware unto Abraham thy father;

α.26.4 Kah k8skannemuneog nummuttaanhéaog onatuh anogqsog kesukqut, kah nuttinnumau k8skannémuneog wame yeush ohkeash: kah wame wutohtim[ó]neash pish wunnàntamunash ut k8skannemuneut.
E.26.4 And I will make thy seed to multiply as the stars of heaven, and will give unto thy seed all these countries; and in thy seed shall all the nations of the earth be blessed;

α.26.5 Newutche Abraham noswetamup n8wadtauatonkqussuonk kah nanahteaop nummeechuméhteaonk, nuttinn8waongash, nukkúhk8waongash, kah nuttinnaumatuongash.
E.26.5 Because that Abraham obeyed my voice, and kept my charge, my commandments, my statutes, and my laws.

α.26.6 Kah Isaak wutohtu Gerar.
E.26.6 And Isaac dwelt in Gerar:

α.26.7 Onk neg nah wodohkitcheg wunnat8tomauôuh papaume ummittumwussoh, kah n8wau yeuoh nummissisis: newutche wabesu n8wadt yeuoh nummittumwoh, ishkont neg ne wodohkitcheg nunnushhukquog wutche Rebekah, newutche noh wunneetu en moneauwóneat.
E.26.7 And the men of the place asked him of his wife; and he said, She is my sister: for he feared to say, She is my wife; lest, said he, the men of the place should kill me for Rebekah; because she was fair to look upon.

α.26.8 Onk n$nih noh sepohteadt: Abimelek ketass8t Philistims sonk8hquaeu wutch k[e]nogkenéganit kah naau, kah kusseh, Isaak pompuog Rebekahoh ummittamwussoh.
E.26.8 And it came to pass, when he had been there a long time, that Abimelech king of the Philistines looked out at a window, and saw, and, behold, Isaac was sporting with Rebekah his wife.

α.26.9 Onk Abimelek ken8nau Isaakoh, kah n8wau; kusseh, wunnamuhkut noh kummittamwus onk toh k8che n8wam, yeuoh nummissis? kah Isaak wuttinuh, newutche nussip, ishkont nunnup newutche nagum.
E.26.9 And Abimelech called Isaac, and said, Behold, of a surety she is thy wife; and how saidst thou, She is my sister? And Isaac said unto him, Because I said, Lest I die for her.

α.26.10 Kah Abimelek teaguas yeu anéhog? paguodcheh woh howan wunneesinuh kummittumwussoh, onk woh kenogskunk8wahukqun matcheseonk.
E.26.10 And Abimelech said, What is this thou hast done unto us? one of the people might lightly have lien with thy wife, and thou shouldest have brought guiltiness upon us.

α.26.11 Onk Abimelek meechumehkónau wame ummissinninnúmoh, n8wau, howan noh masunónt yeu wosketomp asuh ummittumwussoh, pish nushau.
E.26.11 And Abimelech charged all his people, saying, He that toucheth this man or his wife shall surely be put to death.

α.26.12 Neit Isaak ohkehteau ne ut ohkit, kah attamunnum ne kodtumuk nequt pasúk8e tahskéganit, kah Jehovah 8nanumúh.
E.26.12 Then Isaac sowed in that land, and received in the same year an hundredfold: and the LORD blessed him.

α.26.13 Onk wosketomp nano missugken, onk nano monchu, onk nano monat, onk yean masugkenuk.
E.26.13 And the man waxed great, and went forward, and grew until he became very great:

α.26.14 Newutche wadchanau flocksog kah hersog, kah monàoh wuttinnúmoh, kah Philistiansog wutiskôunóuh.
E.26.14 For he had possession of flocks, and possession of herds, and great store of servants: and the Philistines envied him.

α.26.15 Newutche wame wutahamongash 8shoh wuttinnumoh 8wónuhkonápash pomantog Abraham 8shoh, Philistiansog ukkuphamunáash, kah wunnumwohtinau ohke.
E.26.15 For all the wells which his father's servants had digged in the days of Abraham his father, the Philistines had stopped them, and filled them with earth.

α.26.16 Onk Abimelek unnau Isaakoh, nukâsinan, newutche m8cheke ken kummissugken onk neenawun. 
E.26.16 And Abimelech said unto Isaac, Go from us; for thou art much mightier than we.

α.26.17 Onk Isaak na 8mun, kah ut weekiteau 8nâúkôanout Geràr, kah na 8tohkin.
E.26.17 And Isaac departed thence, and pitched his tent in the valley of Gerar, and dwelt there.

α.26.18 Kah Isaak qushkeit, kut[á]ham wutahamongash nish kodhamukupash pomantog Abrahamoh 8shoh, newutche Philistiansog ukkuphamonaoash mahche nukup Abraham, kah wuttissowetamunash, 8shoh ne âs8wétogkup.
E.26.18 And Isaac digged again the wells of water, which they had digged in the days of Abraham his father; for the Philistines had stopped them after the death of Abraham: and he called their names after the names by which his father had called them.

α.26.19 Kah wuttinnúmoh Isaak wônéteaog 8neuhkôi, kah na wunnampteauunneau tohkékomue wutahamonk.
E.26.19 And Isaac's servants digged in the valley, and found there a well of springing water.

α.26.20 Kah assamoncheg netasu wutch Gerar kéketehtôadtuog Isaak assamónutcheh wunnetasúmoh, n8waog, nippe nutaihen, kah wuttissowetamun wutahamonk Ezek, newutche uppenuanumóuh.
E.26.20 And the herdmen of Gerar did strive with Isaac's herdmen, saying, The water is ours: and he called the name of the well Esek; because they strove with him.

α.26.21 Kah ketahamwog onkatuk wutahamonk, kah ne wutch wonk penuanumóneau, kah wuttiss[ô]wetamun Sitnah.
E.26.21 And they digged another well, and strove for that also: and he called the name of it Sitnah.

α.26.22 Kah na 8ch ont8tan, kah kutaham onkatuk wutahamonk kah ne mat penuanuttinneau, kah wuttissowetamun Rehoboth: kah n8wau newutche yeuyeu God kutayimungqun wamut appuonk, kah pish kummishummeechumimun yeu ohkit.
E.26.22 And he removed from thence, and digged another well; and for that they strove not: and he called the name of it Rehoboth; and he said, For now the LORD hath made room for us, and we shall be fruitful in the land.

α.26.23 Onk na 8mun en Beersheba.
E.26.23 And he went up from thence to Beersheba.

α.26.24 Kah Jehovah wunnaéihtau ne nohkog kah n8wau, neen ummanitt8moh k8sh Abraham, ahque wabesish, newutche k8wetomsh, kah k8nanumush, kah kumm8chekéhtaush k8skannemuneog, newutche Abraham nuttinnúm.
E.26.24 And the LORD appeared unto him the same night, and said, I am the God of Abraham thy father: fear not, for I am with thee, and will bless thee, and multiply thy seed for my servant Abraham's sake.

α.26.25 Onk na wuttit ayimun Altar, kah wéhquetum 8wesuonk Jehovah, kah na 8weekin, kah na$ut wuttinnúmoh Isaak kutahamwoh wutahamonk.
E.26.25 And he builded an altar there, and called upon the name of the LORD, and pitched his tent there: and there Isaac's servants digged a well.

α.26.26 Kah Abimelech n[â]sukauau wutch Gerar, kah Ahuzzath pasuk 8weetatteamungoh, kah Phikol missugkenomp ut wutayeuwohteamut.
E.26.26 Then Abimelech went to him from Gerar, and Ahuzzath one of his friends, and Phichol the chief captain of his army.

α.26.27 Kah Isaak wuttinuh nahog, tohwutch peyaaúseóg kenaau, kah sekeneauweyóg, kah kutam[a]nimwop?
E.26.27 And Isaac said unto them, Wherefore come ye to me, seeing ye hate me, and have sent me away from you?

α.26.28 Kah n8waog, naumunnan wunnamuhkut Jehovah k8wetomuk, kah nussimun yeuyeu chadchekeittitteuh neenáwun kah ken, kah togkodtamuttúh wunn8waonk.
E.26.28 And they said, We saw certainly that the LORD was with thee: and we said, Let there be now an oath betwixt us, even betwixt us and thee, and let us make a covenant with thee;

α.26.29 Onk woh mat kummatcheneheúmun, neyane mat kummussúnunnómunnónup, kah [neyane] wanne teág nummatchteoh, webe k8nenéhennumun, kah k8nohteae moncheahennumunnônup: ken yeuyeu k8nanumuk Jehovah. 
E.26.29 That thou wilt do us no hurt, as we have not touched thee, and as we have done unto thee nothing but good, and have sent thee away in peace: thou art now the blessed of the LORD.

α.26.30 Onk ummishadtupheuh, kah nag meetsuog, kah wuttattamwog.
E.26.30 And he made them a feast, and they did eat and drink.

α.26.31 Kah nompoaeu omohkeog, kah chadchekeittúog, kah Isaak ummoncheahuk, & wunnohteae wunnukonóuh.
E.26.31 And they rose up betimes in the morning, and sware one to another: and Isaac sent them away, and they departed from him in peace.

α.26.32 Kah n$nih ne kesukok Isaak wuttinnúmoh peyâoh, kah wuttugquoh, papaume wutahamonk ne kodhamohetteup, kah wuttinóuh nummiskomumun nippe.
E.26.32 And it came to pass the same day, that Isaac's servants came, and told him concerning the well which they had digged, and said unto him, We have found water.

α.26.33 Kah wutissowetamun Sheba, newajeh hettamuk Keihtotan Beersheba pajeh yeu kesukok.
E.26.33 And he called it Shebah: therefore the name of the city is Beersheba unto this day.

α.26.34 Kah Esau yauunchage kodtumwohkom wamittumwussissit Judith wuttaunoh Beeri Wuthittite, kah Bashemath wuttaunoh Elon Wuthittite.
E.26.34 And Esau was forty years old when he took to wife Judith the daughter of Beeri the Hittite, and Bashemath the daughter of Elon the Hittite:

α.26.35 Yeug 8wesogitteahaongan8 Isaak kah Rebeckah.
E.26.35 Which were a grief of mind unto Isaac and to Rebekah.

α.27.1 ONk n$nih Isaak kohchisu8ut, kah yaném8uk wuskesukquash, woh mat naum8, kah weekomau Esauoh mohtomegheoncheh, kah wuttinuh, Nunnaumon, kah wuttinuh, kusseh neen yeu.
E.27.1 And it came to pass, that when Isaac was old, and his eyes were dim, so that he could not see, he called Esau his eldest son, and said unto him, My son: and he said unto him, Behold, here am I.

α.27.2 Kah n8wau, kusseh yeuyeu nukkechisu, matta n8wahteoh utti$yeu kesukod adt nupp8.
E.27.2 And he said, Behold now, I am old, I know not the day of my death:

α.27.3 Kah yeuyeu neemunush, k8wehquetumoush, kutauwohteongash, kuppetan, & kutahtomp, kah sohhash en ohteakonit, kah ahchuteah weyaús.
E.27.3 Now therefore take, I pray thee, thy weapons, thy quiver and thy bow, and go out to the field, and take me some venison;

α.27.4 Kah ayimah weekummeechum, neyane womantam, kah paudtah, onk woh nummeechun, onk woh nukketeahogkou k8nanumuk ash nanupp8omp.
E.27.4 And make me savoury meat, such as I love, and bring it to me, that I may eat; that my soul may bless thee before I die.

α.27.5 Onk Rebekah n8tam Isaak kôn8nont Esau wunnaumonuh, kah Esau au ohteakonit, ahchuwehteau weyaus, kah uppaudtauna.
E.27.5 And Rebekah heard when Isaac spake to Esau his son. And Esau went to the field to hunt for venison, and to bring it.

α.27.6 Kah Rebekah ken8nau Jakoboh wunnaumonuh, n8wau, kusseh, nunn8tau K8sh, ken8nau Esauoh keématoh, n8wau,
E.27.6 And Rebekah spake unto Jacob her son, saying, Behold, I heard thy father speak unto Esau thy brother, saying,

α.27.7 Paudtah weyaus, kah ayimah wunnummeechum, onk woh numméets, onk woh k8nanumash ut anaquabit Jehovah ash na nupp8omp.
E.27.7 Bring me venison, and make me savoury meat, that I may eat, and bless thee before the LORD before my death.

α.27.8 Newutche yeuyeu nunnaumon, nosweetash kuttinninn8wonk neyan unn8nun.
E.27.8 Now therefore, my son, obey my voice according to that which I command thee.

α.27.9 Aush yeuyeu en flocksut, nemskomah na$wutch neesuog goatsemesog wônogqutcheg, kah nag n8numéchumehkónuk wutch K8sh, neyane womóntog.
E.27.9 Go now to the flock, and fetch me from thence two good kids of the goats; and I will make them savoury meat for thy father, such as he loveth:

α.27.10 Kah woh kuppaudtauun K8sh, onk woh meetsu, onk woh k8nanumuk ash na nupp8kup.
E.27.10 And thou shalt bring it to thy father, that he may eat, and that he may bless thee before his death.

α.27.11 Onk Jakob unnau Rebekah noh okasoh, kusseh Esau nemat 8weshaganu, qut neen numm8ses.
E.27.11 And Jacob said to Rebekah his mother, Behold, Esau my brother is a hairy man, and I am a smooth man:

α.27.12 Paguodche n8sh woh nukquttinuk, kah ut wuskesukqut nen woh neyane as8kekodteámoénin, neit woh nuppaudtau nuhhog matánittuonk, qut matta wunánittuonk.
E.27.12 My father peradventure will feel me, and I shall seem to him as a deceiver; and I shall bring a curse upon me, and not a blessing.

α.27.13 Onk okasoh unnuk, matanittuonk ahtaúwutti nunnaumon, qut webe noswetash kúttinnunn8onk, kah monch nag nemskomah.
E.27.13 And his mother said unto him, Upon me be thy curse, my son: only obey my voice, and go fetch me them.

α.27.14 Onk [naau] kah wunâusuoh, kah uppaudtauónuh ohkasah, kah okasoh ayimwoh wekum mechum, neyane womontog 8shoh.
E.27.14 And he went, and fetched, and brought them to his mother: and his mother made savoury meat, such as his father loved.

α.27.15 Kah Rebekah nemunum 8néogk8onk mohtoméginitche wunnaumonuh Esauoh, ne ohtag weekit, kah wutogquonon Jakoboh nahohtôeu wunnaumonuh.
E.27.15 And Rebekah took goodly raiment of her eldest son Esau, which were with her in the house, and put them upon Jacob her younger son:

α.27.16 Onk upponamauoh goatsemese askonuh wunnutcheganit, kah umm8sittuppukanit.
E.27.16 And she put the skins of the kids of the goats upon his hands, and upon the smooth of his neck:

α.27.17 Onk wuttinnúmauh wekum mechum, kah petukqunnunk ne quoshauwehtog, ut wunnutcheganit wunnaumonuh Jakob.
E.27.17 And she gave the savoury meat and the bread, which she had prepared, into the hand of her son Jacob.

α.27.18 Kah peyaónau 8shoh, kah n8wau, n8sh, kah n8wau, nen yeu howan ken nunnaumon?
E.27.18 And he came unto his father, and said, My father: and he said, Here am I; who art thou, my son?

α.27.19 Kah Jakob unnau 8shoh, nen Esau mohtomegheadt, nummahche ussen neyan ann8sean, omohkish k8wehquetumoush, nummatapsh, kah meetch n8weyaus onk woh kukketeahogkou n8nanumuk.
E.27.19 And Jacob said unto his father, I am Esau thy first born; I have done according as thou badest me: arise, I pray thee, sit and eat of my venison, that thy soul may bless me.

α.27.20 Kah Isaak unnau wunnaumonuh, toh kittin teanuk namehteauun nunnaumon? kah n8wau, newutche Jehovah kummánitt8m nuppaudtunkqun anaquabeh.
E.27.20 And Isaac said unto his son, How is it that thou hast found it so quickly, my son? And he said, Because the LORD thy God brought it to me.

α.27.21 Onk Isaak unnau Jakoboh, pas8sukah yeuyeu nunnaumon onk woh kukqutunush uttohun wunnamuhkut ken nunnaumon Esau, asuh matta.
E.27.21 And Isaac said unto Jacob, Come near, I pray thee, that I may feel thee, my son, whether thou be my very son Esau or not.

α.27.22 Kah Jakob pas8sukauau Isaakoh 8shoh, kah ukquttinoh, kah n8wau, unnont8waonk wuttinnont8waonk Jakob, qut menutchegash wunnutchegash Esau.
E.27.22 And Jacob went near unto Isaac his father; and he felt him, and said, The voice is Jacob's voice, but the hands are the hands of Esau.

α.27.23 Kah matta 8wáheuh newutche wunnutchegash weshakinná8ash, neyane wunnutchegash Esau, neit 8nanumuh.
E.27.23 And he discerned him not, because his hands were hairy, as his brother Esau's hands: so he blessed him.

α.27.24 Kah n8wau, ken wunnamuhkut nunnaumon Esau? kah n8[m]au nen.
E.27.24 And he said, Art thou my very son Esau? And he said, I am.

α.27.25 Kah n8wau pas8che paudtah, kah nummeech 8weyausum nunnaumon, onk woh nukketeahogkou k8nanumuk: kah uppas8che paudtauón, kah metsu, kah uppaudtauoh wine, kah wuttattam.
E.27.25 And he said, Bring it near to me, and I will eat of my son's venison, that my soul may bless thee. And he brought it near to him, and he did eat: and he brought him wine and he drank.

α.27.26 Onk 8shoh Isaakoh wuttugquoh, pas8sukah yeuyeu, kah chipwutt8n[à]pweh nunnaumon.
E.27.26 And his father Isaac said unto him, Come near now, and kiss me, my son.

α.27.27 Kah uppas8sukauoh, kah wutchipwutt8nápoh, kah manontam ne asumungquok hogk8onk, kah 8nanumuh, kah n8wau, Kusseh, wuttissumunkqussuonk nunnaumon onatuh ne asumunkquok ohteuk, ne Jehovah wônantog.
E.27.27 And he came near, and kissed him: and he smelled the smell of his raiment, and blessed him, and said, See, the smell of my son is as the smell of a field which the LORD hath blessed:

α.27.28 Newutche God anninnumungqush néchipog wutch kesukquiug, kah 8nogk8onk ohke, kah m8natit weahchiminneash kah wine.
E.27.28 Therefore God give thee of the dew of heaven, and the fatness of the earth, and plenty of corn and wine:

α.27.29 Missinninnuog wuttinnúmish, kah wutohtimoneash nauaeihtunkqush, ken Sontimaish ut kematut, kah kokas wunnaumonuh nauae[i]htunkqush, matanumúnaj nish$noh pasuk noh matanumukquean, kah wunnanumunaj noh wananumukquean.
E.27.29 Let people serve thee, and nations bow down to thee: be lord over thy brethren, and let thy mother's sons bow down to thee: cursed be every one that curseth thee, and blessed be he that blesseth thee.

α.27.30 Onk n$nih Isaak mahche wunanumont Jakoboh, kah Jakob quenau monchit wutche anaquabenit Isaakoh 8shoh, Esau wematoh petutteau, wutche wutadchanat.
E.27.30 And it came to pass, as soon as Isaac had made an end of blessing Jacob, and Jacob was yet scarce gone out from the presence of Isaac his father, that Esau his brother came in from his hunting.

α.27.31 Kah noh wonk ayim wunnummechum, kah uppaudtauon 8shoh, kah unnau 8shoh, N8sh omohkij, kah mechitch 8weyaus wunnaumonuh, onk woh kukketeahogkou n8nanumuk;
E.27.31 And he also had made savoury meat, and brought it unto his father, and said unto his father, Let my father arise, and eat of his son's venison, that thy soul may bless me.

α.27.32 Kah Isaakoh 8shoh wuttugquoh, Howan ken? kah wuttinuh neen kenaumon mohtomegheadt Esau.
E.27.32 And Isaac his father said unto him, Who art thou? And he said, I am thy son, thy firstborn Esau.

α.27.33 Kah Isaak nunnukshau mishenukshaonk m8cheke, kah n8wau howan? uttiyeuoh mahche âdchant wutche weyaus, kah nuppaudtunkqun, kah nummahchipwun asquam papeyauop, & nummahche wunnanum, nux, kah noh pish wunnanumau.
E.27.33 And Isaac trembled very exceedingly, and said, Who? where is he that hath taken venison, and brought it me, and I have eaten of all before thou camest, and have blessed him? yea, and he shall be blessed.

α.27.34 Kah Esau n8tog ukkutt8wongash 8shoh, mau, muttaupp8su, kah wesogkohpausu, kah unnau 8shoh, Wunnanumeh, nen wonk, woi n8sh.
E.27.34 And when Esau heard the words of his father, he cried with a great and exceeding bitter cry, and said unto his father, Bless me, even me also, O my father.

α.27.35 Onk n8wau kemat wunnompuwussuwae peyau, kah amaunum k8nanumitteaongan.
E.27.35 And he said, Thy brother came with subtilty, and hath taken away thy blessing.

α.27.36 Kah n8wau, sun$nummatta wunnamuhkut ussuowesu Jakob, newutche nutas8kekomuk neesit nompe: amaúnum nummohtomegitteau8onk, kah kusseh, yeuyeu amaunum n8nanumitteaonk, kah n8wau, matta k8wadchanumiyeuh wunnanittuonk?
E.27.36 And he said, Is not he rightly named Jacob? for he hath supplanted me these two times: he took away my birthright; and, behold, now he hath taken away my blessing. And he said, Hast thou not reserved a blessing for me?

α.27.37 Kah Isaak wunnamp8hamauoh, kah unnau Esauoh, Kusseh, nutayimau k8sontimominneat, kah nuttinnumau wame weematuh 8tinninnúmunneat, kah numahche menéhke weachuminneash kah wine: onk toh woh kittinhennun ken nunnaumon.
E.27.37 And Isaac answered and said unto Esau, Behold, I have made him thy lord, and all his brethren have I given to him for servants; and with corn and wine have I sustained him: and what shall I do now unto thee, my son?

α.27.38 Kah Esau unnau 8shoh, Ken sun [n]ont kenequtahtoh wunanitteaonk n8sh; wunnanuméh, neen wonk woi n8sh, kah Esau mishont8wau kah mau.
E.27.38 And Esau said unto his father, Hast thou but one blessing, my father? bless me, even me also, O my father. And Esau lifted up his voice, and wept.

α.27.39 Kah 8shoh Isaakoh wunnamp8hamungquoh, kah wuttugquoh, Kusseh 8nogk8onk ohke, ne pish k8tohkin, & neechipog wutch ongkouwe kesukqut.
E.27.39 And Isaac his father answered and said unto him, Behold, thy dwelling shall be the fatness of the earth, and of the dew of heaven from above;

α.27.40 Kah pish kenashpe pomantam kuttogkomoneg, kah pish ken wuttinnúmoh kemat, & pish n$nih, ahtauan nanawunnumóonk pish kuppohquanum8wéyan wutch kussittippukanit.
E.27.40 And by thy sword shalt thou live, and shalt serve thy brother; and it shall come to pass when thou shalt have the dominion, that thou shalt break his yoke from off thy neck.

α.27.41 Kah Esau sekaneauau Jakoboh newutche wunnanittuonk unnadt woh wunnanumukupuh 8shoh, kah n8wau ut wúttahut, mauongane kesukodtash wutche n8sh teanuk peyau$m8ash, neit pish nunnush nemat Jakob.
E.27.41 And Esau hated Jacob because of the blessing wherewith his father blessed him: and Esau said in his heart, The days of mourning for my father are at hand; then will I slay my brother Jacob.

α.27.42 Yéush ukkutt8wongash Esau mohtomegheonche unnonash Rebekah, kah an8team8 kah wehkomon Jakob nahohtôeu wunnaumonuh, kah wuttinuh kusseh, kemat Esau taphéau wuhhogkuh papaume ken, noh kittinshikqunat.
E.27.42 And these words of Esau her elder son were told to Rebekah: and she sent and called Jacob her younger son, and said unto him, Behold, thy brother Esau, as touching thee, doth comfort himself, purposing to kill thee.

α.27.43 Newutche yeuyeu nunnaumon, nosweetash nuttinn8waonk kah neepaush, kenupsaush en Laban nemattut, ut Haran.
E.27.43 Now therefore, my son, obey my voice; arise, flee thou to Laban my brother to Haran;

α.27.44 Kah weetom ogkussequnne, yeán kemat kutáhquanumukqunat.
E.27.44 And tarry with him a few days, until thy brother's fury turn away;

α.27.45 Yeán kemat ummusquantamòonk qushkem8uk wutche ken, onk woh 8wa[n]antamun ne ánheadt, neit nutan8team, kah pish kenemskont na wutche, tohwutch woh wannéhenóg pasuk kesuk?
E.27.45 Until thy brother's anger turn away from thee, and he forget that which thou hast done to him: then I will send, and fetch thee from thence: why should I be deprived also of you both in one day?

α.27.46 Kah Rebekah wuttinuh Isaakuh, neen nussauunum nuppomantamóonk newutche wuttônuh Heth: Jakob ummittumwussit wuttaunoh Heth, yeug netatup nawajeh wuttaúnimukeg ne ohkeit, toh woh nuttinne wunnenehukqun nuppomantamóonk.
E.27.46 And Rebekah said to Isaac, I am weary of my life because of the daughters of Heth: if Jacob take a wife of the daughters of Heth, such as these which are of the daughters of the land, what good shall my life do me?

α.28.1 ONk Isaak wehkomau Jakoboh, kah 8nanumuh, kah ummechuméhkonuh, kah wuttinuh, Matta k8mittumwussissu wuttonin wutch Kanaan.
E.28.1 And Isaac called Jacob, and blessed him, and charged him, and said unto him, Thou shalt not take a wife of the daughters of Canaan.

α.28.2 Neepaush aush Padan-Aram weekit Bethuel 8shoh kokas, kah na ut ummittumwussish wutt[ô]noh Laban kokas wematoh.
E.28.2 Arise, go to Padanaram, to the house of Bethuel thy mother's father; and take thee a wife from thence of the daughers of Laban thy mother's brother.

α.28.3 Kah wamenuhkesu Manit wunnanumukqush, kah ayimungqush mônáonk, muttaanhukqush onk woh kummònam ut kummissinninnúuneat.
E.28.3 And God Almighty bless thee, and make thee fruitful, and multiply thee, that thou mayest be a multitude of people;

α.28.4 Kah aninnumunkqush wunnanumàonk Abrahamoh, ken kah k8skaneemuneog weeche ken, onk woh kutohtouun ohke neadt penuwohteaiyean, uttiyeu God anumauomp Abrahamoh.
E.28.4 And give thee the blessing of Abraham, to thee, and to thy seed with thee; that thou mayest inherit the land wherein thou art a stranger, which God gave unto Abraham.

α.28.5 Kah Isaak moncheàheau Jakoboh, kah au Padan-Aram en Laban wunnaumonuh Bethuel Wussyrian, Rebekah wunohtonukqussoh, Jakob kah Esau okasuoh.
E.28.5 And Isaac sent away Jacob: and he went to Padanaram unto Laban, son of Bethuel the Syrian, the brother of Rebekah, Jacob's and Esau's mother.

α.28.6 Esau nag* Isaak wunnanumau Jakóboh, kah ummoncheahheuh en Padan-Aram woh ummittumwussu na wutche, kah wunnanumont[,] kah ummechuméhkonuh n8wau, Matta pish k8mittumwussissu wuttôninneunk wutch Kanaan.
E.28.6 When Esau saw that Isaac had blessed Jacob, and sent him away to Padanaram, to take him a wife from thence; and that as he blessed him he gave him a charge, saying, Thou shalt not take a wife of the daughers of Canaan;

α.28.7 Kah Jakob n8swehtauau 8shoh kah okasoh kah mahche ont Padan-Aram.
E.28.7 And that Jacob obeyed his father and his mother, and was gone to Padanaram;

α.28.8 Onk Esau nag* wuttôneunk wutch Kanaan matchit ut wuskesukqut Isaak 8shoh.
E.28.8 And Esau seeing that the daughters of Canaan pleased not Isaac his father;

α.28.9 Neit Esau au Ishmaelut, kah wonk ummittumwussu, mahche nees8kauont, Mahalalhoh wuttônoh Ishmael, wunnaumonuh Abraham, wètatu Nebaioth, 8mittumwussissinneat.
E.28.9 Then went Esau unto Ishmael, and took unto the wives which he had Mahalath the daughter of Ishmael Abraham's son, the sister of Nebajoth, to be his wife.

α.28.10 Onk Jakob sohhám wutch Beersheba, kah au nogwu Haran.
E.28.10 And Jacob went out from Beersheba, and went toward Haran.

α.28.11 Onk ne peyon ayeuonganit, kah 8wampanóhkon newutche wayau, kah nemunum na ohtagish qussukquanash, kah wutohpukquasinúnash, & ne wussepsinin [á]yeuonganit.
E.28.11 And he lighted upon a certain place, and tarried there all night, because the sun was set; and he took of the stones of that place, and put them for his pillows, and lay down in that place to sleep.

α.28.12 Kah unnukquom, kah kusseh, tohk8tauonk neepatau ohkeit, kah ompachissin kesukqut, kah kusseh, wutangelsumoh God tohk8tauóog kah n8kontauóog.
E.28.12 And he dreamed, and behold a ladder set up on the earth, and the top of it reached to heaven: and behold the angels of God ascending and descending on it.

α.28.13 Kah kusseh Jehovah waabe neepau, kah n8wau, Nen Jehovah Ummanitt8moh Abraham k8sh, kah Ummanitt8moh Isaak, ne ohke ne sepsinan, ne kittinnumauunun kah k8skanemuneog.
E.28.13 And, behold, the LORD stood above it, and said, I am the LORD God of Abraham thy father, and the God of Isaac: the land whereon thou liest, to thee will I give it, and to thy seed;

α.28.14 Kah k8skanemuneog onatuh pish puppissiyeuash ohkeit, kah pish kutchachapénóog en wutcheksúaeyu, kah en wutchepwóeu, kah en nanúmaeu, kah sowanaeu, kah en kuhhogkat, kah en k8skanemuneog wame nish$noh wutteashiyéuunneau ohkeit pish wunnanumóog.
E.28.14 And thy seed shall be as the dust of the earth, and thou shalt spread abroad to the west, and to the east, and to the north, and to the south: and in thee and in thy seed shall all the families of the earth be blessed.

α.28.15 Kah kusseh k8wetomsh kah k8wadchansh nish$noh kutônush, onk yeu ut pish kukquihchuunush yeu ohkeit, newutche matta kenúkonún8, onk mahche ussean uttiyeu ánunnomp/
E.28.15 And, behold, I am with thee, and will keep thee in all places whither thou goest, and will bring thee again into this land; for I will not leave thee, until I have done that which I have spoken to thee of.

α.28.16 Kah Jakob t8kit wutch ukkouénat kah n8wau, wunamuhkut Jehovah yeu wutapin ayeuonganit, kah matta n8wahteauúnap. 
E.28.16 And Jacob awaked out of his sleep, and he said, Surely the LORD is in this place; and I knew it not.

α.28.17 Onk wabesu, kah n8wau, Uttiyeuun wabesuohkeyeu8? yeu matta onkatuk qut week God kah yeu kesukque squoant.
E.28.17 And he was afraid, and said, How dreadful is this place! this is none other but the house of God, and this is the gate of heaven.

α.28.18 Kah Jakob omohkeu nompoâeu, kah nemunum qussuk ne ápukquásukup, kah wunnepatauun wutche pogkomuhquonk, kah sokanum pumme wanashque.
E.28.18 And Jacob rose up early in the morning, and took the stone that he had put for his pillows, and set it up for a pillar, and poured oil upon the top of it.

α.28.19 Kah ne ayeuonk wuttehettamun Bethel, qut ne 8wesuonk otan negonne hettamuneau Luz.
E.28.19 And he called the name of that place Bethel: but the name of that city was called Luz at the first.

α.28.20 Kah Jakob quoshóau quoshaumaonk God, n8wau, God weetomukquean, kah wadchanukquean neyayeoi, kah aninnumungquean petukqununk ne woh meechu, kah hogk8onk agwee.
E.28.20 And Jacob vowed a vow, saying, If God will be with me, and will keep me in this way that I go, and will give me bread to eat, and raiment to put on,

α.28.21 Onk woh nukqushkem wonk n8sh weekit wunnohteàé, neit Jehovah pish N8manitt8mun.
E.28.21 So that I come again to my father's house in peace; then shall the LORD be my God:

α.28.22 Kah yeu qussuk neepatauomp wutch pogkomuhquonk, pish God 8weekin, kah wame ne pish ánumaiyean wunnamuhkut pish kittinumaush nish$noh piukque chepai.
E.28.22 And this stone, which I have set for a pillar, shall be God's house: and of all that thou shalt give me I will surely give the tenth unto thee.

α.29.1 Neit Jakob au wutaonganit, kah peyau ut ohkit wunneechaninneunk ut wutch[e]pwoaeu.
E.29.1 Then Jacob went on his journey, and came into the land of the people of the east.

α.29.2 Kah ummoninneauoh, kah kusseh wutahamonk ut ohteakonit, kah kusseh nishuog shepse chipanuog sepsinwog kishke, newutche ne wutch wutahamonganit 8tattamheonneau floksoh: kah mishikqussuk ohteau wussitt8nonog.
E.29.2 And he looked, and behold a well in the field, and, lo, there were three flocks of sheep lying by it; for out of that well they watered the flocks: and a great stone was upon the well's mouth.

α.29.3 Kah na peahettit wame floksog, kah wutomp8wutchanumunneau mishikqussuk wutc[h] wussitt8nónog, & wuttattamweheaog shepsoh, kah wonk upponamunneau qussuk wussit8nonog wutayeuonganit.
E.29.3 And thither were all the flocks gathered: and they rolled the stone from the well's mouth, and watered the sheep, and put the stone again upon the well's mouth in his place.

α.29.4 Kah Jakob wuttinuh nahog, neematog toh kuttaiinneau? kah n8waog Haran neenawun.
E.29.4 And Jacob said unto them, My brethren, whence be ye? And they said, Of Haran are we.

α.29.5 Kah wuttinuh nahog, K8waheaumw8 Laban wunnaumonuh Nahor? kah n8waog n8wahe[ò]un.
E.29.5 And he said unto them, Know ye Laban the son of Nahor? And they said, We know him.

α.29.6 Kah wuttinuh nahog, as kongketeau? kah n8waog as keteau, kah kusseh Rachel wuttaunoh pas8oh shepsoh.
E.29.6 And he said unto them, Is he well? And they said, He is well: and, behold, Rachel his daughter cometh with the sheep.

α.29.7 Kah n8wau, Kusseh ash qunni kesuk, kah asquam woh pas8wóog neetasuog moeu, wuttattamwáhuk shepsoh, kah monchek kah assam8k.
E.29.7 And he said, Lo, it is yet high day, neither is it time that the cattle should be gathered together: water ye the sheep, and go and feed them.

α.29.8 Kah n8waog, n8nanumumun, yean wame pas8wônaònt floksog moeu, kah yean wutomp8chanumunaónt qussuk wutch wussit8nónog, neit n8tattamheómun shepsoh.
E.29.8 And they said, We cannot, until all the flocks be gathered together, and till they roll the stone from the well's mouth; then we water the sheep.

α.29.9 Kah as konkekut8kauont nahog, Rachel peyau weeche 8shoh wuttushepsumoh, newutch wutassamuh.
E.29.9 And while he yet spake with them, Rachel came with her father's sheep; for she kept them.

α.29.10 Kah n$nih, Jakob nauont Racheloh wuttaunoh Laban, weematoh okasoh, kah wuttuṣshepsumoh Laban, okasoh wetateuh, & Jakob uppas8sukauoh, & wutomp8chânum qussuk wutch wussit8nónog, kah wuttattamwèheuh Laban uffloksumoh, okasoh wetatu.
E.29.10 And it came to pass, when Jacob saw Rachel the daughter of Laban his mother's brother, and the sheep of Laban his mother's brother, that Jacob went near, and rolled the stone from the well's mouth, and watered the flock of Laban his mother's brother.

α.29.11 Kah Jakob chipwutt8napwau Racheloh, kah mishont8wau kah mau.
E.29.11 And Jacob kissed Rachel, and lifted up his voice, and wept.

α.29.12 Kah Jakob wuttinuh Racheloh, Neen k8sh weematoh, kah Rebekah wunnaumonuh: kah quogqueu wuttinnon 8shoh.
E.29.12 And Jacob told Rachel that he was her father's brother, and that he was Rebekah's son: and she ran and told her father.

α.29.13 Kah n$nih Laban n8tog unaunchem8onaonk Jakob ummississoh wunnaumonuh, kah na ussishau wunnogskauoh, kah ukkoshkodtanuh, kah wutchipwutt8napo, kah uppetutteaheuh weekit, kah wuttinnonash Labanoh wame yeush kutt8wongash.
E.29.13 And it came to pass, when Laban heard the tidings of Jacob his sister's son, that he ran to meet him, and embraced him, and kissed him, and brought him to his house. And he told Laban all these things.

α.29.14 Kah Laban wuttinuh, Wunnamuhkut ken nuskon, kah n8weyaus, kah 8wetómuh ukkesukodtumash nepâuz.
E.29.14 And Laban said to him, Surely thou art my bone and my flesh. And he abode with him the space of a month.

α.29.15 Kah Laban wuttinuh Jak[a]boh, newutche ken neemat, sun woh n8tinninneum kuhhog wutch mon$teag? missohhamah toh an unkquatauun?
E.29.15 And Laban said unto Jacob, Because thou art my brother, shouldest thou therefore serve me for nought? tell me, what shall thy wages be?

α.29.16 Kah Laban nesitâunioh, 8wesuonk mohtomegit Leah, kah 8wesuonk nahohtôeu Rachel.
E.29.16 And Laban had two daughters: the name of the elder was Leah, and the name of the younger was Rachel.

α.29.17 Leah pannikquau, qut Rachel wunnetu, kah wunnompamukqussu.
E.29.17 Leah was tender eyed; but Rachel was beautiful and well favoured.

α.29.18 Kah Jakob womonau Racheloh, kah n8wau, nen kittinninneum nuhhog nes[a]usuk tahshit kodtumwae wutch Rachel peississit kuttannes.
E.29.18 And Jacob loved Rachel; and said, I will serve thee seven years for Rachel thy younger daughter.

α.29.19 Kah Laban n8wau, an wunnegik ken kuttinnúmauununonk, neit aninnumauog onkatuk wosketomp: weetómeh.
E.29.19 And Laban said, It is better that I give her to thee, than that I should give her to another man: abide with me.

α.29.20 Kah Jakob wuttinnúmuhkausu wuhhogkuh nes[à]usuk tahshe kodtumwae, wutch Racheloh: qut wunnauóuh oggúhsequinne newutche 8womonaonk.
E.29.20 And Jacob served seven years for Rachel; and they seemed unto him but a few days, for the love he had to her.

α.29.21 Neit Jakob unnau Labanoh, aninnumah nummittumwos, (newutche nukkesukodtumash numwohtaash) onk woh nuppetukau.
E.29.21 And Jacob said unto Laban, Give me my wife, for my days are fulfilled, that I may go in unto her.

α.29.22 Kah Laban mohmounau wame ne apitcheg, kah ayim mishadtup8onk.
E.29.22 And Laban gathered together all the men of the place, and made a feast.

α.29.23 Onk n$nih wanonk88k, kah nemunau Leahoh wuttaunoh, kah uppaudtauónuh, kah uppetukauuh.
E.29.23 And it came to pass in the evening, that he took Leah his daughter, and brought her to him; and he went in unto her.

α.29.24 Kah Laban aninnumauau wuttaunoh Leahoh, Zilpha wuttinúmun, onk woh ummaidumuh.
E.29.24 And Laban gave unto his daughter Leah Zilpah his maid for an handmaid.

α.29.25 Onk n$nih nompoaeu, kah kusseh, noh Leah, kah wuttinuh Labanah chaugua yeu anhéan? sunnummatta k8tinnineumeúmus nuhhog wutch Rachel? kah toh wútch kutas8kekomeh?
E.29.25 And it came to pass, that in the morning, behold, it was Leah: and he said to Laban, What is this thou hast done unto me? did not I serve with thee for Rachel? wherefore then hast thou beguiled me?

α.29.26 Kah Laban n8wau, Woh mô nano ut nutohkin, negoñe magun peississit nukasquam mohtomégit.
E.29.26 And Laban said, It must not be so done in our country, to give the younger before the firstborn.

α.29.27 Numwohtaush 8weekum wonk, kah yeuoh wonk kittiñumauunan newutche kutanakausuonk, anúhkonéhtaieum wonk nesausuk kodtumwae.
E.29.27 Fulfil her week, and we will give thee this also for the service which thou shalt serve with me yet seven other years.

α.29.28 Kah Jakob wuttussen, kah wunnumwohtauun 8weekum: kah wuttinnumauunoh Racheloh 8mittumwussisineat.
E.29.28 And Jacob did so, and fulfilled her week: and he gave him Rachel his daughter to wife also.

α.29.29 Kah Laban aninnumauau Racheloh wuttaunoh Bilhah wuttinnúmun mittumwussissoh wuttinnúmoh.
E.29.29 And Laban gave to Rachel his daughter Bilhah his handmaid to be her maid.

α.29.30 Kah petukauau wonk Racheloh, kah womonoh R[a]cheloh m8cheke onk Leahhoh, kah wonk wuttinnúmehkausu wuh[g]ogkuh nesausuk tahshe onkatogish kodtum8ash.
E.29.30 And he went in also unto Rachel, and he loved also Rachel more than Leah, and served with him yet seven other years.

α.29.31 Onk Jehovah nag* Leah sekeneaóonk wôhshinnúmaau wut$utkutôontómukkomut, qut Rachel mehchéeu.
E.29.31 And when the LORD saw that Leah was hated, he opened her womb: but Rachel was barren.

α.29.32 Kah Leah wompoquau, kah wunnaumonaeu, kah wuttissowenuh Ruben: newutche n8wau, wunnamuhkut Jehovah mónunneam n8támepunáonk, newutche yeuyeu nasuk n8womónuk.
E.29.32 And Leah conceived, and bare a son, and she called his name Reuben: for she said, Surely the LORD hath looked upon my affliction; now therefore my husband will love me.

α.29.33 Kah wonk wompoquau, kah wunnaumónaeu, kah n8wau, newutche Jehovah wunn8tamun nussekeneànteaonk, newutche yeuh wonk nuttinnumunkqunuh, kah wuttissowenuh Simeon.
E.29.33 And she conceived again, and bare a son; and said, Because the LORD hath heard I was hated, he hath therefore given me this son also: and she called his name Simeon.

α.29.34 Kah wonk wompoquau, kah wunnaumonaeu, kah n8wau yeu aquompak nasuk umm8sogquéhtunk, newutche nish wompaékitteau: newaj hennit Levi.
E.29.34 And she conceived again, and bare a son; and said, Now this time will my husband be joined unto me, because I have born him three sons: therefore was his name called Levi.

α.29.35 Kah wonk womoquau kah wunnaumonaeu, kah n8wau, yeuyeu nuttabuttantamau Jehovah, newutche ussowénont Judah kah ahquegheau.
E.29.35 And she conceived again, and bare a son: and she said, Now will I praise the LORD: therefore she called his name Judah; and left bearing.

α.30.1 KAH Rachel nag* matta wutchekitteauau Jakob, Rachel wutishkauónuh ummissesoh, kah unnau Jakoboh, aninnumah mukkiésog, qut matta, onk nunnup.
E.30.1 And when Rachel saw that she bare Jacob no children, Rachel envied her sister; and said unto Jacob, Give me children, or else I die.

α.30.2 Kah [j]akob ummusquanumáuonk n8hn8unau Racheloh, kah n8wau sun nen nompin God, noh kospaudtamungqean ummeechummúonk wutoontòmut.
E.30.2 And Jacob's anger was kindled against Rachel: and he said, Am I in God's stead, who hath withheld from thee the fruit of the womb?

α.30.3 Kah n8waú, kusseh nuttinnúm mittumwussis Bilhah, noh petukau, kah pish neechau ut nukkutukqut, onk woh n8neecham noh wutche.
E.30.3 And she said, Behold my maid Bilhah, go in unto her; and she shall bear upon my knees, that I may also have children by her.

α.30.4 Kah wuttinnumáoh Bilhahoh ummaidumoh 8mittumwussissinneat, kah Jakob uppetukauau.
E.30.4 And she gave him Bilhah her handmaid to wife: and Jacob went in unto her.

α.30.5 Kah Bilhah wompequau, kah neechanushao Jakoboh.
E.30.5 And Bilhah conceived, and bare Jacob a son.

α.30.6 Kah Rachel n8wop, God n8sumukup, & wonk n8tam n8wadtauatonkqussuonk, kah nuttinnumunk wunnaumonain, newaj hennont Dan.
E.30.6 And Rachel said, God hath judged me, and hath also heard my voice, and hath given me a son: therefore called she his name Dan.

α.30.7 Kah Bilhah wuttinúmoh Rachel wonk wompequau, kah nahohtôeu wutchekitteauau Jakoboh.
E.30.7 And Bilhah Rachel's maid conceived again, and bare Jacob a second son.

α.30.8 Kah Rachel n8wau, mishe quogquadtinnittúonk nukquogquadtinohkon nummissis: kah nussongqueh, kah wuttissowenuh Naphtali.
E.30.8 And Rachel said, With great wrestlings have I wrestled with my sister, and I have prevailed: and she called his name Naphtali.

α.30.9 Leah nag* wutahquegheaonk, neemunau Zilpha ummaidumoh, kah wuttinnumauónuh Jakoboh 8mitumwussissinneat.
E.30.9 When Leah saw that she had left bearing, she took Zilpah her maid, and gave her Jacob to wife.

α.30.10 Kah Zilpha ummaidumoh Leah neekitteauau wunnaumonuh Jakoboh.
E.30.10 And Zilpah Leah's maid bare Jacob a son.

α.30.11 Kah Leah n8wau, m8naouk peyaum8 kah wuttissowenuh Gad.
E.30.11 And Leah said, A troop cometh: and she called his name Gad.

α.30.12 Kah Zilphah Leah ummaidumoh nohohtôeu nekitteauau Jakoboh wuñaumonuh
E.30.12 And Zilpah Leah's maid bare Jacob a second son.

α.30.13 Kah Leah n8wau, n8ni, newutche wuttônéunk pish nuttinnúkquog k8nanumit kah wuttissowenuh Ashur.
E.30.13 And Leah said, Happy am I, for the daughters will call me blessed: and she called his name Asher.

α.30.14 Kah Ruben pomushau kesukodáeu eninnowaut wheatash, kah namehteau Mandrakes ut ohteakonit, kah uppaudtauun okasoh Leahoh: neit Rachel unnau Leahoh, aninnumah k8wequetumoush kenaumon ummandraksumash.
E.30.14 And Reuben went in the days of wheat harvest, and found mandrakes in the field, and brought them unto his mother Leah. Then Rachel said to Leah, Give me, I pray thee, of thy son's mandrakes.

α.30.15 Kah wuttinuh, sun peamesan keneemunúmayeuonk nahsuk, kah wonk kukkod amaunum ummandraksum nunnaumon? kah Rachel n8wau, newutche woh keneesinau yeu nohkog newutche kenaumon ummandraksum.
E.30.15 And she said unto her, Is it a small matter that thou hast taken my husband? and wouldest thou take away my son's mandrakes also? And Rachel said, Therefore he shall lie with thee to night for thy son's mandrakes.

α.30.16 Kah Jakob 8m ohteakonit wunnonkquàe, kah Leah sohham wunnogskauoh, kah n8wau, nawhónk kuppetukah nen, newutche wunnamuhkut nummahche kutann8nsh ken wutche nunnaumon ummandraksumoh, kah weetukquom8tuog ne nohkog.
E.30.16 And Jacob came out of the field in the evening, and Leah went out to meet him, and said, Thou must come in unto me; for surely I have hired thee with my son's mandrakes. And he lay with her that night.

α.30.17 Kah God wunn8tauuh Leahhoh, kah wompoquau, kah wutcheketeauau Jakoboh napanna wutteáshompaneaont.
E.30.17 And God hearkened unto Leah, and she conceived, and bare Jacob the fifth son.

α.30.18 Kah Leah n8wau, God nuttinnumunk nunnoguhkouonk, newutche nutinnumau nummaidumoh nahsuk: kah wuttissowenuh Issachar.
E.30.18 And Leah said, God hath given me my hire, because I have given my maiden to my husband: and she called his name Issachar.

α.30.19 Kah wonk Leah womoquau, kah nekitteauau Jakoboh nequtta tahshu wunnaumōnuh.
E.30.19 And Leah conceived again, and bare Jacob the sixth son.

α.30.20 Onk Leah n8wau, God nummahche ani[ñ]umunk n8[ne]ohtóonk, yeuyeu nasuk n8weetomuk, newutche nequtta nutteeashompaégitteau, kah wuttussowenuh Zebulun.
E.30.20 And Leah said, God hath endued me with a good dowry; now will my husband dwell with me, because I have born him six sons: and she called his name Zebulun.

α.30.21 Kah ompetak wuttòneu, kah wuttissowenuh Dinah.
E.30.21 And afterwards she bare a daughter, and called her name Dinah.

α.30.22 Kah God mehquanumau Racheloh, kah God wunn8tauoh, kah woshwúnumauoh wututkut[ô]ontómukkomut.
E.30.22 And God remembered Rachel, and God hearkened to her, and opened her womb.

α.30.23 Kah wompoquau, kah wunnaumonaeu kah n8wau, God amau[n]m nuttiaspinumiteaonk.
E.30.23 And she conceived, and bare a son; and said, God hath taken away my reproach:

α.30.24 Kah wuttehenuh Joseph, kah n8wau, Jehovah pish nuttinnumunk onkatoge nunnaumonuh.
E.30.24 And she called his name Joseph; and said, The LORD shall add to me another son.

α.30.25 Onk n$nih, Rachel neechad Josephuh, Jakob unnau Labanoh, Monche[à]heh, onk woh nuttóm nutayeuonganit, kah nutohket
E.30.25 And it came to pass, when Rachel had born Joseph, that Jacob said unto Laban, Send me away, that I may go unto mine own place, and to my country.

α.30.26 Aninnumah nummittumwussog, kah neechanog newutche nag k8tenúmukaúunup nuhhogk, kah moncheti: newutche k8wahteoh k8tinninnúmuhkauunop nuhhog.
E.30.26 Give me my wives and my children, for whom I have served thee, and let me go: for thou knowest my service which I have done thee.

α.30.27 Kah Laban wuttinuh, k8wihquetumoush namehteauon kitteamonteanittuonk ut kuskesukqut, yeu apsh, nunnetúhtouun wutch qutchehteaonganit Jehovah, n8nanumuk newutche ken.
E.30.27 And Laban said unto him, I pray thee, if I have found favour in thine eyes, tarry: for I have learned by experience that the LORD hath blessed me for thy sake.

α.30.28 Kah n8wau, missohhamah kutonkquatunk noh wonk kittinnumaúunun.
E.30.28 And he said, Appoint me thy wages, and I will give it.

α.30.29 Kah wuttinuh, k8wahteoun ne án wuttinneumuhkauun nuhhog, & toh nuttin nánauweheonup kenetasumog.
E.30.29 And he said unto him, Thou knowest how I have served thee, and how thy cattle was with me.

α.30.30 Newutche kutohguhsétit weske peyam, onk muttaonoóg: kah Jehovah k8nanumuk nadteoh paôon, kah yeuyeu ahquompak woh wonk nukquoshaeihtam nehenwonche neek?
E.30.30 For it was little which thou hadst before I came, and it is now increased unto a multitude; and the LORD hath blessed thee since my coming: and now when shall I provide for mine own house also?

α.30.31 Kah n8wau, chauguash kittinnumaúush, kah Jakob n8wau matta teag kittinnumaiyeush: yeu nehhean, wonk pish nukqushkem, nutassam, kah nanauéhheoóg kuffloksumog.
E.30.31 And he said, What shall I give thee? And Jacob said, Thou shalt not give me any thing: if thou wilt do this thing for me, I will again feed and keep thy flock.

α.30.32 Nuppannumwusham wame kuffloksumog yeu kesukok, nutamaun wame momonesitcheg, mômóechohkesitcheg netasuog, kah wame moompamukqussitcheg neetasuog kenugke shepsoh, kah chohkesitcheg, & momonesitcheg, ut kenugke goatsog, & yeu pish nutonkquatunk.
E.30.32 I will pass through all thy flock to day, removing from thence all the speckled and spotted cattle, and all the brown cattle among the sheep, and the spotted and speckled among the goats: and of such shall be my hire.

α.30.33 Neit pish nussampweusseonk wauw[o]m8 wutch nen saup, toh utt8che peyaum8uk wutch nutonkquatunk anaquabean: nish$noh mat mónónesein, kah mat mômochohkesein? kenugke goatsut, kah matta moampánukqussein kenugke shepsog, ne pish tatupantamauonuh kôm8tukus.
E.30.33 So shall my righteousness answer for me in time to come, when it shall come for my hire before thy face: every one that is not speckled and spotted among the goats, and brown among the sheep, that shall be counted stolen with me.

α.30.34 Kah Laban n8wau kusseh, nukkodtantam niyôuut ne an8wáan.
E.30.34 And Laban said, Behold, I would it might be according to thy word.

α.30.35 Onk amaunau ne kesukok nompashimau goatsoh momonesit, kah wame squaushimwe goatsoh momonésinutcheh, & cho[h]kesinitche nish$noh pasuk n8wompechohkesit, kah wame mom8esitcheh kenugke shepsoh, kah wuttinuumaunuh nahog en wunnutcheganit wunnaumonuh. 
E.30.35 And he removed that day the he goats that were ringstraked and spotted, and all the she goats that were speckled and spotted, and every one that had some white in it, and all the brown among the sheep, and gave them into the hand of his sons.

α.30.36 Onk nishikquinushon na ponamun nôeu nehenwonche kah Jakob, kah Jakob assamau wunneetasumoh onkatogane Laban.
E.30.36 And he set three days' journey betwixt himself and Jacob: and Jacob fed the rest of Laban's flocks.

α.30.37 Kah Jakob neemunumau mehtugk8mesash ashkuhquame metwe, kah paudteateamenash, kah wompemusseshash, & 8wowómpehinuh, kah momoneteauunash mehtugk8mesash.
E.30.37 And Jacob took him rods of green poplar, and of the hazel and chestnut tree; and pilled white strakes in them, and made the white appear which was in the rods.

α.30.38 Kah ne ponamun mehtugk8mesash nish wowompekinukish anaquabhettit floksog ut pasohtheganit, kah ahhut wuttattamohettit, floksog paahettit wuttattamohettit, onk woh wompequau8og notsipamóhettit.
E.30.38 And he set the rods which he had pilled before the flocks in the gutters in the watering troughs when the flocks came to drink, that they should conceive when they came to drink.

α.30.39 Kah floksog wompequauog ut anaquohtag mehtugk8mesash, kah nechaog neetasuog mômônesitcheg, chohchohkesitcheg & wéénu momonesitcheg.
E.30.39 And the flocks conceived before the rods, and brought forth cattle ringstraked, speckled, and spotted.

α.30.40 Kah Jakob chipin[a]u lambsog, kah weongqua8kaoh wuskesukquash floksog nogqueu en kohtipusquanepisinutche, kah wame moampamukqúsinutche en ufflocksumut Laban, kah chippeponam nehenwonche uffloksumoh, kah matta upponuh Laban wunnetasumut.
E.30.40 And Jacob did separate the lambs, and set the faces of the flocks toward the ringstraked, and all the brown in the flock of Laban; and he put his own flocks by themselves, and put them not unto Laban's cattle.

α.30.41 Onk n$[u]ih matikenukeg netasuog wompequahettit, Jakob ponam mehtugk8mesash ut anaquabhettit wuskesukk8ont, ut pasohtheganit, onk woh wompequau8og kenugke mehtugk8mesekontu.
E.30.41 And it came to pass, whensoever the stronger cattle did conceive, that Jacob laid the rods before the eyes of the cattle in the gutters, that they might conceive among the rods.

α.30.42 Qut neetasuog n8chemweṣhettit, matta ne ponamauau, nemuhkuh nan8chumwesuoh Laban, qut menuhkesuoh Jâkob.
E.30.42 But when the cattle were feeble, he put them not in: so the feebler were Laban's, and the stronger Jacob's.

α.30.43 Onk wosketomp nano mon[à]oh m8cheke, kah m8chekohshau nétasu, kah mittumwussisse wuttinneúmoh, kah wosketompae wuttinnumoh, kah kamelsog kah assesog.
E.30.43 And the man increased exceedingly, and had much cattle, and maidservants, and menservants, and camels, and asses.

α.31.1 ONK n8tam ukkutt8wongash wunnaumonuh Laban, n8waog, Jakob amaunum wame ohtaukupash k8shinonut: & ne 8tahtauun ohtágkup k8shinonut, wame ne sohsum8onk wutohqunúmun.
E.31.1 And he heard the words of Laban's sons, saying, Jacob hath taken away all that was our father's; and of that which was our father's hath he gotten all this glory.

α.31.2 Kah Jakob kuhkinneam wuttinnússúonk Laban, kah kusseh, matta uppóe[ú] moneauoh neyane negonae.
E.31.2 And Jacob beheld the countenance of Laban, and, behold, it was not toward him as before.

α.31.3 Kah Jehovah unnau Jakoboh, qushkish en wutohket k8shog, kah kuttinnowamôuhtu kah k8wetomsh.
E.31.3 And the LORD said unto Jacob, Return unto the land of thy fathers, and to thy kindred; and I will be with thee.

α.31.4 Kah Jakob an8team8, & weekomoh Rachel kah Leah en ohteakonit, en wutchippashum8mehtu.
E.31.4 And Jacob sent and called Rachel and Leah to the field unto his flock,

α.31.5 Kah wuttinuh nahog, nunaum k8sheu wuttinnussuonk, matta nupp[ô]e monunneungk8, neyane negonaeu, qut ummanitt8moh n8sh n8wetomukup.
E.31.5 And said unto them, I see your father's countenance, that it is not toward me as before; but the God of my father hath been with me.

α.31.6 Kah k8wahteauunneau, n8tinninnúmuhkau k8sheu nuhhogkuh weeche wame nummenuhkesuonk.
E.31.6 And ye know that with all my power I have served your father.

α.31.7 Kah k8sheu nutass8kekomuk & ôs8wunum nutonkquatunkash piogqut nompe, qut God matta wuttinnánumoh n8woskhukqunat.
E.31.7 And your father hath deceived me, and changed my wages ten times; but God suffered him not to hurt me.

α.31.8 Yeu n8wadt mom8echohkésitcheg, ne pish kutonkquatunk, neit wame neetasuog neecháog mohm8echohkésunitche: asuh yeu n8wadt wééne momoeesit, ne pish kutunkquatunk, neit wame neetasuog neechaog weenompasik, wutchohkein8.
E.31.8 If he said thus, The speckled shall be thy wages; then all the cattle bare speckled: and if he said thus, The ringstraked shall be thy hire; then bare all the cattle ringstraked.

α.31.9 Yeu in God amaunau wunnetasumoh k8sheu, kah nuttinumunkqunash.
E.31.9 Thus God hath taken away the cattle of your father, and given them to me.

α.31.10 Onk n$nih, ne áhutt8che wompoquahettit neetasuog, nuttishpadtauomp, kah nunnaum ut kouenat, kah kusseh nomposhimwogineg ayimáuukeg, neg wutchohkéin8 weenompasu, kah mohm8e chohkesuog, kah momonesuog.
E.31.10 And it came to pass at the time that the cattle conceived, that I lifted up mine eyes, and saw in a dream, and, behold, the rams which leaped upon the cattle were ringstraked, speckled, and grisled.

α.31.11 Káh wutangelsumoh God nuken8nukup ut koenat, kah nussim nen yeu.
E.31.11 And the angel of God spake unto me in a dream, saying, Jacob: And I said, Here am I.

α.31.12 Onk n8wau yeuyeu spuhquáish, kah n[a]ish, wame nomposhimwog neg ayimauukeg, wutchohkéinnu weenompasik, mohm8e chohkésuog kah momonesuog, newutche nunnaumun wame Laban anhukquean.
E.31.12 And he said, Lift up now thine eyes, and see, all the rams which leap upon the cattle are ringstraked, speckled, and grisled: for I have seen all that Laban doeth unto thee.

α.31.13 Nen Manitto ut Bethel uttôhadt samúnumop pogkomuhquonk, kah uttoh adt quoshauáop quoshaumáonk God: yeuyeu nepaush, sohhash yeu wutch ohket, kah qushkish en wutohtuóut kuttinonkumóog.
E.31.13 I am the God of Bethel, where thou anointedst the pillar, and where thou vowedst a vow unto me: now arise, get thee out from this land, and return unto the land of thy kindred.

α.31.14 Kah Rachel kah Leah wunnamp8hamauoh, kah wuttinóuh, as na ohteau nutchippunumónteaonganun, asuh ahteóonk wutche nenawun n8shun wekit?
E.31.14 And Rachel and Leah answered and said unto him, Is there yet any portion or inheritance for us in our father's house?

α.31.15 Sunnum$matta nutogquanumuk8un penuwohteáut? newutche mag8 nuhhogkanonash, kah máhtshadtau wame nutteagwunnónut.
E.31.15 Are we not counted of him strangers? for he hath sold us, and hath quite devoured also our money.

α.31.16 Newutche wame wenauwetuongash God amaunukish wutch n8shunnónut nen nutaihéin kah neech[au]sinnonog, yeuyeu neit uttoh anukquéan God, ne ussish.
E.31.16 For all the riches which God hath taken from our father, that is ours, and our children's: now then, whatsoever God hath said unto thee, do.

α.31.17 Neit Jakob neepau, kah ponau wunnaumonuh, kah ummittumwussoh, kamelsut.
E.31.17 Then Jacob rose up, and set his sons and his wives upon camels;

α.31.18 Kah monchanau wame wunnetasumoh, kah wame maumachiash nish nóhtwunukish, kah netasu wamuhwhonche ut Padan$Aram, onk woh au Isaakanit 8shut ohkit Kanaan.
E.31.18 And he carried away all his cattle, and all his goods which he had gotten, the cattle of his getting, which he had gotten in Padanaram, for to go to Isaac his father in the land of Canaan.

α.31.19 Kah Laban monchu m8swau shepsoh, kah Rachel komm8to wuttinneukontunkoh 8shoh.
E.31.19 And Laban went to shear his sheep: and Rachel had stolen the images that were her father's.

α.31.20 Kah Jakob monchu matta wahteauug Laban Wussyrian, matta unnunk nummonchem.
E.31.20 And Jacob stole away unawares to Laban the Syrian, in that he told him not that he fled.
